import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein
import numpy as np

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1001
CHECK_NAME  = "DOP matched with Customer Invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1001"

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA  (raw dataframes kept UNCHANGED)
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df_raw = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows (RAW): {len(unst_df_raw)}")   # should print 6802

# =========================================================
# CATEGORY LOOKUP  (attch_id -> category from base_df)
# built BEFORE dedup so every attachment's category is captured
# =========================================================
CATEGORY_LOOKUP = {}
for _, _r in base_df.iterrows():
    _aid = _r.get("attch_id")
    _cat = _r.get("category")
    if _aid is None:
        continue
    _aid = str(_aid).strip()
    if _aid == "" or _aid in CATEGORY_LOOKUP:
        continue
    CATEGORY_LOOKUP[_aid] = ("" if _cat is None else str(_cat).strip())

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS  (work on a COPY, raw stays intact)
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df_raw.copy()
unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

def parse_date_any(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return None
    s = str(v).strip()
    fmts = [
        "%Y-%m-%d", "%Y/%m/%d", "%d-%m-%Y", "%d/%m/%Y",
        "%d.%m.%Y", "%m-%d-%Y", "%m/%d/%Y",
        "%d-%b-%Y", "%d %b %Y", "%d-%B-%Y", "%d %B %Y",
        "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
    ]
    for f in fmts:
        try:
            return datetime.strptime(s[:len(f) + 4], f).date()
        except:
            continue
    try:
        d = pd.to_datetime(s, dayfirst=True, errors="coerce")
        return d.date() if pd.notna(d) else None
    except:
        return None

# =========================================================
# POSITIONALLY-ALIGNED AGGREGATION
# (no dropna, no unique -> every column keeps 1 element per row
#  so attch_id stays perfectly aligned with date_of_purchase)
# =========================================================
def join_aligned(series):
    out = []
    for v in series.tolist():
        if v is None:
            out.append("Not available")
            continue
        try:
            if pd.isna(v):
                out.append("Not available")
                continue
        except Exception:
            pass
        s = str(v).strip()
        out.append(s if s != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(out)

unst_agg = unst_df.groupby(JOIN_KEYS, as_index=False).agg(join_aligned)

print(f"unst aggregated rows (per header_crm_id+sr_id): {len(unst_agg)}")

# =========================================================
# DEDUP BASE TO ONE ROW PER SR (avoids duplicate output rows)
# =========================================================
base_one_per_sr = base_df.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS, keep="first").copy()
print(f"base_df deduped to one row per SR: {len(base_one_per_sr)}")

# =========================================================
# MERGE  (one base row per SR x one unst row per SR)
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_one_per_sr,
    unst_agg.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE CHECK  (OR LOGIC, aligned attch_id)
# =========================================================
def check_date_attachmentwise(expected_date, observed_dates, attch_ids):
    """
    Match if ANY observed value matches the expected date.

    Rules:
      - ANY element matches expected            -> MATCH (flag 0), report matching attch_id(s)
      - All observed values missing/not-avail   -> MATCH (flag 0)
      - Valid value(s) present but none match    -> MISMATCH (flag 1)

    Returns: flag, matched_attchs, mismatch_attchs
    """
    expected = parse_date_any(expected_date)

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_dates).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched_attchs   = []
    mismatch_attchs  = []
    valid_value_seen = False

    for idx, obs_date in enumerate(obs_list):

        if idx < len(attch_list):
            attch = attch_list[idx]
        elif attch_list:
            attch = attch_list[-1]
        else:
            attch = ""

        if is_missing(obs_date):
            continue

        valid_value_seen = True
        obs = parse_date_any(obs_date)

        if expected is not None and obs is not None and obs == expected:
            matched_attchs.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatch_attchs.append(attch)

    matched_attchs  = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched_attchs if a]))
    mismatch_attchs = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatch_attchs if a]))

    if not valid_value_seen:
        return 0, "", ""
    if matched_attchs:
        return 0, ",".join(matched_attchs), ""
    return 1, "", ",".join(mismatch_attchs)

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK  (use ALIGNED unst attch_id)
# =========================================================
temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_date_attachmentwise(
        r.get("purchase_date"),
        r.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")          # aligned attach ids from unst table
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"] = temp.apply(lambda x: x[0]).astype(int)
merged_df["matched_attch_ids"]      = temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["mismatch_attch_ids"]     = temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

# Output attch_id = aligned unst attach ids (fallback to base attch_id if unst missing)
def resolve_attch(r):
    u = r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("attch_id")

merged_df["attch_id_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_attch, axis=1)

# =========================================================
# CATEGORY (~ separated) built by mapping each attch_id -> category
# =========================================================
def build_category(attch_str):
    if attch_str is None or (isinstance(attch_str, float) and pd.isna(attch_str)):
        return None
    ids = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_str).split("~")]
    cats = []
    for aid in ids:
        cat = CATEGORY_LOOKUP.get(aid, "")
        cats.append(cat if cat != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(cats)

merged_df["category_out"] = merged_df["attch_id_out"].apply(build_category)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def remark_text(flag):
    if flag == 0:
        return "purchase date is matching with system date"
    else:
        return "purchase date is not matching with system date"

def additional_remarks_text(row):
    if row["date_of_purchase_check"] == 0:
        if row["matched_attch_ids"]:
            return f"Purchase date matched with attachment(s): {row['matched_attch_ids']}"
        else:
            return "Purchase date was not extracted in any attachment"
    else:
        return f"Purchase date mismatch in attachment(s): {row['mismatch_attch_ids']}"

# ----- NEW: reformat each ~-separated observed date to MM/DD/YYYY -----
def format_observed_mmddyyyy(observed_str):
    if observed_str is None:
        return observed_str
    try:
        if pd.isna(observed_str):
            return observed_str
    except Exception:
        pass
    parts = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    out = []
    for p in parts:
        d = parse_date_any(p)
        if d is not None:
            out.append(d.strftime("%m/%d/%Y"))   # MM/DD/YYYY
        else:
            out.append(p)                          # keep original (e.g. 'Not available')
    return "~".join(out)

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":            CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":          CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":          now_ts,
    "updated_at":          now_ts,
    "is_active":           merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":       merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":           merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":            merged_df["attch_id_out"],
    "category":            merged_df["category_out"],          # <-- ~ separated
    "dop_observed_value":  merged_df.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
    "dop_expected_value":  merged_df.get("purchase_date"),
    "exception_flag":      merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(
        lambda x: "yes" if x == 1 else "no"
    ),
    "reason":              merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(remark_text),
})

output_df["additional_remarks"] = merged_df.apply(additional_remarks_text, axis=1)

output_df["reason"] = np.where(
    (output_df["additional_remarks"].isin(["Purchase date was not extracted in any attachment"])),
    "Purchase date was not extracted in any attachment",
    output_df["reason"]
)

# ----- Reformat BOTH observed and expected to MM/DD/YYYY (output only, logic untouched) -----
output_df["dop_observed_value"] = output_df["dop_observed_value"].apply(format_observed_mmddyyyy)
output_df["dop_expected_value"] = output_df["dop_expected_value"].apply(format_observed_mmddyyyy)

# =========================================================
# JOINT DEDUP: attch_id + category stay 1:1 aligned
# =========================================================
def dedup_attch_and_category(attch_val, cat_val):
    if pd.isna(attch_val) or attch_val is None:
        return attch_val, cat_val

    attch_list = str(attch_val).split("~")
    cat_list   = str(cat_val).split("~") if (cat_val is not None and not pd.isna(cat_val)) else []

    seen = set()
    out_attch, out_cat = [], []

    for idx, a in enumerate(attch_list):
        if a in seen:
            continue                      # duplicate attachment -> skip it AND its category
        seen.add(a)
        out_attch.append(a)
        if idx < len(cat_list):
            out_cat.append(cat_list[idx])

    return "~".join(out_attch), "~".join(out_cat)

_deduped = output_df.apply(
    lambda r: dedup_attch_and_category(r["attch_id"], r["category"]),
    axis=1
)
output_df["attch_id"] = _deduped.apply(lambda x: x[0])
output_df["category"] = _deduped.apply(lambda x: x[1])

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")

# =========================================================
# SUMMARY COUNT
# =========================================================
total_rows   = len(output_df)
match_count  = (output_df["exception_flag"] == "no").sum()
mismatch_cnt = (output_df["exception_flag"] == "yes").sum()

print("----------------------------------------")
print("SUMMARY")
print(f"Total rows       : {total_rows}")
print(f"Matches (no)     : {match_count}")
print(f"Mismatches (yes) : {mismatch_cnt}")
print("----------------------------------------")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   updated_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id TEXT,
#   category TEXT,
#   dop_observed_value TEXT,
#   dop_expected_value TEXT,
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   reason TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id(255))
# )
# """
# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id", "check_name", "created_at", "updated_at", "is_active",
    "header_crm_id", "sr_number", "attch_id", "category",
    "dop_observed_value", "dop_expected_value",
    "exception_flag", "reason", "additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list     = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols
               if c not in ["check_id", "header_crm_id", "sr_number", "attch_id", "created_at"]]
update_sql  = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i + BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i + len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1001")

import re

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1001
CHECK_NAME  = "DOP matched with Customer Invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1001"

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA  (raw dataframes kept UNCHANGED)

base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df_raw = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows (RAW): {len(unst_df_raw)}")   # should print 6802

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS  (work on a COPY, raw stays intact)
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df_raw.copy()
unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

def parse_date_any(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return None
    s = str(v).strip()
    fmts = [
        "%Y-%m-%d", "%Y/%m/%d", "%d-%m-%Y", "%d/%m/%Y",
        "%d.%m.%Y", "%m-%d-%Y", "%m/%d/%Y",
        "%d-%b-%Y", "%d %b %Y", "%d-%B-%Y", "%d %B %Y",
        "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
    ]
    for f in fmts:
        try:
            return datetime.strptime(s[:len(f) + 4], f).date()
        except:
            continue
    try:
        d = pd.to_datetime(s, dayfirst=True, errors="coerce")
        return d.date() if pd.notna(d) else None
    except:
        return None

# =========================================================
# POSITIONALLY-ALIGNED AGGREGATION
# (no dropna, no unique -> every column keeps 1 element per row
#  so attch_id stays perfectly aligned with date_of_purchase)
# =========================================================
def join_aligned(series):
    out = []
    for v in series.tolist():
        if v is None:
            out.append("Not available")
            continue
        try:
            if pd.isna(v):
                out.append("Not available")
                continue
        except Exception:
            pass
        s = str(v).strip()
        out.append(s if s != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(out)

unst_agg = unst_df.groupby(JOIN_KEYS, as_index=False).agg(join_aligned)

print(f"unst aggregated rows (per header_crm_id+sr_id): {len(unst_agg)}")

# =========================================================
# MERGE  (base grain preserved -> raw base data unchanged)
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_agg.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE CHECK  (OR LOGIC, aligned attch_id)
# =========================================================
def check_date_attachmentwise(expected_date, observed_dates, attch_ids):
    """
    Match if ANY observed value matches the expected date.

    Rules:
      - ANY element matches expected            -> MATCH (flag 0), report matching attch_id(s)
      - All observed values missing/not-avail   -> MATCH (flag 0)
      - Valid value(s) present but none match    -> MISMATCH (flag 1)

    Returns: flag, matched_attchs, mismatch_attchs
    """
    expected = parse_date_any(expected_date)

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_dates).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched_attchs   = []
    mismatch_attchs  = []
    valid_value_seen = False

    for idx, obs_date in enumerate(obs_list):

        # attch_id is now aligned; safe fallback just in case
        if idx < len(attch_list):
            attch = attch_list[idx]
        elif attch_list:
            attch = attch_list[-1]
        else:
            attch = ""

        # Skip missing / invalid observed values
        if is_missing(obs_date):
            continue

        valid_value_seen = True
        obs = parse_date_any(obs_date)

        if expected is not None and obs is not None and obs == expected:
            matched_attchs.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatch_attchs.append(attch)

    matched_attchs  = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched_attchs if a]))
    mismatch_attchs = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatch_attchs if a]))

    # CASE 1: all values missing / not available -> MATCH
    if not valid_value_seen:
        return 0, "", ""

    # CASE 2: at least one matched -> MATCH
    if matched_attchs:
        return 0, ",".join(matched_attchs), ""

    # CASE 3: valid values present but none matched -> MISMATCH
    return 1, "", ",".join(mismatch_attchs)

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK  (use ALIGNED unst attch_id)
# =========================================================
temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_date_attachmentwise(
        r.get("purchase_date"),
        r.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")          # <-- aligned attach ids from unst table
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"] = temp.apply(lambda x: x[0]).astype(int)
merged_df["matched_attch_ids"]      = temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["mismatch_attch_ids"]     = temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

# Output attch_id = aligned unst attach ids (fallback to base attch_id if unst missing)
def resolve_attch(r):
    u = r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("attch_id")

merged_df["attch_id_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_attch, axis=1)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def remark_text(flag):
    if flag == 0:
        return "purchase date is matching with system date"
    else:
        return "purchase date is not matching with system date"

def additional_remarks_text(row):
    if row["date_of_purchase_check"] == 0:
        if row["matched_attch_ids"]:
            return f"Purchase date matched with attachment(s): {row['matched_attch_ids']}"
        else:
            return "Purchase date was not extracted in any attachment"
    else:
        return f"Purchase date mismatch in attachment(s): {row['mismatch_attch_ids']}"

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":            CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":          CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":          now_ts,
    "updated_at":          now_ts,
    "is_active":           merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":       merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":           merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":            merged_df["attch_id_out"],
    "category":            merged_df.get("category"),
    "dop_observed_value":  merged_df.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
    "dop_expected_value":  merged_df.get("purchase_date"),
    "exception_flag":      merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(
        lambda x: "yes" if x == 1 else "no"
    ),
    "reason":              merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(remark_text),
})

output_df["additional_remarks"] = merged_df.apply(additional_remarks_text, axis=1)


output_df["reason"]=np.where((output_df["additional_remarks"].isin(["Purchase date was not extracted in any attachment"])),"Purchase date was not extracted in any attachment",output_df["reason"])


def remove_duplicate_attch_ids(val):
    if pd.isna(val):
        return val
    return "~".join(dict.fromkeys(str(val).split("~")))

output_df["attch_id"] = output_df["attch_id"].apply(remove_duplicate_attch_ids)





output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")

# =========================================================
# SUMMARY COUNT
# =========================================================
total_rows   = len(output_df)
match_count  = (output_df["exception_flag"] == "no").sum()
mismatch_cnt = (output_df["exception_flag"] == "yes").sum()

print("----------------------------------------")
print("SUMMARY")
print(f"Total rows       : {total_rows}")
print(f"Matches (no)     : {match_count}")
print(f"Mismatches (yes) : {mismatch_cnt}")
print("----------------------------------------")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""

import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein
import numpy as np

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1001
CHECK_NAME  = "DOP matched with Customer Invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1001"

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA  (raw dataframes kept UNCHANGED)
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df_raw = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows (RAW): {len(unst_df_raw)}")   # should print 6802

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS  (work on a COPY, raw stays intact)
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df_raw.copy()
unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

def parse_date_any(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return None
    s = str(v).strip()
    fmts = [
        "%Y-%m-%d", "%Y/%m/%d", "%d-%m-%Y", "%d/%m/%Y",
        "%d.%m.%Y", "%m-%d-%Y", "%m/%d/%Y",
        "%d-%b-%Y", "%d %b %Y", "%d-%B-%Y", "%d %B %Y",
        "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
    ]
    for f in fmts:
        try:
            return datetime.strptime(s[:len(f) + 4], f).date()
        except:
            continue
    try:
        d = pd.to_datetime(s, dayfirst=True, errors="coerce")
        return d.date() if pd.notna(d) else None
    except:
        return None

# =========================================================
# POSITIONALLY-ALIGNED AGGREGATION
# (no dropna, no unique -> every column keeps 1 element per row
#  so attch_id stays perfectly aligned with date_of_purchase)
# =========================================================
def join_aligned(series):
    out = []
    for v in series.tolist():
        if v is None:
            out.append("Not available")
            continue
        try:
            if pd.isna(v):
                out.append("Not available")
                continue
        except Exception:
            pass
        s = str(v).strip()
        out.append(s if s != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(out)

unst_agg = unst_df.groupby(JOIN_KEYS, as_index=False).agg(join_aligned)

print(f"unst aggregated rows (per header_crm_id+sr_id): {len(unst_agg)}")

# =========================================================
# MERGE  (base grain preserved -> raw base data unchanged)
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_agg.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE CHECK  (OR LOGIC, aligned attch_id)
# =========================================================
def check_date_attachmentwise(expected_date, observed_dates, attch_ids):
    """
    Match if ANY observed value matches the expected date.

    Rules:
      - ANY element matches expected            -> MATCH (flag 0), report matching attch_id(s)
      - All observed values missing/not-avail   -> MATCH (flag 0)
      - Valid value(s) present but none match    -> MISMATCH (flag 1)

    Returns: flag, matched_attchs, mismatch_attchs
    """
    expected = parse_date_any(expected_date)

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_dates).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched_attchs   = []
    mismatch_attchs  = []
    valid_value_seen = False

    for idx, obs_date in enumerate(obs_list):

        # attch_id is now aligned; safe fallback just in case
        if idx < len(attch_list):
            attch = attch_list[idx]
        elif attch_list:
            attch = attch_list[-1]
        else:
            attch = ""

        # Skip missing / invalid observed values
        if is_missing(obs_date):
            continue

        valid_value_seen = True
        obs = parse_date_any(obs_date)

        if expected is not None and obs is not None and obs == expected:
            matched_attchs.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatch_attchs.append(attch)

    matched_attchs  = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched_attchs if a]))
    mismatch_attchs = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatch_attchs if a]))

    # CASE 1: all values missing / not available -> MATCH
    if not valid_value_seen:
        return 0, "", ""

    # CASE 2: at least one matched -> MATCH
    if matched_attchs:
        return 0, ",".join(matched_attchs), ""

    # CASE 3: valid values present but none matched -> MISMATCH
    return 1, "", ",".join(mismatch_attchs)

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK  (use ALIGNED unst attch_id)
# =========================================================
temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_date_attachmentwise(
        r.get("purchase_date"),
        r.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")          # <-- aligned attach ids from unst table
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"] = temp.apply(lambda x: x[0]).astype(int)
merged_df["matched_attch_ids"]      = temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["mismatch_attch_ids"]     = temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

# Output attch_id = aligned unst attach ids (fallback to base attch_id if unst missing)
def resolve_attch(r):
    u = r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("attch_id")

merged_df["attch_id_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_attch, axis=1)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def remark_text(flag):
    if flag == 0:
        return "purchase date is matching with system date"
    else:
        return "purchase date is not matching with system date"

def additional_remarks_text(row):
    if row["date_of_purchase_check"] == 0:
        if row["matched_attch_ids"]:
            return f"Purchase date matched with attachment(s): {row['matched_attch_ids']}"
        else:
            return "Purchase date was not extracted in any attachment"
    else:
        return f"Purchase date mismatch in attachment(s): {row['mismatch_attch_ids']}"

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":            CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":          CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":          now_ts,
    "updated_at":          now_ts,
    "is_active":           merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":       merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":           merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":            merged_df["attch_id_out"],
    "category":            merged_df.get("category"),
    "dop_observed_value":  merged_df.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
    "dop_expected_value":  merged_df.get("purchase_date"),
    "exception_flag":      merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(
        lambda x: "yes" if x == 1 else "no"
    ),
    "reason":              merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(remark_text),
})

output_df["additional_remarks"] = merged_df.apply(additional_remarks_text, axis=1)


output_df["reason"]=np.where((output_df["additional_remarks"].isin(["Purchase date was not extracted in any attachment"])),"Purchase date was not extracted in any attachment",output_df["reason"])


def remove_duplicate_attch_ids(val):
    if pd.isna(val):
        return val
    return "~".join(dict.fromkeys(str(val).split("~")))

output_df["attch_id"] = output_df["attch_id"].apply(remove_duplicate_attch_ids)





output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")

# =========================================================
# SUMMARY COUNT
# =========================================================
total_rows   = len(output_df)
match_count  = (output_df["exception_flag"] == "no").sum()
mismatch_cnt = (output_df["exception_flag"] == "yes").sum()

print("----------------------------------------")
print("SUMMARY")
print(f"Total rows       : {total_rows}")
print(f"Matches (no)     : {match_count}")
print(f"Mismatches (yes) : {mismatch_cnt}")
print("----------------------------------------")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""

# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id", "check_name", "created_at", "updated_at", "is_active",

    "dop_observed_value", "dop_expected_value",

               if c not in ["check_id", "header_crm_id", "sr_number", "attch_id", "created_at"]]

import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1004
CHECK_NAME  = "Name and Serial Number match with Customer Invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1004"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "customer_name": {"ratio": 0.70, "max_edits": 5},
    "serial":        {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 2},
}

# Base columns to compare against unst serial
SERIAL_BASE_COLS = [
    "sr_serial_number",
    "sr_split_serial_number",
]

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA  (raw dataframes kept UNCHANGED)
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df_raw = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows (RAW): {len(unst_df_raw)}")   # should print 6802

# =========================================================
# CATEGORY LOOKUP  (attch_id -> category from base_df)
# =========================================================
CATEGORY_LOOKUP = {}
for _, _r in base_df.iterrows():
    _aid = _r.get("attch_id")
    _cat = _r.get("category")
    if _aid is None:
        continue
    _aid = str(_aid).strip()
    if _aid == "" or _aid in CATEGORY_LOOKUP:
        continue
    CATEGORY_LOOKUP[_aid] = ("" if _cat is None else str(_cat).strip())

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS  (work on a COPY, raw stays intact)
# NOTE: attch_id removed from JOIN_KEYS so attachments aggregate with ~
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df_raw.copy()
unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "not_available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found",
    "blank", "unknown", "missing",
    "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."
}

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES

def all_observed_missing(observed_str):
    """True only if EVERY ~-separated observed value is missing/not-available."""
    if observed_str is None:
        return True
    parts = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    return all(is_invalid(p) for p in parts)

def norm_alnum_upper(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())

def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s

def split_multi(v, sep=r"[\^,;/|]"):
    if is_missing(v):
        return []
    return [x.strip() for x in re.split(sep, str(v)) if x.strip()]

def serial_set(v):
    """Return set of normalized serial numbers (uppercase alnum)."""
    out = set()
    for part in split_multi(v):
        s = norm_alnum_upper(part)
        if s:
            out.add(s)
    return out

def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()

def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)

def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False

def any_pair_matches(set_a, set_b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not set_a or not set_b:
        return False
    if set_a & set_b:
        return True
    for x in set_a:
        for y in set_b:
            if fuzzy_match(x, y, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
                return True
    return False

# =========================================================
# POSITIONALLY-ALIGNED AGGREGATION
# =========================================================
def join_aligned(series):
    out = []
    for v in series.tolist():
        if v is None:
            out.append("Not available")
            continue
        try:
            if pd.isna(v):
                out.append("Not available")
                continue
        except Exception:
            pass
        s = str(v).strip()
        out.append(s if s != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(out)

unst_agg = unst_df.groupby(JOIN_KEYS, as_index=False).agg(join_aligned)

print(f"unst aggregated rows (per header_crm_id+sr_id): {len(unst_agg)}")

# =========================================================
# DEDUP BASE TO ONE ROW PER SR
# =========================================================
base_one_per_sr = base_df.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS, keep="first").copy()
print(f"base_df deduped to one row per SR: {len(base_one_per_sr)}")

# =========================================================
# MERGE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_one_per_sr,
    unst_agg.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE CUSTOMER NAME CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_customer_name_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                                       t=THRESHOLDS["customer_name"]):
    """
    Match if ANY observed customer name matches expected.
    Returns: flag('yes'/'no'), matched_attchs, mismatch_attchs
    """
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_text(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_text(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True
        if a_norm == b_norm:
            matched.append(attch)
        elif fuzz.token_set_ratio(a_norm, b_norm) >= t["ratio"] * 100:
            matched.append(attch)
        elif edit_distance(a_norm, b_norm) <= t["max_edits"]:
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE SERIAL CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_serial_attachmentwise(base_vals, observed_str, attch_ids,
                                t=THRESHOLDS["serial"]):
    """
    Match if ANY observed serial (per attachment) matches ANY valid base serial.
    Returns: flag('yes'/'no'), matched_attchs, mismatch_attchs, matched_col
    """
    # Build per-column base sets
    col_sets = {}
    any_valid_base = False
    for col_name in SERIAL_BASE_COLS:
        val = base_vals.get(col_name)
        if is_invalid(val):
            continue
        s = serial_set(val)
        if not s:
            continue
        any_valid_base = True
        col_sets[col_name] = s

    # No valid base serial -> not present in crm -> treat as match
    if not any_valid_base:
        return "yes", "", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False
    matched_cols_all = set()

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        obs_set = serial_set(obs)
        if not obs_set:
            continue

        valid_seen = True

        this_cols = []
        for col_name, bset in col_sets.items():
            if any_pair_matches(obs_set, bset, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
                this_cols.append(col_name)

        if this_cols:
            matched.append(attch)
            matched_cols_all.update(this_cols)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    # Determine matched-column label
    if len(matched_cols_all) == len(SERIAL_BASE_COLS):
        matched_col = "both"
    elif matched_cols_all:
        matched_col = next(iter(matched_cols_all))
    else:
        matched_col = ""

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), "", matched_col
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched), ""

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECKS
# =========================================================
def row_check(r):
    name_flag, name_matched_attch, name_mismatch_attch = \
        check_customer_name_attachmentwise(
            r.get("customer_name"),
            r.get("customer_name_unst_str"),
            r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
        )

    base_vals = {c: r.get(c) for c in SERIAL_BASE_COLS}
    serial_flag, serial_matched_attch, serial_mismatch_attch, matched_col = \
        check_serial_attachmentwise(
            base_vals,
            r.get("product_serial_number_unst_str"),
            r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
        )

    return pd.Series({
        "customer_name_match":         name_flag,
        "name_matched_attch":          name_matched_attch,
        "name_mismatch_attch":         name_mismatch_attch,
        "product_serial_match":        serial_flag,
        "serial_matched_attch":        serial_matched_attch,
        "serial_mismatch_attch":       serial_mismatch_attch,
        "serial_matched_with_column":  matched_col if matched_col else "",
    })

check_results = merged_df.apply(row_check, axis=1)
for col in ["customer_name_match", "name_matched_attch", "name_mismatch_attch",
            "product_serial_match", "serial_matched_attch", "serial_mismatch_attch",
            "serial_matched_with_column"]:
    merged_df[col] = check_results[col]

# =========================================================
# resolve attch_id + category (~ separated)
# =========================================================
def resolve_attch(r):
    u = r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("attch_id")

merged_df["attch_id_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_attch, axis=1)

def build_category(attch_str):
    if attch_str is None or (isinstance(attch_str, float) and pd.isna(attch_str)):
        return None
    ids = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_str).split("~")]
    cats = []
    for aid in ids:
        cat = CATEGORY_LOOKUP.get(aid, "")
        cats.append(cat if cat != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(cats)

merged_df["category_out"] = merged_df["attch_id_out"].apply(build_category)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def all_base_serials_invalid(row):
    return all(is_invalid(row.get(c)) for c in SERIAL_BASE_COLS)

def build_exception_flag(name_match, serial_match):
    if name_match == "yes" and serial_match == "yes":
        return "no"
    return "yes"

# reason: priority -> not present in crm > was not extracted > matching/not matching
def build_reason(row):
    # ---------- CUSTOMER NAME ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("customer_name")):
        name_txt = "customer name not present in crm"
    elif all_observed_missing(row.get("customer_name_unst_str")):
        name_txt = "customer name was not extracted"
    elif row["customer_name_match"] == "yes":
        name_txt = "customer name is matching"
    else:
        name_txt = "customer name is not matching"

    # ---------- SERIAL ----------
    if all_base_serials_invalid(row):
        serial_txt = "serial number not present in crm"
    elif all_observed_missing(row.get("product_serial_number_unst_str")):
        serial_txt = "serial number was not extracted"
    elif row["product_serial_match"] == "yes":
        mc = row["serial_matched_with_column"]
        if mc == "both":
            serial_txt = ("product serial number is matching with both "
                          "sr_serial_number and sr_split_serial_number")
        elif mc:
            serial_txt = f"product serial number is matching with {mc}"
        else:
            serial_txt = "product serial number is matching"
    else:
        serial_txt = "product serial number is not matching"

    return f"{name_txt}; {serial_txt}"

# additional_remarks: same priority + attachment IDs
def build_additional_remarks(row):
    parts = []

    # ---------- CUSTOMER NAME ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("customer_name")):
        parts.append("customer_name not present in crm")
    elif all_observed_missing(row.get("customer_name_unst_str")):
        parts.append("customer_name was not extracted")
    elif row["customer_name_match"] == "yes":
        parts.append(f"Customer name matched with attachment(s): {row['name_matched_attch']}")
    else:
        parts.append(f"Customer name mismatch in attachment(s): {row['name_mismatch_attch']}")

    # ---------- SERIAL ----------
    if all_base_serials_invalid(row):
        parts.append("serial_number not present in crm")
    elif all_observed_missing(row.get("product_serial_number_unst_str")):
        parts.append("serial_number was not extracted")
    elif row["product_serial_match"] == "yes":
        mc = row["serial_matched_with_column"]
        col_txt = ("both sr_serial_number and sr_split_serial_number"
                   if mc == "both" else (f"'{mc}'" if mc else "serial column"))
        parts.append(f"Serial matched with {col_txt} in attachment(s): {row['serial_matched_attch']}")
    else:
        parts.append(f"Serial mismatch in attachment(s): {row['serial_mismatch_attch']}")

    return " | ".join(parts)

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                             CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                           CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                           now_ts,
    "updated_at":                           now_ts,
    "is_active":                            merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                        merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                            merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                             merged_df["attch_id_out"],
    "category":                             merged_df["category_out"],
    "customer_name_observed_value":         merged_df.get("customer_name_unst_str"),
    "customer_name_expected_value":         merged_df.get("customer_name"),
    "product_serial_number_observed_value": merged_df.get("product_serial_number_unst_str"),
    "sr_serial_number_expected_value":      merged_df.get("sr_serial_number"),
    "sr_split_serial_number_expected_value":merged_df.get("sr_split_serial_number"),
    "customer_name_match":                  merged_df["customer_name_match"],
    "product_serial_match":                 merged_df["product_serial_match"],
    "serial_matched_with_column":           merged_df["serial_matched_with_column"],
    "exception_flag": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_exception_flag(r["customer_name_match"], r["product_serial_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "reason":              merged_df.apply(build_reason, axis=1),
    "additional_remarks":  merged_df.apply(build_additional_remarks, axis=1),
})

# =========================================================
# JOINT DEDUP: attch_id + category stay 1:1 aligned
# =========================================================
def dedup_attch_and_category(attch_val, cat_val):
    if pd.isna(attch_val) or attch_val is None:
        return attch_val, cat_val

    attch_list = str(attch_val).split("~")
    cat_list   = str(cat_val).split("~") if (cat_val is not None and not pd.isna(cat_val)) else []

    seen = set()
    out_attch, out_cat = [], []

    for idx, a in enumerate(attch_list):
        if a in seen:
            continue
        seen.add(a)
        out_attch.append(a)
        if idx < len(cat_list):
            out_cat.append(cat_list[idx])

    return "~".join(out_attch), "~".join(out_cat)

_deduped = output_df.apply(
    lambda r: dedup_attch_and_category(r["attch_id"], r["category"]),
    axis=1
)
output_df["attch_id"] = _deduped.apply(lambda x: x[0])
output_df["category"] = _deduped.apply(lambda x: x[1])

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Name match=yes:   {(output_df['customer_name_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Name match=no:    {(output_df['customer_name_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Serial match=yes: {(output_df['product_serial_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Serial match=no:  {(output_df['product_serial_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no (both match):            {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes (one or both mismatch): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "customer_name_observed_value",
    "customer_name_expected_value",
    "product_serial_number_observed_value",
    "sr_serial_number_expected_value",
    "sr_split_serial_number_expected_value",
    "customer_name_match","product_serial_match","serial_matched_with_column",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1004")

from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# DB CONFIG

)

# =========================================================

THRESHOLDS = {
    "customer_name": {"ratio": 0.70, "max_edits": 5},
    "serial":        {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 2},
}

# Base columns to compare against unst serial
SERIAL_BASE_COLS = [
    "sr_serial_number",
    "sr_split_serial_number",
]

)
unst_df = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows: {len(unst_df)}")

merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "error", "na", "n/a"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS


def norm_alnum_upper(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())


def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s


def split_multi(v, sep=r"[\^,;/|]"):
    if is_missing(v):
        return []
    return [x.strip() for x in re.split(sep, str(v)) if x.strip()]


def serial_set(v):
    """Return set of normalized serial numbers (uppercase alnum)."""
    out = set()
    for part in split_multi(v):
        s = norm_alnum_upper(part)
        if s:
            out.add(s)
    return out


def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()


def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)


def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False


def any_pair_matches(set_a, set_b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not set_a or not set_b:
        return False
    if set_a & set_b:
        return True
    for x in set_a:
        for y in set_b:
            if fuzzy_match(x, y, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
                return True
    return False


INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found"
}

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES


def check_customer_name(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["customer_name"]):
    """
    Customer name check logic:
        "yes" = matching (or unst value is 'not available' -> treat as matching)
        "no"  = not matching
    """

    # If OBSERVED (invoice) value is invalid / not available -> treat as MATCH
    if is_invalid(b):
        return "yes"

    if is_invalid(a):
        return "no"

    a_norm, b_norm = norm_text(a), norm_text(b)

    if not a_norm or not b_norm:
        if not b_norm:
            return "yes"
        return "no"

    if a_norm == b_norm:
        return "yes"

    score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a_norm, b_norm)
    if score >= t["ratio"] * 100:
        return "yes"

    if edit_distance(a_norm, b_norm) <= t["max_edits"]:
        return "yes"

    return "no"


# def check_serial_against_many(unst_val, base_vals, t=THRESHOLDS["serial"]):
#     """
#     Check unst serial(s) against ALL base columns independently.
#     Returns (matched_flag, matched_columns_str)
#     matched_columns_str = "sr_serial_number", "sr_split_serial_number",
#                           "both", or "" if no match.
#     """
#     unst_set = serial_set(unst_val)
#     if not unst_set:
#         return 0, ""

#     matched_cols = []
#     for col_name, val in base_vals.items():
#         base_set = serial_set(val)
#         if any_pair_matches(unst_set, base_set, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
#             matched_cols.append(col_name)

#     if not matched_cols:
#         return 0, ""
#     if len(matched_cols) == len(SERIAL_BASE_COLS):
#         return 1, "both"
#     return 1, matched_cols[0]


def check_serial_against_many(unst_val, base_vals, t=THRESHOLDS["serial"]):
    """
    Returns:
        flag, matched_columns_str

    flag:
        "yes" = Match found with at least one of sr_serial_number
                or sr_split_serial_number
                OR unst value is 'not available' (treat as matching)
        "no"  = Not Match

    matched_columns_str:
        "sr_serial_number"
        "sr_split_serial_number"
        "both"
        "" (empty)
    """

    # If OBSERVED value is invalid / not available -> treat as MATCH
    if is_invalid(unst_val):
        return "yes", ""

    unst_set = serial_set(unst_val)
    if not unst_set:
        return "yes", ""

    matched_cols = []
    valid_base_found = False

    for col_name, val in base_vals.items():
        if is_invalid(val):
            continue

        base_set = serial_set(val)
        if not base_set:
            continue

        valid_base_found = True

        if any_pair_matches(
            unst_set,
            base_set,
            t["ratio"],
            t["max_edits"]
        ):
            matched_cols.append(col_name)

    if matched_cols:
        if len(matched_cols) == len(SERIAL_BASE_COLS):
            return "yes", "both"
        return "yes", matched_cols[0]

    if not valid_base_found:
        return "no", ""

    return "no", ""


# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECKS
# =========================================================
def row_check(r):
    name_flag = check_customer_name(
        r.get("customer_name"), r.get("customer_name_unst_str")
    )

    base_vals = {c: r.get(c) for c in SERIAL_BASE_COLS}
    serial_flag, matched_col = check_serial_against_many(
        r.get("product_serial_number_unst_str"), base_vals
    )

    return pd.Series({
        "customer_name_match":        name_flag,       # "yes" / "no"
        "product_serial_match":       serial_flag,     # "yes" / "no"
        "serial_matched_with_column": matched_col if matched_col else ""
    })

check_results = merged_df.apply(row_check, axis=1)
merged_df["customer_name_match"]        = check_results["customer_name_match"]
merged_df["product_serial_match"]       = check_results["product_serial_match"]
merged_df["serial_matched_with_column"] = check_results["serial_matched_with_column"]

test = merged_df.loc[:, [
    "customer_name", "customer_name_unst_str", "customer_name_match",
    "sr_serial_number", "sr_split_serial_number",
    "product_serial_number_unst_str", "product_serial_match",
    "serial_matched_with_column"
]]


# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(name_match, serial_match):
    if name_match == "yes" and serial_match == "yes":
        return "no"
    return "yes"


def build_observed_value(name_match, serial_match, matched_col):
    name_txt = (
        "customer name is matching"
        if name_match == "yes"
        else "customer name is not matching"
    )

    if serial_match == "yes":
        if matched_col == "both":
            serial_txt = (
                "product serial number is matching with both "
                "sr_serial_number and sr_split_serial_number"
            )
        elif matched_col:
            serial_txt = f"product serial number is matching with {matched_col}"
        else:
            serial_txt = "product serial number is matching"
    else:
        serial_txt = "product serial number is not matching"

    return f"{name_txt}; {serial_txt}"


def build_additional_remarks(name_match, serial_match, matched_col):

    if name_match == "yes" and serial_match == "yes":
        if matched_col == "both":
            return (
                "Both customer name and product serial number are matching "
                "with customer invoice (serial matched with both "
                "sr_serial_number and sr_split_serial_number)"
            )
        if matched_col:
            return (
                f"Both customer name and product serial number are matching "
                f"with customer invoice (serial matched with '{matched_col}')"
            )
        return "Both customer name and product serial number are matching with customer invoice"

    if name_match == "no" and serial_match == "yes":
        if matched_col == "both":
            return (
                "Customer name is not matching but product serial number is "
                "matching with both sr_serial_number and sr_split_serial_number"
            )
        if matched_col:
            return (
                f"Customer name is not matching but product serial number is "
                f"matching with '{matched_col}'"
            )
        return "Customer name is not matching but product serial number is matching"

    if name_match == "yes" and serial_match == "no":
        return (
            "Customer name is matching but product serial number is not "
            "matching "
        )

    return (
        "Both customer name and product serial number are not matching "
        "with customer invoice"
    )


output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                       CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                     CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                     now_ts,
    "updated_at":                     now_ts,
    "is_active":                      merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                  merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                      merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                       merged_df["attch_id"],
    "category":                       merged_df.get("category"),
    "customer_name_observed_value":         merged_df.get("customer_name_unst_str"),
    "customer_name_expected_value":                  merged_df.get("customer_name"),
    "product_serial_number_observed_value": merged_df.get("product_serial_number_unst_str"),
    "sr_serial_number_expected_value":               merged_df.get("sr_serial_number"),
    "sr_split_serial_number_expected_value":         merged_df.get("sr_split_serial_number"),
    "customer_name_match":            merged_df["customer_name_match"],
    "product_serial_match":           merged_df["product_serial_match"],
    "serial_matched_with_column":     merged_df["serial_matched_with_column"],
    "exception_flag": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_exception_flag(r["customer_name_match"], r["product_serial_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_observed_value(
            r["customer_name_match"],
            r["product_serial_match"],
            r["serial_matched_with_column"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
    "additional_remarks": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_additional_remarks(
            r["customer_name_match"],
            r["product_serial_match"],
            r["serial_matched_with_column"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
})

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test=output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']


aa=output_df.groupby(['customer_name_match','product_serial_match','exception_flag']).agg({'header_crm_id':'count'}).unstack().reset_index()

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Name match=yes:   {(output_df['customer_name_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Name match=no:    {(output_df['customer_name_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Serial match=yes: {(output_df['product_serial_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Serial match=no:  {(output_df['product_serial_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no (both match): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes (one or both mismatch): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id VARCHAR(255),

#   customer_name_unst_str TEXT,
#   customer_name TEXT,
#   product_serial_number_unst_str TEXT,
#   sr_serial_number TEXT,
#   sr_split_serial_number TEXT,
#   customer_name_match TINYINT,
#   product_serial_match TINYINT,
#   serial_matched_with_column VARCHAR(100),
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   observed_value TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id)
# )
# """

# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()


insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "customer_name_observed_value",
    "customer_name_expected_value",
    "product_serial_number_observed_value",
    "sr_serial_number_expected_value",
    "sr_split_serial_number_expected_value",
    "customer_name_match","product_serial_match","serial_matched_with_column",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1004")
