import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1003
CHECK_NAME  = "Contact details match with Customer Invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1003"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "phone": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 2},
}

# Base columns to compare against unst phone
PHONE_BASE_COLS = [
    "customer_contact",
    "customer_registered_phone",
    "customer_alternate_phone",
    "customer_sr_raise_phone",
]

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA  (raw dataframes kept UNCHANGED)
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df_raw = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows (RAW): {len(unst_df_raw)}")   # should print 6802

# =========================================================
# CATEGORY LOOKUP  (attch_id -> category from base_df)
# =========================================================
CATEGORY_LOOKUP = {}
for _, _r in base_df.iterrows():
    _aid = _r.get("attch_id")
    _cat = _r.get("category")
    if _aid is None:
        continue
    _aid = str(_aid).strip()
    if _aid == "" or _aid in CATEGORY_LOOKUP:
        continue
    CATEGORY_LOOKUP[_aid] = ("" if _cat is None else str(_cat).strip())

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS  (work on a COPY, raw stays intact)
# NOTE: attch_id removed from JOIN_KEYS so attachments aggregate with ~
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df_raw.copy()
unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "not_available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found",
    "blank", "unknown", "missing",
    "not applicable",
    "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."
}

INVALID_SUBSTRINGS = (
    "not available",
    "not_available",
    "not found",
    "not applicable",
    "n/a",
)

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    s = str(v).strip().lower()
    if s == "" or s in INVALID_VALUES:
        return True
    for token in INVALID_SUBSTRINGS:
        if token in s:
            return True
    return False

def split_multi(v, sep=r"[\^,;/|]"):
    if is_missing(v):
        return []
    return [x.strip() for x in re.split(sep, str(v)) if x.strip()]

def last10_set(v):
    """Return set of last-10-digit phone numbers."""
    nums = set()
    for part in split_multi(v):
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)
        if len(digits) >= 10:
            nums.add(digits[-10:])
    return nums

def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()

def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)

def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False

def find_matching_phone(unst_set, base_set, t):
    """Return the matched phone (from base_set) if any pair matches (exact then fuzzy)."""
    if not unst_set or not base_set:
        return None
    common = unst_set & base_set
    if common:
        return next(iter(common))
    for x in unst_set:
        for y in base_set:
            if fuzzy_match(x, y, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
                return y
    return None

# =========================================================
# POSITIONALLY-ALIGNED AGGREGATION
# =========================================================
def join_aligned(series):
    out = []
    for v in series.tolist():
        if v is None:
            out.append("Not available")
            continue
        try:
            if pd.isna(v):
                out.append("Not available")
                continue
        except Exception:
            pass
        s = str(v).strip()
        out.append(s if s != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(out)

unst_agg = unst_df.groupby(JOIN_KEYS, as_index=False).agg(join_aligned)

print(f"unst aggregated rows (per header_crm_id+sr_id): {len(unst_agg)}")

# =========================================================
# DEDUP BASE TO ONE ROW PER SR
# =========================================================
base_one_per_sr = base_df.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS, keep="first").copy()
print(f"base_df deduped to one row per SR: {len(base_one_per_sr)}")

# =========================================================
# MERGE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_one_per_sr,
    unst_agg.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE PHONE CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_phone_attachmentwise(base_vals, observed_str, attch_ids,
                               t=THRESHOLDS["phone"]):
    """
    Match if ANY observed invoice phone (per attachment) matches ANY valid base phone.

    Returns:
        flag ('yes'/'no'),
        matched_attchs (str),
        mismatch_attchs (str),
        matched_phone (str),
        matched_col (str)
    """
    # Build combined base phone set + remember which column each number came from
    base_set = set()
    num_to_col = {}
    any_valid_base = False
    for col_name in PHONE_BASE_COLS:
        val = base_vals.get(col_name)
        if is_invalid(val):
            continue
        s = last10_set(val)
        if not s:
            continue
        any_valid_base = True
        for num in s:
            base_set.add(num)
            num_to_col.setdefault(num, col_name)

    # If NO valid base phone at all -> not present in crm -> treat as match
    if not any_valid_base:
        return "yes", "", "", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False
    matched_phone_out, matched_col_out = "", ""

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        obs_set = last10_set(obs)
        if not obs_set:
            continue

        valid_seen = True
        mp = find_matching_phone(obs_set, base_set, t)
        if mp:
            matched.append(attch)
            if not matched_phone_out:
                matched_phone_out = mp
                matched_col_out   = num_to_col.get(mp, "")
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    # All observed missing -> not extracted -> treat as match (no exception)
    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", "", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), "", matched_phone_out, matched_col_out
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched), "", ""

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK
# =========================================================
def row_check(r):
    base_vals = {c: r.get(c) for c in PHONE_BASE_COLS}
    flag, matched_attch, mismatch_attch, matched_phone, matched_col = \
        check_phone_attachmentwise(
            base_vals,
            r.get("customer_phone_number_unst_str"),
            r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
        )
    return pd.Series({
        "customer_contact_match":   flag,
        "matched_attch":            matched_attch,
        "mismatch_attch":           mismatch_attch,
        "matched_phone":            matched_phone,
        "matched_with_column":      matched_col,
    })

check_results = merged_df.apply(row_check, axis=1)
merged_df["customer_contact_match"] = check_results["customer_contact_match"]
merged_df["matched_attch"]          = check_results["matched_attch"]
merged_df["mismatch_attch"]         = check_results["mismatch_attch"]
merged_df["matched_phone"]          = check_results["matched_phone"]
merged_df["matched_with_column"]    = check_results["matched_with_column"]

# =========================================================
# resolve attch_id + category (~ separated)
# =========================================================
def resolve_attch(r):
    u = r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("attch_id")

merged_df["attch_id_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_attch, axis=1)

def build_category(attch_str):
    if attch_str is None or (isinstance(attch_str, float) and pd.isna(attch_str)):
        return None
    ids = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_str).split("~")]
    cats = []
    for aid in ids:
        cat = CATEGORY_LOOKUP.get(aid, "")
        cats.append(cat if cat != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(cats)

merged_df["category_out"] = merged_df["attch_id_out"].apply(build_category)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def all_base_phones_invalid(row):
    return all(is_invalid(row.get(c)) for c in PHONE_BASE_COLS)

def all_observed_missing(observed_str):
    if observed_str is None:
        return True
    parts = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    return all(is_invalid(p) for p in parts)

def build_exception_flag(match_flag):
    return "no" if match_flag == "yes" else "yes"

# reason: priority -> not present in crm > was not extracted > matching/not matching
def build_reason(row):
    if all_base_phones_invalid(row):
        return "customer phone number not present in crm"
    if all_observed_missing(row.get("customer_phone_number_unst_str")):
        return "customer phone number was not extracted"
    if row["customer_contact_match"] == "yes":
        if row["matched_phone"]:
            return (f"Customer phone number {row['matched_phone']} matched with "
                    f"'{row['matched_with_column']}'")
        return "Customer phone number is matching"
    return "Customer contact number is not matching with any of the phone numbers"

# additional_remarks: same priority + attachment IDs
def build_additional_remarks(row):
    if all_base_phones_invalid(row):
        return "customer phone number not present in crm"
    if all_observed_missing(row.get("customer_phone_number_unst_str")):
        return "customer phone number was not extracted"
    if row["customer_contact_match"] == "yes":
        if row["matched_phone"]:
            return (f"Phone {row['matched_phone']} matched with '{row['matched_with_column']}' "
                    f"in attachment(s): {row['matched_attch']}")
        return "Customer phone number is matching"
    return f"Customer phone number mismatch in attachment(s): {row['mismatch_attch']}"

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                                  CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                                CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                                now_ts,
    "updated_at":                                now_ts,
    "is_active":                                 merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                             merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                                 merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                                  merged_df["attch_id_out"],
    "category":                                  merged_df["category_out"],
    "customer_phone_number_observed_value":      merged_df.get("customer_phone_number_unst_str"),
    "customer_contact_expected_value":           merged_df.get("customer_contact"),
    "customer_registered_phone_expected_value":  merged_df.get("customer_registered_phone"),
    "customer_alternate_phone_expected_value":   merged_df.get("customer_alternate_phone"),
    "customer_sr_raise_phone_expected_value":    merged_df.get("customer_sr_raise_phone"),
    "customer_contact_match":                    merged_df["customer_contact_match"],
    "matched_with_column": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: (f"{r['matched_phone']} (in {r['matched_with_column']})"
                   if r["matched_phone"] else ""),
        axis=1
    ),
    "exception_flag": merged_df["customer_contact_match"].apply(build_exception_flag),
    "reason":              merged_df.apply(build_reason, axis=1),
    "additional_remarks":  merged_df.apply(build_additional_remarks, axis=1),
})

# =========================================================
# JOINT DEDUP: attch_id + category stay 1:1 aligned
# =========================================================
def dedup_attch_and_category(attch_val, cat_val):
    if pd.isna(attch_val) or attch_val is None:
        return attch_val, cat_val

    attch_list = str(attch_val).split("~")
    cat_list   = str(cat_val).split("~") if (cat_val is not None and not pd.isna(cat_val)) else []

    seen = set()
    out_attch, out_cat = [], []

    for idx, a in enumerate(attch_list):
        if a in seen:
            continue
        seen.add(a)
        out_attch.append(a)
        if idx < len(cat_list):
            out_cat.append(cat_list[idx])

    return "~".join(out_attch), "~".join(out_cat)

_deduped = output_df.apply(
    lambda r: dedup_attch_and_category(r["attch_id"], r["category"]),
    axis=1
)
output_df["attch_id"] = _deduped.apply(lambda x: x[0])
output_df["category"] = _deduped.apply(lambda x: x[1])

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

# ==== Diagnostic prints ====
print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Match=yes (matched):     {(output_df['customer_contact_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Match=no  (not matched): {(output_df['customer_contact_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes:           {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no:            {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   updated_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id TEXT,
#   category TEXT,
#   customer_phone_number_observed_value TEXT,
#   customer_contact_expected_value TEXT,
#   customer_registered_phone_expected_value TEXT,
#   customer_alternate_phone_expected_value TEXT,
#   customer_sr_raise_phone_expected_value TEXT,
#   customer_contact_match VARCHAR(10),
#   matched_with_column VARCHAR(100),
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   reason TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id(255))
# )
# """
# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "customer_phone_number_observed_value",
    "customer_contact_expected_value",
    "customer_registered_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_alternate_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_sr_raise_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_contact_match","matched_with_column",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols
               if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1003")

import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1003
CHECK_NAME  = "Contact details match with Customer Invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1003"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "phone": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 2},
}

# Base columns to compare against unst phone
PHONE_BASE_COLS = [
    "customer_contact",
    "customer_registered_phone",
    "customer_alternate_phone",
    "customer_sr_raise_phone",
]

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows: {len(unst_df)}")

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id", "attch_id"]

unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# MERGE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_df.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "error", "na", "n/a"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS


def split_multi(v, sep=r"[\^,;/|]"):
    if is_missing(v):
        return []
    return [x.strip() for x in re.split(sep, str(v)) if x.strip()]


def last10_set(v):
    """Return set of last-10-digit phone numbers."""
    nums = set()
    for part in split_multi(v):
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)
        if len(digits) >= 10:
            nums.add(digits[-10:])
    return nums


def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()


def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)


def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False


INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found",
    "blank", "unknown", "missing",
    "not applicable",
    "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."
}

# Substrings that should trigger invalid detection anywhere in the string
INVALID_SUBSTRINGS = (
    "not available",
    "not found",
    "not applicable",
    "n/a",
)

def is_invalid(v):
    """
    Returns True if the value is None, NaN, empty, or contains any known
    NA-like token (case-insensitive, whitespace-tolerant).
    """
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    s = str(v).strip().lower()
    if s == "" or s in INVALID_VALUES:
        return True
    # Substring safety net (handles "Not Available", "  not available  ", etc.)
    for token in INVALID_SUBSTRINGS:
        if token in s:
            return True
    return False


def find_matching_phone(unst_set, base_set, t):
    """
    Return the actual matched phone number (from base_set) if any pair matches.
    Prefers exact match first, then fuzzy match.
    """
    if not unst_set or not base_set:
        return None
    # Exact match first
    common = unst_set & base_set
    if common:
        return next(iter(common))
    # Fuzzy match
    for x in unst_set:
        for y in base_set:
            if fuzzy_match(x, y, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
                return y
    return None


def check_phone_against_many(unst_val, base_vals, t=THRESHOLDS["phone"]):
    """
    Returns:
        match_flag_str, matched_phone, matched_column

    match_flag_str:
        "yes" = Matched with at least one base column
                OR observed value is 'Not available' / invalid (skip check -> yes)
        "no"  = Not matched
    """
    # If OBSERVED (invoice) value is invalid / not available -> treat as MATCH
    if is_invalid(unst_val):
        return "yes", "", ""

    unst_set = last10_set(unst_val)
    if not unst_set:
        return "yes", "", ""

    found_valid_base = False

    for col_name, val in base_vals.items():
        if is_invalid(val):
            continue

        base_set = last10_set(val)
        if not base_set:
            continue

        found_valid_base = True

        matched_phone = find_matching_phone(unst_set, base_set, t)
        if matched_phone:
            return "yes", matched_phone, col_name

    # If no valid base numbers to compare against, treat as match (skip)
    if not found_valid_base:
        return "yes", "", ""

    # Valid numbers were compared but no match found
    return "no", "", ""

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK
# =========================================================
def row_check(r):
    base_vals = {c: r.get(c) for c in PHONE_BASE_COLS}

    match_flag, matched_phone, matched_col = check_phone_against_many(
        r.get("customer_phone_number_unst_str"),
        base_vals
    )

    return pd.Series({
        "customer_contact_match": match_flag,           # "yes" or "no"
        "matched_phone":          matched_phone,         # actual matched number
        "matched_with_column":    matched_col            # base column name
    })


check_results = merged_df.apply(row_check, axis=1)
merged_df["customer_contact_match"] = check_results["customer_contact_match"]
merged_df["matched_phone"]          = check_results["matched_phone"]
merged_df["matched_with_column"]    = check_results["matched_with_column"]

# =========================================================
# SAFETY NET — force yes/no correctly when observed is invalid
# =========================================================
# This guarantees that regardless of anything above, any row where
# customer_phone_number_unst_str is invalid/NA becomes match="yes".
observed_is_invalid_mask = merged_df["customer_phone_number_unst_str"].apply(is_invalid)
merged_df.loc[observed_is_invalid_mask, "customer_contact_match"] = "yes"
merged_df.loc[observed_is_invalid_mask, "matched_phone"]          = ""
merged_df.loc[observed_is_invalid_mask, "matched_with_column"]    = ""

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(match_flag):
    # match=yes -> exception=no ;  match=no -> exception=yes
    return "no" if match_flag == "yes" else "yes"


def build_reason(match_flag, matched_phone, matched_col):
    if match_flag == "yes":
        if matched_phone:
            return (f"Customer phone number {matched_phone} matched with "
                    f"'{matched_col}'")
        return "Customer phone number is matching"
    return "Customer contact number is not matching with any of the phone numbers"


def build_additional_remarks(match_flag, matched_phone, matched_col):
    if match_flag == "yes":
        if matched_phone:
            return (f"Customer phone number from invoice ({matched_phone}) "
                    f"matched with '{matched_col}' in p_base_data")
        return "Customer phone number is matching"
    return ("Customer phone number from invoice did not match with any of: "
            "customer_contact, customer_registered_phone, "
            "customer_alternate_phone, customer_sr_raise_phone")


output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                                  CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                                CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                                now_ts,
    "updated_at":                                now_ts,
    "is_active":                                 merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                             merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                                 merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                                  merged_df["attch_id"],
    "category":                                  merged_df.get("category"),
    "customer_phone_number_observed_value":      merged_df.get("customer_phone_number_unst_str"),
    "customer_contact_expected_value":           merged_df.get("customer_contact"),
    "customer_registered_phone_expected_value":  merged_df.get("customer_registered_phone"),
    "customer_alternate_phone_expected_value":   merged_df.get("customer_alternate_phone"),
    "customer_sr_raise_phone_expected_value":    merged_df.get("customer_sr_raise_phone"),
    "customer_contact_match":                    merged_df["customer_contact_match"],
    "matched_with_column": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: (f"{r['matched_phone']} (in {r['matched_with_column']})"
                   if r["matched_phone"] else ""),
        axis=1
    ),
    "exception_flag": merged_df["customer_contact_match"].apply(build_exception_flag),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_reason(
            r["customer_contact_match"], r["matched_phone"], r["matched_with_column"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
    "additional_remarks": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_additional_remarks(
            r["customer_contact_match"], r["matched_phone"], r["matched_with_column"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
})


output_df['additional_remarks'] = 'NA'

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)


test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

# ==== Diagnostic prints (to confirm the fix works) ====
print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Match=yes (matched):    {(output_df['customer_contact_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Match=no  (not matched):{(output_df['customer_contact_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes:          {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no:           {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")

# Verify no "Not available" rows have exception=yes
na_but_flagged = output_df[
    output_df['customer_phone_number_observed_value'].apply(is_invalid) &
    (output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes')
]
print(f"Rows with observed=NA but exception=yes (should be 0): {len(na_but_flagged)}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "customer_phone_number_observed_value",
    "customer_contact_expected_value",
    "customer_registered_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_alternate_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_sr_raise_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_contact_match","matched_with_column",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols
               if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1003")

# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'

                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1002
CHECK_NAME  = "Dealer name and GST match with customer invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1002"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "dealer_name": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 3},
    "gstin":       {"ratio": 0.85, "max_edits": 2},
}

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA  (raw dataframes kept UNCHANGED)
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df_raw = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows (RAW): {len(unst_df_raw)}")   # should print 6802

# =========================================================
# CATEGORY LOOKUP  (attch_id -> category from base_df)
# built BEFORE any dedup so every attachment's category is captured
# =========================================================
CATEGORY_LOOKUP = {}
for _, _r in base_df.iterrows():
    _aid = _r.get("attch_id")
    _cat = _r.get("category")
    if _aid is None:
        continue
    _aid = str(_aid).strip()
    if _aid == "" or _aid in CATEGORY_LOOKUP:
        continue
    CATEGORY_LOOKUP[_aid] = ("" if _cat is None else str(_cat).strip())

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS  (work on a COPY, raw stays intact)
# NOTE: attch_id removed from JOIN_KEYS so attachments aggregate with ~
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df_raw.copy()
unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "not_available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found",
    "blank", "unknown", "missing",
    "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."
}

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES

def all_observed_missing(observed_str):
    """True only if EVERY ~-separated observed value is missing/not-available."""
    if observed_str is None:
        return True
    parts = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    return all(is_invalid(p) for p in parts)

def norm_alnum_upper(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())

def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s

BUSINESS_SUFFIXES = {
    "pvt", "private", "ltd", "limited", "llp", "inc", "co", "company",
    "corp", "corporation", "enterprises", "enterprise", "trader", "traders",
    "trading", "agency", "agencies", "sales", "services", "service",
    "and", "the", "of"
}

def norm_dealer_name(v):
    s = norm_text(v)
    if not s:
        return ""
    tokens = [t for t in s.split() if t not in BUSINESS_SUFFIXES]
    return " ".join(tokens)

def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()

def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)

def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False

# =========================================================
# POSITIONALLY-ALIGNED AGGREGATION
# (keeps 1 element per original row for EVERY column so
#  attch_id / dealer_name / dealer_gst remain aligned)
# =========================================================
def join_aligned(series):
    out = []
    for v in series.tolist():
        if v is None:
            out.append("Not available")
            continue
        try:
            if pd.isna(v):
                out.append("Not available")
                continue
        except Exception:
            pass
        s = str(v).strip()
        out.append(s if s != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(out)

unst_agg = unst_df.groupby(JOIN_KEYS, as_index=False).agg(join_aligned)

print(f"unst aggregated rows (per header_crm_id+sr_id): {len(unst_agg)}")

# =========================================================
# DEDUP BASE TO ONE ROW PER SR  (removes duplicate output rows)
# CRM expected values (dealer_name/dealer_gst) are per SR, so first is fine
# =========================================================
base_one_per_sr = base_df.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS, keep="first").copy()
print(f"base_df deduped to one row per SR: {len(base_one_per_sr)}")

# =========================================================
# MERGE  (one base row per SR  x  one unst row per SR)
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_one_per_sr,
    unst_agg.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE DEALER NAME CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_dealer_name_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                                      t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_dealer_name(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_dealer_name(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True
        score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a_norm, b_norm)  # 0-100
        if score >= t["ratio"] * 100 or edit_distance(a_norm, b_norm) <= t["max_edits"]:
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE GSTIN CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_gstin_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                               t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_alnum_upper(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_alnum_upper(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True

        if a_norm == b_norm:
            matched.append(attch)
        elif len(a_norm) < 12 or len(b_norm) < 12:
            mismatched.append(attch)
        elif fuzzy_match(a_norm, b_norm, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECKS  (use ALIGNED unst attch_id)
# =========================================================
name_temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_dealer_name_attachmentwise(
        r.get("dealer_name"),
        r.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    ),
    axis=1
)

gst_temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_gstin_attachmentwise(
        r.get("dealer_gst"),
        r.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["dealer_name_match"]          = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[0])
merged_df["dealer_name_matched_attch"]  = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["dealer_name_mismatch_attch"] = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

merged_df["dealer_gst_match"]           = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[0])
merged_df["dealer_gst_matched_attch"]   = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["dealer_gst_mismatch_attch"]  = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

# Output attch_id = aligned unst attach ids (fallback to base attch_id if unst missing)
def resolve_attch(r):
    u = r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("attch_id")

merged_df["attch_id_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_attch, axis=1)

# =========================================================
# CATEGORY (~ separated) built by mapping each attch_id -> category
# from the CATEGORY_LOOKUP (base_df).  This gives one category per
# attachment, perfectly aligned with attch_id_out.
# =========================================================
def build_category(attch_str):
    if attch_str is None or (isinstance(attch_str, float) and pd.isna(attch_str)):
        return None
    ids = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_str).split("~")]
    cats = []
    for aid in ids:
        cat = CATEGORY_LOOKUP.get(aid, "")
        cats.append(cat if cat != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(cats)

merged_df["category_out"] = merged_df["attch_id_out"].apply(build_category)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(name_match, gst_match):
    if name_match == "no" or gst_match == "no":
        return "yes"
    return "no"

# reason: priority -> not present in crm > was not extracted > matching/not matching
def build_reason(row):
    # ---------- DEALER NAME ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_name")):
        name_txt = "dealer name not present in crm"
    elif all_observed_missing(row.get("dealer_name_unst_str")):
        name_txt = "dealer name was not extracted"
    elif row["dealer_name_match"] == "yes":
        name_txt = "dealer name is matching"
    else:
        name_txt = "dealer name is not matching"

    # ---------- DEALER GST ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_gst")):
        gst_txt = "GST not present in crm"
    elif all_observed_missing(row.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str")):
        gst_txt = "GST was not extracted"
    elif row["dealer_gst_match"] == "yes":
        gst_txt = "GST number is matching"
    else:
        gst_txt = "GST number is not matching"

    return f"{name_txt}; {gst_txt}"

# additional_remarks: same priority as reason
def build_additional_remarks(row):
    parts = []

    # ---------- DEALER NAME ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_name")):
        parts.append("dealer_name not present in crm")
    elif all_observed_missing(row.get("dealer_name_unst_str")):
        parts.append("dealer_name was not extracted")
    elif row["dealer_name_match"] == "yes":
        parts.append(f"Dealer name matched with attachment(s): {row['dealer_name_matched_attch']}")
    else:
        parts.append(f"Dealer name mismatch in attachment(s): {row['dealer_name_mismatch_attch']}")

    # ---------- DEALER GST ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_gst")):
        parts.append("dealer_gst not present in crm")
    elif all_observed_missing(row.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str")):
        parts.append("dealer_gst was not extracted")
    elif row["dealer_gst_match"] == "yes":
        parts.append(f"GST matched with attachment(s): {row['dealer_gst_matched_attch']}")
    else:
        parts.append(f"GST mismatch in attachment(s): {row['dealer_gst_mismatch_attch']}")

    return " | ".join(parts)

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                       CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                     CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                     now_ts,
    "updated_at":                     now_ts,
    "is_active":                      merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                  merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                      merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                       merged_df["attch_id_out"],
    "category":                       merged_df["category_out"],
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value":    merged_df.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
    "dealer_gst_observed_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
    "dealer_name_expected_value":     merged_df.get("dealer_name"),
    "dealer_gst_expected_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst"),
    "dealer_name_match":              merged_df["dealer_name_match"],
    "dealer_gst_match":               merged_df["dealer_gst_match"],
    "exception_flag": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_exception_flag(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(build_reason, axis=1),
})

output_df["additional_remarks"] = merged_df.apply(build_additional_remarks, axis=1)

# =========================================================
# JOINT DEDUP: attch_id + category stay 1:1 aligned
# =========================================================
def dedup_attch_and_category(attch_val, cat_val):
    if pd.isna(attch_val) or attch_val is None:
        return attch_val, cat_val

    attch_list = str(attch_val).split("~")
    cat_list   = str(cat_val).split("~") if (cat_val is not None and not pd.isna(cat_val)) else []

    seen = set()
    out_attch, out_cat = [], []

    for idx, a in enumerate(attch_list):
        if a in seen:
            continue                      # duplicate attachment -> skip it AND its category
        seen.add(a)
        out_attch.append(a)
        if idx < len(cat_list):
            out_cat.append(cat_list[idx])

    return "~".join(out_attch), "~".join(out_cat)

_deduped = output_df.apply(
    lambda r: dedup_attch_and_category(r["attch_id"], r["category"]),
    axis=1
)
output_df["attch_id"] = _deduped.apply(lambda x: x[0])
output_df["category"] = _deduped.apply(lambda x: x[1])

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Name match=yes:  {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Name match=no:   {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=yes:   {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=no:    {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no (both match):            {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes (one or both mismatch): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value",
    "dealer_gst_observed_value",
    "dealer_name_expected_value",
    "dealer_gst_expected_value",
    "dealer_name_match","dealer_gst_match",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

CHECK_ID    = 1002
CHECK_NAME  = "Dealer name and GST match with customer invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1002"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "dealer_name": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 3},
    "gstin":       {"ratio": 0.85, "max_edits": 2},
}

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA  (raw dataframes kept UNCHANGED)
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df_raw = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows (RAW): {len(unst_df_raw)}")   # should print 6802

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS  (work on a COPY, raw stays intact)
# NOTE: attch_id removed from JOIN_KEYS so attachments aggregate with ~
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df_raw.copy()
unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "not_available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found",
    "blank", "unknown", "missing",
    "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."
}

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES

def all_observed_missing(observed_str):
    """True only if EVERY ~-separated observed value is missing/not-available."""
    if observed_str is None:
        return True
    parts = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    return all(is_invalid(p) for p in parts)

def norm_alnum_upper(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())

def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s

BUSINESS_SUFFIXES = {
    "pvt", "private", "ltd", "limited", "llp", "inc", "co", "company",
    "corp", "corporation", "enterprises", "enterprise", "trader", "traders",
    "trading", "agency", "agencies", "sales", "services", "service",
    "and", "the", "of"
}

def norm_dealer_name(v):
    s = norm_text(v)
    if not s:
        return ""
    tokens = [t for t in s.split() if t not in BUSINESS_SUFFIXES]
    return " ".join(tokens)

def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()

def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)

def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False

# =========================================================
# POSITIONALLY-ALIGNED AGGREGATION
# (keeps 1 element per original row for EVERY column so
#  attch_id / dealer_name / dealer_gst / category remain aligned)
# =========================================================
def join_aligned(series):
    out = []
    for v in series.tolist():
        if v is None:
            out.append("Not available")
            continue
        try:
            if pd.isna(v):
                out.append("Not available")
                continue
        except Exception:
            pass
        s = str(v).strip()
        out.append(s if s != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(out)

unst_agg = unst_df.groupby(JOIN_KEYS, as_index=False).agg(join_aligned)

print(f"unst aggregated rows (per header_crm_id+sr_id): {len(unst_agg)}")

# =========================================================
# MERGE  (base grain preserved)
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_agg.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE DEALER NAME CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_dealer_name_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                                      t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_dealer_name(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_dealer_name(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True
        score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a_norm, b_norm)  # 0-100
        if score >= t["ratio"] * 100 or edit_distance(a_norm, b_norm) <= t["max_edits"]:
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE GSTIN CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_gstin_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                               t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_alnum_upper(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_alnum_upper(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True

        if a_norm == b_norm:
            matched.append(attch)
        elif len(a_norm) < 12 or len(b_norm) < 12:
            mismatched.append(attch)
        elif fuzzy_match(a_norm, b_norm, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECKS  (use ALIGNED unst attch_id)
# =========================================================
name_temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_dealer_name_attachmentwise(
        r.get("dealer_name"),
        r.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    ),
    axis=1
)

gst_temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_gstin_attachmentwise(
        r.get("dealer_gst"),
        r.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["dealer_name_match"]          = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[0])
merged_df["dealer_name_matched_attch"]  = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["dealer_name_mismatch_attch"] = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

merged_df["dealer_gst_match"]           = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[0])
merged_df["dealer_gst_matched_attch"]   = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["dealer_gst_mismatch_attch"]  = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

# Output attch_id = aligned unst attach ids (fallback to base attch_id if unst missing)
def resolve_attch(r):
    u = r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("attch_id")

merged_df["attch_id_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_attch, axis=1)

# category = ~ separated per-attachment (from unst), fallback to base
def resolve_category(r):
    u = r.get("category_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("category")

merged_df["category_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_category, axis=1)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(name_match, gst_match):
    # Exception = "yes" if EITHER name or GST does NOT match
    if name_match == "no" or gst_match == "no":
        return "yes"
    return "no"

# reason: priority -> not present in crm > was not extracted > matching/not matching
def build_reason(row):
    # ---------- DEALER NAME ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_name")):                       # CRM missing -> highest priority
        name_txt = "dealer name not present in crm"
    elif all_observed_missing(row.get("dealer_name_unst_str")):  # observed not extracted
        name_txt = "dealer name was not extracted"
    elif row["dealer_name_match"] == "yes":
        name_txt = "dealer name is matching"
    else:
        name_txt = "dealer name is not matching"

    # ---------- DEALER GST ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_gst")):                        # CRM missing -> highest priority
        gst_txt = "GST not present in crm"
    elif all_observed_missing(row.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str")):
        gst_txt = "GST was not extracted"
    elif row["dealer_gst_match"] == "yes":
        gst_txt = "GST number is matching"
    else:
        gst_txt = "GST number is not matching"

    return f"{name_txt}; {gst_txt}"

# additional_remarks: same priority as reason
def build_additional_remarks(row):
    parts = []

    # ---------- DEALER NAME ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_name")):                       # CRM missing -> highest priority
        parts.append("dealer_name not present in crm")
    elif all_observed_missing(row.get("dealer_name_unst_str")):  # observed not extracted
        parts.append("dealer_name was not extracted")
    elif row["dealer_name_match"] == "yes":
        parts.append(f"Dealer name matched with attachment(s): {row['dealer_name_matched_attch']}")
    else:
        parts.append(f"Dealer name mismatch in attachment(s): {row['dealer_name_mismatch_attch']}")

    # ---------- DEALER GST ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_gst")):                        # CRM missing -> highest priority
        parts.append("dealer_gst not present in crm")
    elif all_observed_missing(row.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str")):
        parts.append("dealer_gst was not extracted")
    elif row["dealer_gst_match"] == "yes":
        parts.append(f"GST matched with attachment(s): {row['dealer_gst_matched_attch']}")
    else:
        parts.append(f"GST mismatch in attachment(s): {row['dealer_gst_mismatch_attch']}")

    return " | ".join(parts)

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                       CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                     CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                     now_ts,
    "updated_at":                     now_ts,
    "is_active":                      merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                  merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                      merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                       merged_df["attch_id_out"],
    "category":                       merged_df["category_out"],
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value":    merged_df.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
    "dealer_gst_observed_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
    "dealer_name_expected_value":     merged_df.get("dealer_name"),
    "dealer_gst_expected_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst"),
    "dealer_name_match":              merged_df["dealer_name_match"],
    "dealer_gst_match":               merged_df["dealer_gst_match"],
    "exception_flag": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_exception_flag(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(build_reason, axis=1),
})

output_df["additional_remarks"] = merged_df.apply(build_additional_remarks, axis=1)

# =========================================================
# JOINT DEDUP: attch_id + category stay 1:1 aligned
# =========================================================
def dedup_attch_and_category(attch_val, cat_val):
    """
    Dedup attch_id by first occurrence; drop the category element
    at the SAME position so attch_id and category stay 1:1 aligned.
    """
    if pd.isna(attch_val) or attch_val is None:
        return attch_val, cat_val

    attch_list = str(attch_val).split("~")
    cat_list   = str(cat_val).split("~") if (cat_val is not None and not pd.isna(cat_val)) else []

    seen = set()
    out_attch, out_cat = [], []

    for idx, a in enumerate(attch_list):
        if a in seen:
            continue                      # duplicate attachment -> skip it AND its category
        seen.add(a)
        out_attch.append(a)
        if idx < len(cat_list):
            out_cat.append(cat_list[idx])

    return "~".join(out_attch), "~".join(out_cat)

_deduped = output_df.apply(
    lambda r: dedup_attch_and_category(r["attch_id"], r["category"]),
    axis=1
)
output_df["attch_id"] = _deduped.apply(lambda x: x[0])
output_df["category"] = _deduped.apply(lambda x: x[1])

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Name match=yes:  {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Name match=no:   {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=yes:   {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=no:    {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no (both match):            {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes (one or both mismatch): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   updated_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id TEXT,
#   category TEXT,
#   dealer_name_obeserved_value TEXT,
#   dealer_gst_observed_value TEXT,
#   dealer_name_expected_value TEXT,
#   dealer_gst_expected_value TEXT,
#   dealer_name_match VARCHAR(10),
#   dealer_gst_match VARCHAR(10),
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   reason TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id(255))
# )
# """
# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value",
    "dealer_gst_observed_value",
    "dealer_name_expected_value",
    "dealer_gst_expected_value",
    "dealer_name_match","dealer_gst_match",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1002")

def dedup_attch_and_category(attch_val, cat_val):
    """
    Dedup attch_id by first occurrence; drop the category element
    at the SAME position so attch_id and category stay 1:1 aligned.
    """
    if pd.isna(attch_val) or attch_val is None:
        return attch_val, cat_val

    attch_list = str(attch_val).split("~")
    cat_list   = str(cat_val).split("~") if (cat_val is not None and not pd.isna(cat_val)) else []

    seen = set()
    out_attch, out_cat = [], []

    for idx, a in enumerate(attch_list):
        if a in seen:
            continue                      # duplicate attachment -> skip it AND its category
        seen.add(a)
        out_attch.append(a)
        if idx < len(cat_list):
            out_cat.append(cat_list[idx])

    return "~".join(out_attch), "~".join(out_cat)

# Apply joint dedup so attch_id and category stay aligned
_deduped = output_df.apply(
    lambda r: dedup_attch_and_category(r["attch_id"], r["category"]),
    axis=1
)
output_df["attch_id"] = _deduped.apply(lambda x: x[0])
output_df["category"] = _deduped.apply(lambda x: x[1])
