import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1002
CHECK_NAME  = "Dealer name and GST match with customer invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1002"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "dealer_name": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 3},
    "gstin":       {"ratio": 0.85, "max_edits": 2},
}

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA  (raw dataframes kept UNCHANGED)
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df_raw = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows (RAW): {len(unst_df_raw)}")   # should print 6802

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS  (work on a COPY, raw stays intact)
# NOTE: attch_id removed from JOIN_KEYS so attachments aggregate with ~
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df_raw.copy()
unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "not_available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found",
    "blank", "unknown", "missing",
    "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."
}

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES

# ----- NEW: split "missing" into two categories -----
NONE_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan"}                 # truly absent -> not present in crm
NOT_EXTRACTED_TOKENS = {"not available", "not_available",  # present but OCR/CRM couldn't read
                        "not found", "na", "n/a", "error",
                        "blank", "unknown", "missing",
                        "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."}

def is_none_val(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NONE_TOKENS

def is_not_extracted(v):
    if v is None:
        return False
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return False
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NOT_EXTRACTED_TOKENS

def norm_alnum_upper(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())

def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s

BUSINESS_SUFFIXES = {
    "pvt", "private", "ltd", "limited", "llp", "inc", "co", "company",
    "corp", "corporation", "enterprises", "enterprise", "trader", "traders",
    "trading", "agency", "agencies", "sales", "services", "service",
    "and", "the", "of"
}

def norm_dealer_name(v):
    s = norm_text(v)
    if not s:
        return ""
    tokens = [t for t in s.split() if t not in BUSINESS_SUFFIXES]
    return " ".join(tokens)

def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()

def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)

def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False

# =========================================================
# POSITIONALLY-ALIGNED AGGREGATION
# (keeps 1 element per original row for EVERY column so
#  attch_id / dealer_name / dealer_gst / category remain aligned)
# =========================================================
def join_aligned(series):
    out = []
    for v in series.tolist():
        if v is None:
            out.append("Not available")
            continue
        try:
            if pd.isna(v):
                out.append("Not available")
                continue
        except Exception:
            pass
        s = str(v).strip()
        out.append(s if s != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(out)

unst_agg = unst_df.groupby(JOIN_KEYS, as_index=False).agg(join_aligned)

print(f"unst aggregated rows (per header_crm_id+sr_id): {len(unst_agg)}")

# =========================================================
# MERGE  (base grain preserved)
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_agg.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE DEALER NAME CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_dealer_name_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                                      t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_dealer_name(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_dealer_name(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True
        score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a_norm, b_norm)  # 0-100
        if score >= t["ratio"] * 100 or edit_distance(a_norm, b_norm) <= t["max_edits"]:
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE GSTIN CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_gstin_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                               t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_alnum_upper(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_alnum_upper(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True

        if a_norm == b_norm:
            matched.append(attch)
        elif len(a_norm) < 12 or len(b_norm) < 12:
            mismatched.append(attch)
        elif fuzzy_match(a_norm, b_norm, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECKS  (use ALIGNED unst attch_id)
# =========================================================
name_temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_dealer_name_attachmentwise(
        r.get("dealer_name"),
        r.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    ),
    axis=1
)

gst_temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_gstin_attachmentwise(
        r.get("dealer_gst"),
        r.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["dealer_name_match"]          = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[0])
merged_df["dealer_name_matched_attch"]  = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["dealer_name_mismatch_attch"] = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

merged_df["dealer_gst_match"]           = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[0])
merged_df["dealer_gst_matched_attch"]   = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["dealer_gst_mismatch_attch"]  = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

# Output attch_id = aligned unst attach ids (fallback to base attch_id if unst missing)
def resolve_attch(r):
    u = r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("attch_id")

merged_df["attch_id_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_attch, axis=1)

# ----- NEW: category = ~ separated per-attachment (from unst), fallback to base -----
def resolve_category(r):
    u = r.get("category_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("category")

merged_df["category_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_category, axis=1)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(name_match, gst_match):
    # Exception = "yes" if EITHER name or GST does NOT match
    if name_match == "no" or gst_match == "no":
        return "yes"
    return "no"

# ----- UPDATED reason: distinguish None (not in crm) vs not-available (not extracted) -----
def build_reason(row):
    # ---------- DEALER NAME ----------
    if is_none_val(row.get("dealer_name")):
        name_txt = "dealer name not present in crm"
    elif is_not_extracted(row.get("dealer_name")):
        name_txt = "dealer name not extracted"
    elif row["dealer_name_match"] == "yes":
        name_txt = "dealer name is matching"
    else:
        name_txt = "dealer name is not matching"

    # ---------- DEALER GST ----------
    if is_none_val(row.get("dealer_gst")):
        gst_txt = "GST not present in crm"
    elif is_not_extracted(row.get("dealer_gst")):
        gst_txt = "GST not extracted"
    elif row["dealer_gst_match"] == "yes":
        gst_txt = "GST number is matching"
    else:
        gst_txt = "GST number is not matching"

    return f"{name_txt}; {gst_txt}"

def build_additional_remarks(row):
    parts = []

    # ---------- DEALER NAME ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_name")):          # expected value (CRM) missing
        parts.append("dealer_name not present in crm")
    elif row["dealer_name_match"] == "yes":
        if row["dealer_name_matched_attch"]:
            parts.append(f"Dealer name matched with attachment(s): {row['dealer_name_matched_attch']}")
        else:
            parts.append("Dealer was not extracted")
    else:
        parts.append(f"Dealer name mismatch in attachment(s): {row['dealer_name_mismatch_attch']}")

    # ---------- DEALER GST ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_gst")):           # expected value (CRM) missing
        parts.append("dealer_gst not present in crm")
    elif row["dealer_gst_match"] == "yes":
        if row["dealer_gst_matched_attch"]:
            parts.append(f"GST matched with attachment(s): {row['dealer_gst_matched_attch']}")
        else:
            parts.append("GST was not extracted")
    else:
        parts.append(f"GST mismatch in attachment(s): {row['dealer_gst_mismatch_attch']}")

    return " | ".join(parts)

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                       CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                     CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                     now_ts,
    "updated_at":                     now_ts,
    "is_active":                      merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                  merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                      merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                       merged_df["attch_id_out"],
    "category":                       merged_df["category_out"],      # <-- ~ separated per attachment
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value":    merged_df.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
    "dealer_gst_observed_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
    "dealer_name_expected_value":     merged_df.get("dealer_name"),
    "dealer_gst_expected_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst"),
    "dealer_name_match":              merged_df["dealer_name_match"],
    "dealer_gst_match":               merged_df["dealer_gst_match"],
    "exception_flag": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_exception_flag(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(build_reason, axis=1),                  # <-- updated reason
})

output_df["additional_remarks"] = merged_df.apply(build_additional_remarks, axis=1)

def remove_duplicate_attch_ids(val):
    if pd.isna(val):
        return val
    return "~".join(dict.fromkeys(str(val).split("~")))

output_df["attch_id"] = output_df["attch_id"].apply(remove_duplicate_attch_ids)

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Name match=yes:  {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Name match=no:   {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=yes:   {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=no:    {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no (both match):            {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes (one or both mismatch): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,

#   reason TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id(255))
# )
# """
# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value",
    "dealer_gst_observed_value",
    "dealer_name_expected_value",
    "dealer_gst_expected_value",
    "dealer_name_match","dealer_gst_match",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetimes
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1002
CHECK_NAME  = "Dealer name and GST match with customer invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1002"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "dealer_name": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 3},
    "gstin":       {"ratio": 0.85, "max_edits": 2},
}

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA  (raw dataframes kept UNCHANGED)
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df_raw = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows (RAW): {len(unst_df_raw)}")   # should print 6802

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS  (work on a COPY, raw stays intact)
# NOTE: attch_id removed from JOIN_KEYS so attachments aggregate with ~
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df_raw.copy()
unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "not_available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found",
    "blank", "unknown", "missing",
    "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."
}

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES

def norm_alnum_upper(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())

def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s

BUSINESS_SUFFIXES = {
    "pvt", "private", "ltd", "limited", "llp", "inc", "co", "company",
    "corp", "corporation", "enterprises", "enterprise", "trader", "traders",
    "trading", "agency", "agencies", "sales", "services", "service",
    "and", "the", "of"
}

def norm_dealer_name(v):
    s = norm_text(v)
    if not s:
        return ""
    tokens = [t for t in s.split() if t not in BUSINESS_SUFFIXES]
    return " ".join(tokens)

def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()

def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)

def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False

# =========================================================
# POSITIONALLY-ALIGNED AGGREGATION
# (keeps 1 element per original row for EVERY column so
#  attch_id / dealer_name / dealer_gst remain aligned)
# =========================================================
def join_aligned(series):
    out = []
    for v in series.tolist():
        if v is None:
            out.append("Not available")
            continue
        try:
            if pd.isna(v):
                out.append("Not available")
                continue
        except Exception:
            pass
        s = str(v).strip()
        out.append(s if s != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(out)

unst_agg = unst_df.groupby(JOIN_KEYS, as_index=False).agg(join_aligned)

print(f"unst aggregated rows (per header_crm_id+sr_id): {len(unst_agg)}")

# =========================================================
# MERGE  (base grain preserved)
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_agg.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE DEALER NAME CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_dealer_name_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                                      t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
    """
    Match if ANY observed dealer name matches expected.
      - expected invalid / not available            -> MATCH
      - all observed invalid / not available         -> MATCH
      - any valid observed matches                   -> MATCH (report attch_id)
      - valid observed present but none match         -> MISMATCH (report attch_id)
    Returns: flag('yes'/'no'), matched_attchs, mismatch_attchs
    """
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_dealer_name(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_dealer_name(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True
        score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a_norm, b_norm)  # 0-100
        if score >= t["ratio"] * 100 or edit_distance(a_norm, b_norm) <= t["max_edits"]:
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE GSTIN CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_gstin_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                               t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):
    """
    Match if ANY observed GST matches expected.
    Same match/skip rules as dealer name.
    Returns: flag('yes'/'no'), matched_attchs, mismatch_attchs
    """
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_alnum_upper(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_alnum_upper(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True

        if a_norm == b_norm:
            matched.append(attch)
        elif len(a_norm) < 12 or len(b_norm) < 12:
            mismatched.append(attch)
        elif fuzzy_match(a_norm, b_norm, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECKS  (use ALIGNED unst attch_id)
# =========================================================
name_temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_dealer_name_attachmentwise(
        r.get("dealer_name"),
        r.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    ),
    axis=1
)

gst_temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_gstin_attachmentwise(
        r.get("dealer_gst"),
        r.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["dealer_name_match"]          = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[0])
merged_df["dealer_name_matched_attch"]  = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["dealer_name_mismatch_attch"] = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

merged_df["dealer_gst_match"]           = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[0])
merged_df["dealer_gst_matched_attch"]   = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["dealer_gst_mismatch_attch"]  = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

# Output attch_id = aligned unst attach ids (fallback to base attch_id if unst missing)
def resolve_attch(r):
    u = r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("attch_id")

merged_df["attch_id_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_attch, axis=1)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(name_match, gst_match):
    # Exception = "yes" if EITHER name or GST does NOT match
    if name_match == "no" or gst_match == "no":
        return "yes"
    return "no"

def build_reason(name_match, gst_match):
    name_txt = "dealer name is matching" if name_match == "yes" else "dealer name is not matching"
    gst_txt  = "GST number is matching"  if gst_match  == "yes" else "GST number is not matching"
    return f"{name_txt}; {gst_txt}"

def build_additional_remarks(row):
    parts = []

    # ---------- DEALER NAME ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_name")):          # expected value (CRM) missing
        parts.append("dealer_name not present in crm")
    elif row["dealer_name_match"] == "yes":
        if row["dealer_name_matched_attch"]:
            parts.append(f"Dealer name matched with attachment(s): {row['dealer_name_matched_attch']}")
        else:
            parts.append("Dealer was not extracted")
    else:
        parts.append(f"Dealer name mismatch in attachment(s): {row['dealer_name_mismatch_attch']}")

    # ---------- DEALER GST ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_gst")):           # expected value (CRM) missing
        parts.append("dealer_gst not present in crm")
    elif row["dealer_gst_match"] == "yes":
        if row["dealer_gst_matched_attch"]:
            parts.append(f"GST matched with attachment(s): {row['dealer_gst_matched_attch']}")
        else:
            parts.append("GST was not extracted")
    else:
        parts.append(f"GST mismatch in attachment(s): {row['dealer_gst_mismatch_attch']}")

    return " | ".join(parts)

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                       CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                     CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                     now_ts,
    "updated_at":                     now_ts,
    "is_active":                      merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                  merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                      merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                       merged_df["attch_id_out"],
    "category":                       merged_df.get("category"),
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value":    merged_df.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
    "dealer_gst_observed_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
    "dealer_name_expected_value":     merged_df.get("dealer_name"),
    "dealer_gst_expected_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst"),
    "dealer_name_match":              merged_df["dealer_name_match"],
    "dealer_gst_match":               merged_df["dealer_gst_match"],
    "exception_flag": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_exception_flag(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_reason(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
})

output_df["additional_remarks"] = merged_df.apply(build_additional_remarks, axis=1)

def remove_duplicate_attch_ids(val):
    if pd.isna(val):
        return val
    return "~".join(dict.fromkeys(str(val).split("~")))

output_df["attch_id"] = output_df["attch_id"].apply(remove_duplicate_attch_ids)

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)




test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Name match=yes:  {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Name match=no:   {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=yes:   {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=no:    {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no (both match):            {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes (one or both mismatch): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   updated_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id TEXT,
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   dealer_name_obeserved_value TEXT,
#   dealer_gst_observed_value TEXT,
#   dealer_name_expected_value TEXT,
#   dealer_gst_expected_value TEXT,
#   dealer_name_match VARCHAR(10),
#   dealer_gst_match VARCHAR(10),
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   reason TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id(255))
# )
# """
# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value",
    "dealer_gst_observed_value",
    "dealer_name_expected_value",
    "dealer_gst_expected_value",
    "dealer_name_match","dealer_gst_match",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1002")

from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'

                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1002
CHECK_NAME  = "Dealer name and GST match with customer invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1002"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "dealer_name": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 3},
    "gstin":       {"ratio": 0.85, "max_edits": 2},
}

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA  (raw dataframes kept UNCHANGED)
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df_raw = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows (RAW): {len(unst_df_raw)}")   # should print 6802

# =========================================================

unst_df = unst_df_raw.copy()

    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "not_available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found",
    "blank", "unknown", "missing",
    "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."
}

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES

def norm_alnum_upper(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())

def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s

BUSINESS_SUFFIXES = {
    "pvt", "private", "ltd", "limited", "llp", "inc", "co", "company",
    "corp", "corporation", "enterprises", "enterprise", "trader", "traders",
    "trading", "agency", "agencies", "sales", "services", "service",
    "and", "the", "of"
}

def norm_dealer_name(v):
    s = norm_text(v)
    if not s:
        return ""
    tokens = [t for t in s.split() if t not in BUSINESS_SUFFIXES]
    return " ".join(tokens)

def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()

def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)

def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False

# =========================================================
# POSITIONALLY-ALIGNED AGGREGATION
# (keeps 1 element per original row for EVERY column so
#  attch_id / dealer_name / dealer_gst remain aligned)
# =========================================================
def join_aligned(series):
    out = []
    for v in series.tolist():
        if v is None:
            out.append("Not available")
            continue
        try:
            if pd.isna(v):
                out.append("Not available")
                continue
        except Exception:
            pass
        s = str(v).strip()
        out.append(s if s != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(out)

unst_agg = unst_df.groupby(JOIN_KEYS, as_index=False).agg(join_aligned)

print(f"unst aggregated rows (per header_crm_id+sr_id): {len(unst_agg)}")

merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_agg.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE DEALER NAME CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_dealer_name_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                                      t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
    """
    Match if ANY observed dealer name matches expected.
      - expected invalid / not available            -> MATCH
      - all observed invalid / not available         -> MATCH
      - any valid observed matches                   -> MATCH (report attch_id)
      - valid observed present but none match         -> MISMATCH (report attch_id)
    Returns: flag('yes'/'no'), matched_attchs, mismatch_attchs
    """
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_dealer_name(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_dealer_name(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True
        score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a_norm, b_norm)  # 0-100
        if score >= t["ratio"] * 100 or edit_distance(a_norm, b_norm) <= t["max_edits"]:
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE GSTIN CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_gstin_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                               t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):
    """
    Match if ANY observed GST matches expected.
    Same match/skip rules as dealer name.
    Returns: flag('yes'/'no'), matched_attchs, mismatch_attchs
    """
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_alnum_upper(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_alnum_upper(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True

        if a_norm == b_norm:
            matched.append(attch)
        elif len(a_norm) < 12 or len(b_norm) < 12:
            mismatched.append(attch)
        elif fuzzy_match(a_norm, b_norm, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECKS  (use ALIGNED unst attch_id)
# =========================================================
name_temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_dealer_name_attachmentwise(
        r.get("dealer_name"),
        r.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    ),
    axis=1
)

gst_temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_gstin_attachmentwise(
        r.get("dealer_gst"),
        r.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["dealer_name_match"]          = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[0])
merged_df["dealer_name_matched_attch"]  = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["dealer_name_mismatch_attch"] = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

merged_df["dealer_gst_match"]           = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[0])
merged_df["dealer_gst_matched_attch"]   = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["dealer_gst_mismatch_attch"]  = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

# Output attch_id = aligned unst attach ids (fallback to base attch_id if unst missing)
def resolve_attch(r):
    u = r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("attch_id")

merged_df["attch_id_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_attch, axis=1)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(name_match, gst_match):
    # Exception = "yes" if EITHER name or GST does NOT match
    if name_match == "no" or gst_match == "no":
        return "yes"
    return "no"

def build_reason(name_match, gst_match):
    name_txt = "dealer name is matching" if name_match == "yes" else "dealer name is not matching"
    gst_txt  = "GST number is matching"  if gst_match  == "yes" else "GST number is not matching"
    return f"{name_txt}; {gst_txt}"

def build_additional_remarks(row):
    parts = []

    # ---------- DEALER NAME ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_name")):          # expected value (CRM) missing
        parts.append("dealer_name not present in crm")
    elif row["dealer_name_match"] == "yes":
        if row["dealer_name_matched_attch"]:
            parts.append(f"Dealer name matched with attachment(s): {row['dealer_name_matched_attch']}")
        else:
            parts.append("Dealer name not available; treated as match")
    else:
        parts.append(f"Dealer name mismatch in attachment(s): {row['dealer_name_mismatch_attch']}")

    # ---------- DEALER GST ----------
    if is_invalid(row.get("dealer_gst")):           # expected value (CRM) missing
        parts.append("dealer_gst not present in crm")
    elif row["dealer_gst_match"] == "yes":
        if row["dealer_gst_matched_attch"]:
            parts.append(f"GST matched with attachment(s): {row['dealer_gst_matched_attch']}")
        else:
            parts.append("GST not available; treated as match")
    else:
        parts.append(f"GST mismatch in attachment(s): {row['dealer_gst_mismatch_attch']}")

    return " | ".join(parts)

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                       CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                     CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                     now_ts,
    "updated_at":                     now_ts,
    "is_active":                      merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                  merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                      merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                       merged_df["attch_id_out"],
    "category":                       merged_df.get("category"),
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value":    merged_df.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
    "dealer_gst_observed_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
    "dealer_name_expected_value":     merged_df.get("dealer_name"),
    "dealer_gst_expected_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst"),
    "dealer_name_match":              merged_df["dealer_name_match"],
    "dealer_gst_match":               merged_df["dealer_gst_match"],
    "exception_flag": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_exception_flag(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_reason(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
})

output_df["additional_remarks"] = merged_df.apply(build_additional_remarks, axis=1)

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Name match=yes:  {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Name match=no:   {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=yes:   {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=no:    {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no (both match):            {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes (one or both mismatch): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   updated_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id TEXT,
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   dealer_name_obeserved_value TEXT,
#   dealer_gst_observed_value TEXT,
#   dealer_name_expected_value TEXT,
#   dealer_gst_expected_value TEXT,
#   dealer_name_match VARCHAR(10),
#   dealer_gst_match VARCHAR(10),
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   reason TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id(255))
# )
# """
# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value",
    "dealer_gst_observed_value",
    "dealer_name_expected_value",
    "dealer_gst_expected_value",
    "dealer_name_match","dealer_gst_match",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1002")























===========================================================================================================

import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1002
CHECK_NAME  = "Dealer name and GST match with customer invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1002"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "dealer_name": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 3},
    "gstin":       {"ratio": 0.85, "max_edits": 2},
}

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA  (raw dataframes kept UNCHANGED)
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df_raw = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows (RAW): {len(unst_df_raw)}")   # should print 6802

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS  (work on a COPY, raw stays intact)
# NOTE: attch_id removed from JOIN_KEYS so attachments aggregate with ~
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df_raw.copy()
unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "not_available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found",
    "blank", "unknown", "missing",
    "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."
}

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES

def norm_alnum_upper(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())

def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s

BUSINESS_SUFFIXES = {
    "pvt", "private", "ltd", "limited", "llp", "inc", "co", "company",
    "corp", "corporation", "enterprises", "enterprise", "trader", "traders",
    "trading", "agency", "agencies", "sales", "services", "service",
    "and", "the", "of"
}

def norm_dealer_name(v):
    s = norm_text(v)
    if not s:
        return ""
    tokens = [t for t in s.split() if t not in BUSINESS_SUFFIXES]
    return " ".join(tokens)

def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()

def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)

def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False

# =========================================================
# POSITIONALLY-ALIGNED AGGREGATION
# (keeps 1 element per original row for EVERY column so
#  attch_id / dealer_name / dealer_gst remain aligned)
# =========================================================
def join_aligned(series):
    out = []
    for v in series.tolist():
        if v is None:
            out.append("Not available")
            continue
        try:
            if pd.isna(v):
                out.append("Not available")
                continue
        except Exception:
            pass
        s = str(v).strip()
        out.append(s if s != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(out)

unst_agg = unst_df.groupby(JOIN_KEYS, as_index=False).agg(join_aligned)

print(f"unst aggregated rows (per header_crm_id+sr_id): {len(unst_agg)}")

# =========================================================
# MERGE  (base grain preserved)
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_agg.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE DEALER NAME CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_dealer_name_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                                      t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
    """
    Match if ANY observed dealer name matches expected.
      - expected invalid / not available            -> MATCH
      - all observed invalid / not available         -> MATCH
      - any valid observed matches                   -> MATCH (report attch_id)
      - valid observed present but none match         -> MISMATCH (report attch_id)
    Returns: flag('yes'/'no'), matched_attchs, mismatch_attchs
    """
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_dealer_name(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_dealer_name(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True
        score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a_norm, b_norm)  # 0-100
        if score >= t["ratio"] * 100 or edit_distance(a_norm, b_norm) <= t["max_edits"]:
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE GSTIN CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_gstin_attachmentwise(expected, observed_str, attch_ids,
                               t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):
    """
    Match if ANY observed GST matches expected.
    Same match/skip rules as dealer name.
    Returns: flag('yes'/'no'), matched_attchs, mismatch_attchs
    """
    if is_invalid(expected):
        return "yes", "", ""

    a_norm = norm_alnum_upper(expected)
    if not a_norm:
        return "yes", "", ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_str).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched, mismatched = [], []
    valid_seen = False

    for idx, obs in enumerate(obs_list):
        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else (attch_list[-1] if attch_list else "")

        if is_invalid(obs):
            continue

        b_norm = norm_alnum_upper(obs)
        if not b_norm:
            continue

        valid_seen = True

        if a_norm == b_norm:
            matched.append(attch)
        elif len(a_norm) < 12 or len(b_norm) < 12:
            mismatched.append(attch)
        elif fuzzy_match(a_norm, b_norm, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
            matched.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatched.append(attch)

    matched    = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched if a]))
    mismatched = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatched if a]))

    if not valid_seen:
        return "yes", "", ""
    if matched:
        return "yes", ",".join(matched), ""
    return "no", "", ",".join(mismatched)

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECKS  (use ALIGNED unst attch_id)
# =========================================================
name_temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_dealer_name_attachmentwise(
        r.get("dealer_name"),
        r.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    ),
    axis=1
)

gst_temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_gstin_attachmentwise(
        r.get("dealer_gst"),
        r.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["dealer_name_match"]          = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[0])
merged_df["dealer_name_matched_attch"]  = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["dealer_name_mismatch_attch"] = name_temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

merged_df["dealer_gst_match"]           = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[0])
merged_df["dealer_gst_matched_attch"]   = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["dealer_gst_mismatch_attch"]  = gst_temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

# Output attch_id = aligned unst attach ids (fallback to base attch_id if unst missing)
def resolve_attch(r):
    u = r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("attch_id")

merged_df["attch_id_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_attch, axis=1)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(name_match, gst_match):
    # Exception = "yes" if EITHER name or GST does NOT match
    if name_match == "no" or gst_match == "no":
        return "yes"
    return "no"

def build_reason(name_match, gst_match):
    name_txt = "dealer name is matching" if name_match == "yes" else "dealer name is not matching"
    gst_txt  = "GST number is matching"  if gst_match  == "yes" else "GST number is not matching"
    return f"{name_txt}; {gst_txt}"

def build_additional_remarks(row):
    parts = []

    # Dealer name part
    if row["dealer_name_match"] == "yes":
        if row["dealer_name_matched_attch"]:
            parts.append(f"Dealer name matched with attachment(s): {row['dealer_name_matched_attch']}")
        else:
            parts.append("Dealer name not available; treated as match")
    else:
        parts.append(f"Dealer name mismatch in attachment(s): {row['dealer_name_mismatch_attch']}")

    # GST part
    if row["dealer_gst_match"] == "yes":
        if row["dealer_gst_matched_attch"]:
            parts.append(f"GST matched with attachment(s): {row['dealer_gst_matched_attch']}")
        else:
            parts.append("GST not available; treated as match")
    else:
        parts.append(f"GST mismatch in attachment(s): {row['dealer_gst_mismatch_attch']}")

    return " | ".join(parts)

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                       CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                     CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                     now_ts,
    "updated_at":                     now_ts,
    "is_active":                      merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                  merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                      merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                       merged_df["attch_id_out"],
    "category":                       merged_df.get("category"),
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value":    merged_df.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
    "dealer_gst_observed_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
    "dealer_name_expected_value":     merged_df.get("dealer_name"),
    "dealer_gst_expected_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst"),
    "dealer_name_match":              merged_df["dealer_name_match"],
    "dealer_gst_match":               merged_df["dealer_gst_match"],
    "exception_flag": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_exception_flag(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_reason(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
})

output_df["additional_remarks"] = merged_df.apply(build_additional_remarks, axis=1)

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Name match=yes:  {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Name match=no:   {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=yes:   {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=no:    {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no (both match):            {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes (one or both mismatch): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   updated_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id TEXT,
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   dealer_name_obeserved_value TEXT,
#   dealer_gst_observed_value TEXT,
#   dealer_name_expected_value TEXT,
#   dealer_gst_expected_value TEXT,
#   dealer_name_match VARCHAR(10),
#   dealer_gst_match VARCHAR(10),
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   reason TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id(255))
# )
# """
# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value",
    "dealer_gst_observed_value",
    "dealer_name_expected_value",
    "dealer_gst_expected_value",
    "dealer_name_match","dealer_gst_match",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1002")

import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()
# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1002
CHECK_NAME  = "Dealer name and GST match with customer invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1002"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "dealer_name": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 3},
    "gstin":       {"ratio": 0.85, "max_edits": 2},
}

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows: {len(unst_df)}")

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id", "attch_id"]

unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# MERGE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(base_df, unst_df.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS), on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left")
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "error", "na", "n/a"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS


def norm_alnum_upper(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())


def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s


BUSINESS_SUFFIXES = {
    "pvt", "private", "ltd", "limited", "llp", "inc", "co", "company",
    "corp", "corporation", "enterprises", "enterprise", "trader", "traders",
    "trading", "agency", "agencies", "sales", "services", "service",
    "and", "the", "of"
}

def norm_dealer_name(v):
    s = norm_text(v)
    if not s:
        return ""
    tokens = [t for t in s.split() if t not in BUSINESS_SUFFIXES]
    return " ".join(tokens)


def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()


def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)


def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False


# def check_dealer_name(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
#     a, b = norm_dealer_name(a), norm_dealer_name(b)
#     if not a or not b:
#         return 0
#     score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a, b)            # 0-100
#     if score >= t["ratio"] * 100:
#         return 1
#     return int(edit_distance(a, b) <= t["max_edits"])


# def check_gstin(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):

#     if not a or not b:
#         return 0
#     if a == b:
#         return 1
#     if len(a) < 12 or len(b) < 12:
#         return 0
#     return int(fuzzy_match(a, b, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]))

INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found",
    "blank", "unknown", "missing",
    "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."
}

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES


def check_dealer_name(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
    """
    a = dealer_name (expected / p_base_data)
    b = dealer_name_unst_str (observed / invoice OCR)

    Returns:
        "yes" = matching (or EITHER side is 'not available' / invalid -> treat as match)
        "no"  = not matching
    """

    # If EITHER value is invalid / not available -> treat as MATCH
    if is_invalid(a) or is_invalid(b):
        return "yes"

    a_norm, b_norm = norm_dealer_name(a), norm_dealer_name(b)

    # If either becomes empty after normalization -> treat as match
    if not a_norm or not b_norm:
        return "yes"

    score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a_norm, b_norm)  # 0-100

    if score >= t["ratio"] * 100:
        return "yes"

    if edit_distance(a_norm, b_norm) <= t["max_edits"]:
        return "yes"

    return "no"


def check_gstin(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):
    """
    a = dealer_gst (expected / p_base_data)
    b = dealer_gst_number_unst_str (observed / invoice OCR)

    Returns:
        "yes" = matching (or EITHER side is 'not available' / invalid -> treat as match)
        "no"  = not matching
    """

    # If EITHER value is invalid / not available -> treat as MATCH
    if is_invalid(a) or is_invalid(b):
        return "yes"

    a_norm, b_norm = norm_alnum_upper(a), norm_alnum_upper(b)

    # If either becomes empty after normalization -> treat as match
    if not a_norm or not b_norm:
        return "yes"

    if a_norm == b_norm:
        return "yes"

    if len(a_norm) < 12 or len(b_norm) < 12:
        return "no"

    if fuzzy_match(a_norm, b_norm, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
        return "yes"

    return "no"


# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECKS
# =========================================================
merged_df["dealer_name_match"] = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_dealer_name(r.get("dealer_name"), r.get("dealer_name_unst_str")),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["dealer_gst_match"] = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_gstin(r.get("dealer_gst"), r.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str")),
    axis=1
)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(name_match, gst_match):
    # Exception = "yes" if EITHER name or GST does NOT match
    if name_match == "no" or gst_match == "no":
        return "yes"
    return "no"


def build_observed_value(name_match, gst_match):
    name_txt = (
        "dealer name is matching"
        if name_match == "yes"
        else "dealer name is not matching"
    )

    gst_txt = (
        "GST number is matching"
        if gst_match == "yes"
        else "GST number is not matching"
    )

    return f"{name_txt}; {gst_txt}"


def build_additional_remarks(name_match, gst_match):
    if name_match == "yes" and gst_match == "yes":
        return "Both dealer name and GST number are matching with customer invoice"

    if name_match == "yes" and gst_match == "no":
        return "Dealer name is matching but GST number is not matching with customer invoice"

    if name_match == "no" and gst_match == "yes":
        return "GST number is matching but dealer name is not matching with customer invoice"

    return "Both dealer name and GST number are not matching with customer invoice"


output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                       CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                     CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                     now_ts,
    "updated_at":                     now_ts,
    "is_active":                      merged_df.get("is_active"),

    "sr_number":                      merged_df.get("sr_number"),

    "dealer_name_obeserved_value":    merged_df.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
    "dealer_gst_observed_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
    "dealer_name_expected_value":     merged_df.get("dealer_name"),
    "dealer_gst_expected_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst"),
    "dealer_name_match":              merged_df["dealer_name_match"],
    "dealer_gst_match":               merged_df["dealer_gst_match"],
    "exception_flag": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_exception_flag(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_observed_value(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    # "additional_remarks": merged_df.apply(
    #     lambda r: build_additional_remarks(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
    #     axis=1
    # ),
})

output_df["additional_remarks"]='N/A'

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)


test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Name match=yes:  {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Name match=no:   {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=yes:   {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=no:    {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no (both match):            {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes (one or both mismatch): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")

WRITE_MODE = "upsert"
