import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1001
CHECK_NAME  = "DOP matched with Customer Invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1001"

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA  (raw dataframes kept UNCHANGED)
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df_raw = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows (RAW): {len(unst_df_raw)}")   # should print 6802

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS  (work on a COPY, raw stays intact)
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df_raw.copy()
unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

def parse_date_any(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return None
    s = str(v).strip()
    fmts = [
        "%Y-%m-%d", "%Y/%m/%d", "%d-%m-%Y", "%d/%m/%Y",
        "%d.%m.%Y", "%m-%d-%Y", "%m/%d/%Y",
        "%d-%b-%Y", "%d %b %Y", "%d-%B-%Y", "%d %B %Y",
        "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
    ]
    for f in fmts:
        try:
            return datetime.strptime(s[:len(f) + 4], f).date()
        except:
            continue
    try:
        d = pd.to_datetime(s, dayfirst=True, errors="coerce")
        return d.date() if pd.notna(d) else None
    except:
        return None

# =========================================================
# POSITIONALLY-ALIGNED AGGREGATION
# (no dropna, no unique -> every column keeps 1 element per row
#  so attch_id stays perfectly aligned with date_of_purchase)
# =========================================================
def join_aligned(series):
    out = []
    for v in series.tolist():
        if v is None:
            out.append("Not available")
            continue
        try:
            if pd.isna(v):
                out.append("Not available")
                continue
        except Exception:
            pass
        s = str(v).strip()
        out.append(s if s != "" else "Not available")
    return "~".join(out)

unst_agg = unst_df.groupby(JOIN_KEYS, as_index=False).agg(join_aligned)

print(f"unst aggregated rows (per header_crm_id+sr_id): {len(unst_agg)}")

# =========================================================
# MERGE  (base grain preserved -> raw base data unchanged)
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_agg.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE CHECK  (OR LOGIC, aligned attch_id)
# =========================================================
def check_date_attachmentwise(expected_date, observed_dates, attch_ids):
    """
    Match if ANY observed value matches the expected date.

    Rules:
      - ANY element matches expected            -> MATCH (flag 0), report matching attch_id(s)
      - All observed values missing/not-avail   -> MATCH (flag 0)
      - Valid value(s) present but none match    -> MISMATCH (flag 1)

    Returns: flag, matched_attchs, mismatch_attchs
    """
    expected = parse_date_any(expected_date)

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_dates).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched_attchs   = []
    mismatch_attchs  = []
    valid_value_seen = False

    for idx, obs_date in enumerate(obs_list):

        # attch_id is now aligned; safe fallback just in case
        if idx < len(attch_list):
            attch = attch_list[idx]
        elif attch_list:
            attch = attch_list[-1]
        else:
            attch = ""

        # Skip missing / invalid observed values
        if is_missing(obs_date):
            continue

        valid_value_seen = True
        obs = parse_date_any(obs_date)

        if expected is not None and obs is not None and obs == expected:
            matched_attchs.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatch_attchs.append(attch)

    matched_attchs  = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in matched_attchs if a]))
    mismatch_attchs = list(dict.fromkeys([a for a in mismatch_attchs if a]))

    # CASE 1: all values missing / not available -> MATCH
    if not valid_value_seen:
        return 0, "", ""

    # CASE 2: at least one matched -> MATCH
    if matched_attchs:
        return 0, ",".join(matched_attchs), ""

    # CASE 3: valid values present but none matched -> MISMATCH
    return 1, "", ",".join(mismatch_attchs)

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK  (use ALIGNED unst attch_id)
# =========================================================
temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_date_attachmentwise(
        r.get("purchase_date"),
        r.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id_unst_str")          # <-- aligned attach ids from unst table
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"] = temp.apply(lambda x: x[0]).astype(int)
merged_df["matched_attch_ids"]      = temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["mismatch_attch_ids"]     = temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

# Output attch_id = aligned unst attach ids (fallback to base attch_id if unst missing)
def resolve_attch(r):
    u = r.get("attch_id_unst_str")
    if u is not None and str(u).strip() != "" and not is_missing(u):
        return u
    return r.get("attch_id")

merged_df["attch_id_out"] = merged_df.apply(resolve_attch, axis=1)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def remark_text(flag):
    if flag == 0:
        return "purchase date is matching with system date"
    else:
        return "purchase date is not matching with system date"

def additional_remarks_text(row):
    if row["date_of_purchase_check"] == 0:
        if row["matched_attch_ids"]:
            return f"Purchase date matched with attachment(s): {row['matched_attch_ids']}"
        else:
            return "Purchase date not available in any attachment; treated as match"
    else:
        return f"Purchase date mismatch in attachment(s): {row['mismatch_attch_ids']}"

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":            CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":          CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":          now_ts,
    "updated_at":          now_ts,
    "is_active":           merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":       merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":           merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":            merged_df["attch_id_out"],
    "category":            merged_df.get("category"),
    "dop_observed_value":  merged_df.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
    "dop_expected_value":  merged_df.get("purchase_date"),
    "exception_flag":      merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(
        lambda x: "yes" if x == 1 else "no"
    ),
    "reason":              merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(remark_text),
})

output_df["additional_remarks"] = merged_df.apply(additional_remarks_text, axis=1)

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")

# =========================================================
# SUMMARY COUNT
# =========================================================
total_rows   = len(output_df)
match_count  = (output_df["exception_flag"] == "no").sum()
mismatch_cnt = (output_df["exception_flag"] == "yes").sum()

print("----------------------------------------")
print("SUMMARY")
print(f"Total rows       : {total_rows}")
print(f"Matches (no)     : {match_count}")
print(f"Mismatches (yes) : {mismatch_cnt}")
print("----------------------------------------")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   updated_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id TEXT,
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   dop_observed_value TEXT,
#   dop_expected_value TEXT,
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   reason TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id(255))
# )
# """
# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id", "check_name", "created_at", "updated_at", "is_active",
    "header_crm_id", "sr_number", "attch_id", "category",
    "dop_observed_value", "dop_expected_value",
    "exception_flag", "reason", "additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list     = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols
               if c not in ["check_id", "header_crm_id", "sr_number", "attch_id", "created_at"]]
update_sql  = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i + BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i + len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1001")

import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1001
CHECK_NAME  = "DOP matched with Customer Invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1001"

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows: {len(unst_df)}")

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

unst_df = (
    unst_df.groupby(["header_crm_id", "sr_id"], as_index=False)
            .agg(lambda x: "~".join(pd.unique(x.dropna().astype(str))))
)

# =========================================================
# MERGE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_df.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "not_available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

def parse_date_any(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return None
    s = str(v).strip()
    fmts = [
        "%Y-%m-%d", "%Y/%m/%d", "%d-%m-%Y", "%d/%m/%Y",
        "%d.%m.%Y", "%m-%d-%Y", "%m/%d/%Y",
        "%d-%b-%Y", "%d %b %Y", "%d-%B-%Y", "%d %B %Y",
        "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
    ]
    for f in fmts:
        try:
            return datetime.strptime(s[:len(f) + 4], f).date()
        except:
            continue
    try:
        d = pd.to_datetime(s, dayfirst=True, errors="coerce")
        return d.date() if pd.notna(d) else None
    except:
        return None

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE CHECK  (OR LOGIC)
# =========================================================
def check_date_attachmentwise(expected_date, observed_dates, attch_ids):
    """
    Match if ANY observed value matches the expected date.

    Rules:
      - If ANY element matches expected -> MATCH (flag = 0), report matching attch_id(s)
      - If all observed values are missing/not-available -> MATCH (flag = 0)
      - Only if there is at least one valid value AND none match -> MISMATCH (flag = 1)

    Returns:
        flag (int): 0 = match, 1 = mismatch
        matched_attchs (str): attch_id(s) where value matched
        mismatch_attchs (str): attch_id(s) where valid value did not match
    """
    expected = parse_date_any(expected_date)

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_dates).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    matched_attchs   = []
    mismatch_attchs  = []
    valid_value_seen = False

    for idx, obs_date in enumerate(obs_list):

        # Skip missing / invalid observed values (not counted either way)
        if is_missing(obs_date):
            continue

        valid_value_seen = True
        obs = parse_date_any(obs_date)

        attch = attch_list[idx] if idx < len(attch_list) else f"index_{idx}"

        if expected is not None and obs is not None and obs == expected:
            matched_attchs.append(attch)
        else:
            mismatch_attchs.append(attch)

    # De-duplicate preserving order
    matched_attchs  = list(dict.fromkeys(matched_attchs))
    mismatch_attchs = list(dict.fromkeys(mismatch_attchs))

    # CASE 1: All values missing / not available -> MATCH
    if not valid_value_seen:
        return 0, "", ""

    # CASE 2: At least one value matched -> MATCH
    if matched_attchs:
        return 0, ",".join(matched_attchs), ""

    # CASE 3: Valid values present but none matched -> MISMATCH
    return 1, "", ",".join(mismatch_attchs)

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK
# =========================================================
temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_date_attachmentwise(
        r.get("purchase_date"),
        r.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id")
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"] = temp.apply(lambda x: x[0]).astype(int)
merged_df["matched_attch_ids"]      = temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["mismatch_attch_ids"]     = temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def remark_text(flag):
    if flag == 0:
        return "purchase date is matching with system date"
    else:
        return "purchase date is not matching with system date"

def additional_remarks_text(row):
    if row["date_of_purchase_check"] == 0:
        if row["matched_attch_ids"]:
            return f"Purchase date matched with attachment(s): {row['matched_attch_ids']}"
        else:
            # all values were not available / missing
            return "Purchase date not available in any attachment; treated as match"
    else:
        return f"Purchase date mismatch in attachment(s): {row['mismatch_attch_ids']}"

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":            CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":          CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":          now_ts,
    "updated_at":          now_ts,
    "is_active":           merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":       merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":           merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":            merged_df["attch_id"],
    "category":            merged_df.get("category"),
    "dop_observed_value":  merged_df.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
    "dop_expected_value":  merged_df.get("purchase_date"),
    "exception_flag":      merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(
        lambda x: "yes" if x == 1 else "no"
    ),
    "reason":              merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(remark_text),
})

# Attachment-wise additional remarks
output_df["additional_remarks"] = merged_df.apply(additional_remarks_text, axis=1)

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")

# =========================================================
# SUMMARY COUNT (validation before insert)
# =========================================================
total_rows   = len(output_df)
match_count  = (output_df["exception_flag"] == "no").sum()
mismatch_cnt = (output_df["exception_flag"] == "yes").sum()

print("----------------------------------------")
print("SUMMARY")
print(f"Total rows       : {total_rows}")
print(f"Matches (no)     : {match_count}")
print(f"Mismatches (yes) : {mismatch_cnt}")
print("----------------------------------------")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   updated_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id TEXT,
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   dop_observed_value TEXT,
#   dop_expected_value TEXT,
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   reason TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id)
# )
# """
# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id", "check_name", "created_at", "updated_at", "is_active",
    "header_crm_id", "sr_number", "attch_id", "category",
    "dop_observed_value", "dop_expected_value",
    "exception_flag", "reason", "additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list     = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols
               if c not in ["check_id", "header_crm_id", "sr_number", "attch_id", "created_at"]]
update_sql  = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i + BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i + len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1001")

temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_date_attachmentwise(
        r.get("purchase_date"),
        r.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id")
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"] = temp.apply(lambda x: x[0]).astype(int)
merged_df["matched_attch_ids"]      = temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])
merged_df["mismatch_attch_ids"]     = temp.apply(lambda x: x[2])

    if flag == 0:
        return "purchase date is matching with system date"
    else:
        return "purchase date is not matching with system date"

def additional_remarks_text(row):
    if row["date_of_purchase_check"] == 0:
        if row["matched_attch_ids"]:
            return f"Purchase date matched with attachment(s): {row['matched_attch_ids']}"
        else:
            # all values were not available / missing
            return "Purchase date not available in any attachment; treated as match"
    else:
        return f"Purchase date mismatch in attachment(s): {row['mismatch_attch_ids']}"

    "reason":              merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(remark_text),

import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1001
CHECK_NAME  = "DOP matched with Customer Invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1001"

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows: {len(unst_df)}")

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id"]

unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

unst_df = (
    unst_df.groupby(["header_crm_id", "sr_id"], as_index=False)
            .agg(lambda x: "~".join(pd.unique(x.dropna().astype(str))))
)

# =========================================================
# MERGE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_df.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available",
             "error", "na", "n/a", "not found", "blank"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS

def parse_date_any(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return None
    s = str(v).strip()
    fmts = [
        "%Y-%m-%d", "%Y/%m/%d", "%d-%m-%Y", "%d/%m/%Y",
        "%d.%m.%Y", "%m-%d-%Y", "%m/%d/%Y",
        "%d-%b-%Y", "%d %b %Y", "%d-%B-%Y", "%d %B %Y",
        "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
    ]
    for f in fmts:
        try:
            return datetime.strptime(s[:len(f) + 4], f).date()
        except:
            continue
    try:
        d = pd.to_datetime(s, dayfirst=True, errors="coerce")
        return d.date() if pd.notna(d) else None
    except:
        return None

# =========================================================
# ATTACHMENT-WISE CHECK
# =========================================================
def check_date_attachmentwise(expected_date, observed_dates, attch_ids):
    """
    Returns:
        flag (int): 0 = match / no mismatch, 1 = mismatch found
        mismatch_attchs (str): comma-separated attch_ids where mismatch found
    """
    if is_missing(observed_dates):
        return 0, ""

    expected = parse_date_any(expected_date)
    if expected is None:
        return 0, ""

    obs_list   = [x.strip() for x in str(observed_dates).split("~")]
    attch_list = [x.strip() for x in str(attch_ids).split("~")]

    mismatch_attchs = []

    for idx, obs_date in enumerate(obs_list):

        # Skip missing / invalid observed values (not a mismatch)
        if is_missing(obs_date):
            continue

        obs = parse_date_any(obs_date)
        if obs is None:
            continue

        if obs != expected:
            # Map to corresponding attch_id if available
            if idx < len(attch_list):
                mismatch_attchs.append(attch_list[idx])
            else:
                mismatch_attchs.append(f"index_{idx}")

    if mismatch_attchs:
        # remove duplicates while preserving order
        mismatch_attchs = list(dict.fromkeys(mismatch_attchs))
        return 1, ",".join(mismatch_attchs)

    return 0, ""

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK
# =========================================================
temp = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_date_attachmentwise(
        r.get("purchase_date"),
        r.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
        r.get("attch_id")
    ),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"] = temp.apply(lambda x: x[0]).astype(int)
merged_df["mismatch_attch_ids"]     = temp.apply(lambda x: x[1])

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def remark_text(flag):
    if flag == 0:
        return "purchase date is matching with system date"
    else:
        return "purchase date is not matching with system date"

def additional_remarks_text(row):
    if row["date_of_purchase_check"] == 1:
        return f"Purchase date mismatch found in attachment(s): {row['mismatch_attch_ids']}"
    else:
        return f"Purchase date matched in attachment(s): {row['attch_id']}"

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":            CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":          CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":          now_ts,
    "updated_at":          now_ts,
    "is_active":           merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":       merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":           merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":            merged_df["attch_id"],
    "category":            merged_df.get("category"),
    "dop_observed_value":  merged_df.get("date_of_purchase_unst_str"),
    "dop_expected_value":  merged_df.get("purchase_date"),
    "exception_flag":      merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(
        lambda x: "yes" if x == 1 else "no"
    ),
    "reason":              merged_df["date_of_purchase_check"].apply(remark_text),
})

# Attachment-wise additional remarks
output_df["additional_remarks"] = merged_df.apply(additional_remarks_text, axis=1)

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   updated_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id TEXT,
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   dop_observed_value TEXT,
#   dop_expected_value TEXT,
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   reason TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id)
# )
# """
# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id", "check_name", "created_at", "updated_at", "is_active",
    "header_crm_id", "sr_number", "attch_id", "category",
    "dop_observed_value", "dop_expected_value",
    "exception_flag", "reason", "additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list     = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols
               if c not in ["check_id", "header_crm_id", "sr_number", "attch_id", "created_at"]]
update_sql  = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i + BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i + len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1001")

#     return int(da == db)


def check_date(a, b):
    invalid_values = {
        None, "", "null", "none", "nan",
        "not available", "error", "na", "n/a","not found"
    }

    # Normalize and check invalid values
    a_str = str(a).strip().lower() if a is not None else None
    b_str = str(b).strip().lower() if b is not None else None

    if a_str in invalid_values or b_str in invalid_values:
        return 0

    da = parse_date_any(a)
    db = parse_date_any(b)

    # If parsing fails for either value, don't count as mismatch
    if da is None or db is None:
        return 0

    # 0 = match, 1 = mismatch
    return int(da != db)

unst_std = (
    unst_std.groupby(["header_crm_id", "sr_id"], as_index=False)
            .agg(lambda x: "^".join(pd.unique(x.dropna().astype(str))))

==================================


dealer_name: 
- Extract the ACTUAL seller / dealer / shop / vendor business name. 
- Usually present at the top/header of invoice. 
- IMPORTANT (Voltas handling): 
* "Voltas Limited", "Voltas Ltd", "Voltas" alone is only a BRAND name, NOT a dealer name. If only Voltas branding is present, return "Not available". 
* "Voltas Authorized Service Partner", "Voltas Authorised Dealer", "Authorized Voltas Dealer" etc. is only a LABEL. The REAL dealer/shop name is usually printed right after / near this label. 
* In such cases, extract ONLY the real dealer/shop name and DROP the Voltas label text. 
Example: "Voltas Authorized Service Partner - Sharma Cooling" => dealer_name = "Sharma Cooling" 
* If no real dealer/shop name exists apart from the Voltas branding/label, return "Not available". 
- Do not extract customer name.


def clean_dealer_name(dealer_value):
    if dealer_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    dealer_value = str(dealer_value).strip()

    if dealer_value == "" or dealer_value.lower() in ["none", "null", "nan", "not available"]:
        return "Not available"

    original = dealer_value

    # Voltas branding / label phrases to strip out
    voltas_phrases = [
        r"voltas\s+authoriz(?:e|s)?ed\s+service\s+partner",
        r"voltas\s+authoris(?:e|s)?ed\s+service\s+partner",
        r"authoriz(?:e|s)?ed\s+voltas\s+(?:service\s+)?(?:partner|dealer)",
        r"authoris(?:e|s)?ed\s+voltas\s+(?:service\s+)?(?:partner|dealer)",
        r"voltas\s+authoriz(?:e|s)?ed\s+dealer",
        r"voltas\s+authoris(?:e|s)?ed\s+dealer",
        r"voltas\s+limited",
        r"voltas\s+ltd\.?",
        r"voltas",
    ]

    cleaned = original
    for phrase in voltas_phrases:
        cleaned = re.sub(phrase, " ", cleaned, flags=re.IGNORECASE)

    # Remove leftover separators/punctuation at the edges
    cleaned = re.sub(r"[-–—:|,/]+", " ", cleaned)
    cleaned = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", cleaned).strip()

    # If a real dealer name remains, keep it
    if cleaned and len(cleaned) >= 3:
        return cleaned

    # Otherwise only Voltas branding was present
    return "Not available"

    raise ValueError("OUTPUT_PKL_FOLDER environment variable is missing.")

# =========================================================
# CLIENT
# =========================================================
http_client = httpx.Client(trust_env=False)

client = OpenAI(
    api_key=AZURE_OPENAI_KEY,
    base_url=AZURE_BASE_URL,
    http_client=http_client
)

# =========================================================

# =========================================================
INVOICE_PROMPT = """
You are a highly accurate invoice data extraction system specialized in
CUSTOMER INVOICES submitted to VOLTAS for WARRANTY CLAIMS.

Extract only the required fields from the invoice image and return STRICT JSON ONLY.

============================================================
GLOBAL RULES
============================================================
1. Output ENGLISH ONLY.
2. Do NOT hallucinate.
3. Do NOT guess or infer values.
4. Extract only values clearly visible in the invoice image.
5. If any value is not clearly visible, return "Not available".
6. Return JSON only. No markdown. No explanation. No comments.
7. Dates must be returned in YYYY-MM-DD format.
8. If only partial date is visible, return "Not available".
9. Phone numbers must contain digits only.
10. Addresses must be single-line comma-separated text.
11. Remove extra spaces, line breaks, and unnecessary punctuation.
12. If multiple invoices are present in one image, return:
    {
      "invoices": [
        { same schema },
        { same schema }
      ]
    }

============================================================
MOST IMPORTANT FIELD: product_serial_number
============================================================
Product serial number is VERY CRITICAL.

Definition of a valid product serial number:
- Alphanumeric only (uppercase letters A-Z and digits 0-9).
- Length must be greater than 14 characters.
- Must contain at least one digit.
- Must NOT contain spaces, slashes, dashes, dots, commas, colons, or any special characters inside.
- Usually starts with digits and ends with digits.
- May contain uppercase letters in between.

Where to look (very important):
- Product serial number is mostly present with the item name or product description.
- It is often written immediately after the product name, item name, or model description.
- It may also appear in the line-item table, in the description column,
  or as a standalone alphanumeric token near the product details.
- LABEL IS NOT MANDATORY:
    The serial number may appear WITHOUT any label like "S.No", "Sr No",
    "Serial No", "S/N", etc. It can simply be printed next to or below the
    item name as a standalone alphanumeric value.
- If a label is present, common labels include:
  Serial No, Sr No, Sr.No, S.No, S No, SR NO, S/N, SN,
  Product Serial No, Product Sr No, Machine No, Unit Serial No,
  Barcode, IDU SR NO, ODU SR NO, Indoor Serial No, Outdoor Serial No.
- Even if no label is present, treat any standalone alphanumeric token
  matching the format rules (length > 14, alphanumeric, contains digits)
  near the item/product description as the product serial number.

Multiple serial numbers:
- A customer may buy multiple products in the same invoice.
- Therefore, multiple product serial numbers may be present.
- Extract ALL valid product serial numbers.
- Join multiple valid product serial numbers using "^" with no spaces.

Strict exclusions — do NOT extract these as product_serial_number:
- Model number / model code (e.g., short codes printed in the model column)
- Item code / SKU
- HSN code / SAC code
- GSTIN (15-char taxpayer ID)
- Invoice number / Bill number / Receipt number
- Customer or dealer mobile/phone number
- Quantity / Rate / Amount / Discount values
- Date values
- PIN code

If no valid product serial number is visible, return "Not available".

============================================================
FIELD RULES
============================================================

invoice_number:
- Extract invoice number / bill number / tax invoice number.
- Look for labels such as Invoice No, Bill No, Tax Invoice No, Inv No, Receipt No.
- Keep slashes and dashes if printed.
- Do not confuse with GSTIN, product serial number, model number, HSN, or phone number.

product_serial_number:
- Extract as per the rules above.
- Multiple serials must be separated using "^".

date_of_purchase: 
- Extract the invoice date / bill date / purchase date from the invoice body or header only. 
- Convert to YYYY-MM-DD. - Do not use due date, delivery date, warranty date, or print date. 
- VERY IMPORTANT (IGNORE GPS / CAMERA STAMP DATE): 
    * Do NOT extract any date printed at the BOTTOM of the image near the longitude / latitude / GPS coordinates. 
    * Such a date is usually a camera / GPS timestamp overlay and typically appears on a BLACK background (dark box with white text). 
    * This overlay date is NOT the purchase date and MUST be ignored. 
- Only pick the genuine invoice/bill/purchase date printed in the invoice content. 
- If no genuine invoice/bill/purchase date is clearly visible, return "Not available".

dealer_name:
- Extract seller / dealer / shop / vendor business name.
- Usually present at the top/header of invoice.
- Do not extract Voltas brand name unless it is the actual dealer name.
- Do not extract customer name.

dealer_name: 
- Extract seller / dealer / shop / vendor business name. 
- Usually present at the top/header of invoice. 
- VERY IMPORTANT: Do NOT extract "Voltas" as the dealer name. 
    * If the dealer/seller name contains the word "Voltas" (in ANY case, e.g. "VOLTAS", "Voltas Ltd", "Voltas Limited"), return "Not available". 
- Do not extract customer name.

dealer_gst_number:
- Extract dealer GSTIN only.
- GSTIN is exactly 15 characters.
- Pick seller/dealer GSTIN, usually in header.
- Do not pick customer GSTIN if both are present.

dealer_address:
- Extract full dealer/seller address from header area.
- Do not mix with customer address.

customer_name:
- Extract buyer/customer name.
- Look near Bill To, Buyer, Customer Name, Sold To, Party Name, Ship To, Consignee.
- Prefer Bill To / Buyer if both Bill To and Ship To are present.
- Do not extract dealer name.

customer_address:
- Extract full customer/buyer address.
- Look near customer name, Bill To, Buyer, Consignee, or Ship To block.
- Do not extract dealer address.

customer_phone_number:
- Extract customer phone/mobile/contact number only.
- Customer phone number may be multiple.
- Multiple numbers may be separated by "/", ",", "&", "|", "and", or "or".
- Extract all customer phone numbers.
- Digits only.
- Join multiple phone numbers using "^" with no spaces.
- Do not extract dealer phone number.

============================================================
OUTPUT JSON SCHEMA
============================================================
{
  "invoice_number": "string",
  "product_serial_number": "string",
  "date_of_purchase": "string",
  "dealer_name": "string",
  "dealer_gst_number": "string",
  "dealer_address": "string",
  "customer_name": "string",
  "customer_address": "string",
  "customer_phone_number": "string"
}

Return JSON only.
"""

SERIAL_ONLY_PROMPT = """
Extract only the product serial number from this Voltas warranty invoice image.

Rules:
- Product serial number is mostly present with the item name or product description.
- It is often written immediately after the product name or model description.
- It may appear WITHOUT any label like "S.No", "Sr No", "Serial No", etc.
- Even an unlabeled standalone alphanumeric token near the product details
  should be considered if it matches the format rules below.
- Product serial number is alphanumeric only.
- Length must be greater than 14 characters.
- Must contain at least one digit.
- No spaces, slashes, dashes, dots, commas, or special characters inside.
- Extract ALL valid serial numbers.
- If multiple serial numbers are present, join them using "^" with no spaces.
- Do not extract HSN code, GSTIN, invoice number, model number, phone number,
  amount, quantity, rate, or date as a serial number.
- If no valid serial number is visible, return "Not available".

Return JSON only:
{
  "product_serial_number": "string"
}
"""

# =========================================================
# FIELD KEYS
# =========================================================
FIELD_KEYS = [
    "invoice_number",
    "product_serial_number",
    "date_of_purchase",
    "dealer_name",
    "dealer_gst_number",
    "dealer_address",
    "customer_name",
    "customer_address",
    "customer_phone_number"
]

# =========================================================
# IMAGE HELPERS
# =========================================================
def resize_image(image_path, max_size=2048):
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        if max(img.size) <= max_size:
            return image_path

        ratio = max_size / max(img.size)
        new_size = (int(img.size[0] * ratio), int(img.size[1] * ratio))

        temp_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()
        temp_path = os.path.join(temp_dir, os.path.basename(image_path))

        img.resize(new_size, Image.LANCZOS).save(temp_path)
        return temp_path


def encode_image(image_path):
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        img = img.convert("RGB")
        buffer = BytesIO()
        img.save(buffer, format="JPEG")
        return base64.b64encode(buffer.getvalue()).decode()

# =========================================================
# CLEANERS / VALIDATORS
# =========================================================
def clean_text(value):
    if value is None:
        return "Not available"

    value = str(value).strip()

    if value == "" or value.lower() in ["none", "null", "nan", "not available"]:
        return "Not available"

    value = re.sub(r"[\r\n\t]+", " ", value)
    value = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", value).strip()

    return value


def is_valid_product_serial(serial):
    """
    Valid product serial:
    - Alphanumeric only (A-Z, 0-9)
    - Length > 14
    - Must contain at least one digit
    """
    if not serial:
        return False

    serial = str(serial).strip().upper()

    if len(serial) <= 14:
        return False

    if not re.match(r"^[A-Z0-9]+$", serial):
        return False

    if not re.search(r"[0-9]", serial):
        return False

    return True


def clean_product_serial_number(serial_value):
    """
    Extract and keep only valid product serial numbers.
    Multiple valid serial numbers are returned using ^ separator.
    """
    if serial_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    serial_value = str(serial_value).upper().strip()

    if serial_value in ["", "NOT AVAILABLE", "ERROR", "NONE", "NULL", "NAN"]:
        return "Not available"

    valid_serials = []

    # Split by common separators including ^
    chunks = re.split(r"[\^,;/|&\s]+", serial_value)

    for chunk in chunks:
        compact = re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", chunk)

        if is_valid_product_serial(compact):
            if compact not in valid_serials:
                valid_serials.append(compact)

    # Fallback regex scan over raw text
    if not valid_serials:
        candidates = re.findall(r"[A-Z0-9]{15,30}", serial_value)
        for cand in candidates:
            if is_valid_product_serial(cand) and cand not in valid_serials:
                valid_serials.append(cand)

    if valid_serials:
        return "^".join(valid_serials)

    return "Not available"


def clean_customer_phone_number(phone_value):
    if phone_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    phone_value = str(phone_value).strip()

    if phone_value == "" or phone_value.lower() in ["not available", "error", "none", "null", "nan"]:
        return "Not available"

    parts = re.split(r"[\^/,;&|]|\band\b|\bor\b", phone_value, flags=re.IGNORECASE)

    final_numbers = []

    for part in parts:
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)

        if not digits:
            continue

        if len(digits) == 12 and digits.startswith("91"):
            digits = digits[-10:]
        elif len(digits) == 11 and digits.startswith("0"):
            digits = digits[-10:]

        if len(digits) == 10 and digits[0] in ["6", "7", "8", "9"]:
            if digits not in final_numbers:
                final_numbers.append(digits)

    if final_numbers:
        return "^".join(final_numbers)

    return "Not available"


def clean_gstin(gstin_value):
    if gstin_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    gstin_value = str(gstin_value).upper().strip()
    gstin_value = re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", gstin_value)

    pattern = r"^[0-9]{2}[A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z][1-9A-Z]Z[0-9A-Z]$"

    if re.match(pattern, gstin_value):
        return gstin_value

    return "Not available"


def clean_dealer_name(dealer_value):
    if dealer_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    dealer_value = str(dealer_value).strip()

    if dealer_value == "" or dealer_value.lower() in ["none", "null", "nan", "not available"]:
        return "Not available"

    if "voltas" in dealer_value.lower():
        return "Not available"

    return dealer_value


def normalize_extracted_data(data):
    normalized = {}

    for key in FIELD_KEYS:
        normalized[key] = clean_text(data.get(key, "Not available"))

    normalized["product_serial_number"] = clean_product_serial_number(
        normalized.get("product_serial_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["customer_phone_number"] = clean_customer_phone_number(
        normalized.get("customer_phone_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["dealer_gst_number"] = clean_gstin(
        normalized.get("dealer_gst_number", "Not available")
    )
    normalized["dealer_name"] = clean_dealer_name(
        normalized.get("dealer_name", "Not available")
    )

    return normalized

# =========================================================
# TARGETED SERIAL EXTRACTION
# =========================================================
def extract_serial_only(image_b64):
    try:
        response = client.chat.completions.create(
            model=MODEL_NAME,
            temperature=0,
            max_tokens=500,
            response_format={"type": "json_object"},
            messages=[
                {
                    "role": "user",
                    "content": [
                        {"type": "text", "text": SERIAL_ONLY_PROMPT},
                        {
                            "type": "image_url",
                            "image_url": {
                                "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_b64}"
                            }
                        }
                    ]
                }
            ]
        )

        raw = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)
        serial = raw.get("product_serial_number", "Not available")

        return clean_product_serial_number(serial)

    except Exception:
        return "Not available"

# =========================================================
# PROCESS IMAGE
# =========================================================
def process_image(image_path):
    backoff = INITIAL_BACKOFF

    for attempt in range(1, MAX_RETRIES + 1):
        try:
            processed_img = resize_image(image_path)
            image_b64 = encode_image(processed_img)

            response = client.chat.completions.create(
                model=MODEL_NAME,
                temperature=0,
                max_tokens=3000,
                response_format={"type": "json_object"},
                messages=[
                    {
                        "role": "user",
                        "content": [
                            {"type": "text", "text": INVOICE_PROMPT},
                            {
                                "type": "image_url",
                                "image_url": {
                                    "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_b64}"
                                }
                            }
                        ]
                    }
                ]
            )

            raw_data = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)

            # =====================================================
            # MULTI-INVOICE SAFE HANDLING
            # =====================================================
            if "invoices" in raw_data and isinstance(raw_data["invoices"], list):

                invoices = raw_data["invoices"]
                merged_data = {k: [] for k in FIELD_KEYS}

                for inv in invoices:
                    inv = normalize_extracted_data(inv)

                    for key in FIELD_KEYS:
                        value = inv.get(key, "Not available")
                        if value and value != "Not available":
                            merged_data[key].append(str(value))

                data = {}

                for key in FIELD_KEYS:
                    if merged_data[key]:
                        if key == "product_serial_number":
                            data[key] = clean_product_serial_number(
                                "^".join(merged_data[key])
                            )
                        elif key == "customer_phone_number":
                            data[key] = clean_customer_phone_number(
                                "^".join(merged_data[key])
                            )
                        else:
                            data[key] = ", ".join(merged_data[key])
                    else:
                        data[key] = "Not available"

            else:
                data = normalize_extracted_data(raw_data)

            # =====================================================
            # SECOND PASS ONLY IF SERIAL NOT FOUND
            # =====================================================
            if data.get("product_serial_number", "Not available") == "Not available":
                serial_second_pass = extract_serial_only(image_b64)
                data["product_serial_number"] = serial_second_pass

            data["file_name"] = os.path.basename(image_path)

            print(f"Processed: {data['file_name']}")
            return data

        except Exception as e:
            if attempt == MAX_RETRIES:
                print(f"Failed after retries: {os.path.basename(image_path)} | Error: {e}")
                break

            print(f"Retry {attempt}/{MAX_RETRIES} for {os.path.basename(image_path)}")
            time.sleep(backoff)
            backoff *= 2

    err_row = {k: "Error" for k in FIELD_KEYS}
    err_row["file_name"] = os.path.basename(image_path)
    return err_row

# =========================================================
# MAIN EXECUTION - IMAGE EXTRACTION
# =========================================================
all_images = [
    os.path.join(IMAGE_FOLDER, f)
    for f in os.listdir(IMAGE_FOLDER)
    if f.lower().endswith((".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png"))
]

print(f"Total images: {len(all_images)}")

results = []

with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=MAX_WORKERS) as executor:
    futures = [executor.submit(process_image, img) for img in all_images]

    for future in as_completed(futures):
        results.append(future.result())

df = pd.DataFrame(results)

# =========================================================

# =========================================================
os.makedirs(OUTPUT_PKL_FOLDER, exist_ok=True)

timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
pkl_file_name = f"output_voltas_warranty_{timestamp}.pkl"
full_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_PKL_FOLDER, pkl_file_name)

df.to_pickle(full_path)

print(f"Pickle File saved at: {full_path}")
print("Exact Columns:", df.columns.tolist())
print("IMAGE EXTRACTION COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")

# =========================================================
# EXTRACT IDs FROM FILE NAME
# =========================================================
def extract_ids(file_name):
    try:
        file_name = str(file_name)

        # Split on ^
        main_part, rest = file_name.split("^")

        # Extract header_crm_id and sr_id
        header_crm_id, sr_id = main_part.split("_")

        # Extract attch_id (before next _)
        attch_id = rest.split("_")[0]

        return header_crm_id, sr_id, attch_id

    except Exception:
        return None, None, None


# Apply to dataframe
df["header_crm_id"], df["sr_id"], df["attch_id"] = zip(
    *df["file_name"].apply(extract_ids)
)
# =========================================================
# MERGE WITH BASE TABLE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    df,
    base_data,
    on=["header_crm_id", "sr_id"],
    how="left"
)

merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print("Merge completed")



# =========================================================
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS
# =========================================================
TABLE_NAME = "p_unst_str_customer_invoice"
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"   # insert | upsert

create_table_query = f"""
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {TABLE_NAME} (

    id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,

    header_crm_id VARCHAR(50),
    sr_id VARCHAR(50),
    attch_id VARCHAR(50),

    sr_open_date DATETIME,
    sr_closed_date DATETIME,

    file_name TEXT,
    invoice_number VARCHAR(255),
    product_serial_number VARCHAR(255),
    date_of_purchase VARCHAR(255),

    dealer_name TEXT,
    dealer_gst_number VARCHAR(255),
    dealer_address TEXT,

    customer_name TEXT,
    customer_address TEXT,
    customer_phone_number VARCHAR(255),

    UNIQUE KEY uniq_invoice (
        header_crm_id,
        sr_id,
        attch_id
    )
)
"""

cursor.execute(create_table_query)
conn.commit()

# =========================================================
# PREPARE DATA
# =========================================================
insert_cols = [
    "header_crm_id",
    "sr_id",
    "attch_id",
    "sr_open_date",
    "sr_closed_date",
    "file_name",
    "invoice_number",
    "product_serial_number",
    "date_of_purchase",
    "dealer_name",
    "dealer_gst_number",
    "dealer_address",
    "customer_name",
    "customer_address",
    "customer_phone_number"
]

for col in insert_cols:
    if col not in merged_df.columns:
        merged_df[col] = None

records = merged_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

# =========================================================
# GENERATE INSERT / UPSERT SQL
# =========================================================
placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

if WRITE_MODE.lower() == "upsert":

    update_cols = [
        c for c in insert_cols
        if c not in ["header_crm_id", "sr_id", "attch_id"]
    ]

    update_sql = ", ".join(
        [f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols]
    )

    insert_sql = f"""
    INSERT INTO {TABLE_NAME} ({col_list})
    VALUES ({placeholders})
    ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE
    {update_sql}
    """

else:

    insert_sql = f"""
    INSERT IGNORE INTO {TABLE_NAME} ({col_list})
    VALUES ({placeholders})
    """

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT / UPSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH_SIZE = 500
DB_MAX_RETRIES = 5

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH_SIZE):

    batch = records[i:i + BATCH_SIZE]

    for attempt in range(DB_MAX_RETRIES):

        try:

            cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
            conn.commit()

            print(
                f"{WRITE_MODE.upper()} : "
                f"{i} to {min(i + len(batch), len(records))}"
            )

            break

        except Exception as e:

            error_text = str(e)

            if "1205" in error_text:

                print(
                    f"Lock detected. Retry "
                    f"{attempt + 1}/{DB_MAX_RETRIES}"
                )

                time.sleep(2)

            else:

                conn.rollback()

                print(
                    f"Database error in batch "
                    f"starting at row {i}: {e}"
                )

                break

# =========================================================
# CLOSE CONNECTION
# =========================================================
cursor.close()
conn.close()

print(f"{WRITE_MODE.upper()} COMPLETED")
print("FULL PIPELINE COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")

INITIAL_BACKOFF = 2

# =========================================================
# PROMPTS
# =========================================================
INVOICE_PROMPT = """
You are a highly accurate invoice data extraction system specialized in
CUSTOMER INVOICES submitted to VOLTAS for WARRANTY CLAIMS.

Extract only the required fields from the invoice image and return STRICT JSON ONLY.

============================================================
GLOBAL RULES
============================================================
1. Output ENGLISH ONLY.
2. Do NOT hallucinate.
3. Do NOT guess or infer values.
4. Extract only values clearly visible in the invoice image.
5. If any value is not clearly visible, return "Not available".
6. Return JSON only. No markdown. No explanation. No comments.
7. Dates must be returned in YYYY-MM-DD format.
8. If only partial date is visible, return "Not available".
9. Phone numbers must contain digits only.
10. Addresses must be single-line comma-separated text.
11. Remove extra spaces, line breaks, and unnecessary punctuation.
12. If multiple invoices are present in one image, return:
    {
      "invoices": [
        { same schema },
        { same schema }
      ]
    }

============================================================
MOST IMPORTANT FIELD: product_serial_number
============================================================
Product serial number is VERY CRITICAL.

Definition of a valid product serial number:
- Alphanumeric only (uppercase letters A-Z and digits 0-9).
- Length must be greater than 14 characters.
- Must contain at least one digit.
- Must NOT contain spaces, slashes, dashes, dots, commas, colons, or any special characters inside.
- Usually starts with digits and ends with digits.
- May contain uppercase letters in between.

Where to look (very important):
- Product serial number is mostly present with the item name or product description.
- It is often written immediately after the product name, item name, or model description.
- It may also appear in the line-item table, in the description column,
  or as a standalone alphanumeric token near the product details.
- LABEL IS NOT MANDATORY:
    The serial number may appear WITHOUT any label like "S.No", "Sr No",
    "Serial No", "S/N", etc. It can simply be printed next to or below the
    item name as a standalone alphanumeric value.
- If a label is present, common labels include:
  Serial No, Sr No, Sr.No, S.No, S No, SR NO, S/N, SN,
  Product Serial No, Product Sr No, Machine No, Unit Serial No,
  Barcode, IDU SR NO, ODU SR NO, Indoor Serial No, Outdoor Serial No.
- Even if no label is present, treat any standalone alphanumeric token
  matching the format rules (length > 14, alphanumeric, contains digits)
  near the item/product description as the product serial number.

Multiple serial numbers:
- A customer may buy multiple products in the same invoice.
- Therefore, multiple product serial numbers may be present.
- Extract ALL valid product serial numbers.
- Join multiple valid product serial numbers using "^" with no spaces.

Strict exclusions — do NOT extract these as product_serial_number:
- Model number / model code (e.g., short codes printed in the model column)
- Item code / SKU
- HSN code / SAC code
- GSTIN (15-char taxpayer ID)
- Invoice number / Bill number / Receipt number
- Customer or dealer mobile/phone number
- Quantity / Rate / Amount / Discount values
- Date values
- PIN code

If no valid product serial number is visible, return "Not available".

============================================================
FIELD RULES
============================================================

invoice_number:
- Extract invoice number / bill number / tax invoice number.
- Look for labels such as Invoice No, Bill No, Tax Invoice No, Inv No, Receipt No.
- Keep slashes and dashes if printed.
- Do not confuse with GSTIN, product serial number, model number, HSN, or phone number.

product_serial_number:
- Extract as per the rules above.
- Multiple serials must be separated using "^".

date_of_purchase:
- Extract invoice date / bill date / purchase date.
- Convert to YYYY-MM-DD.
- Do not use due date, delivery date, warranty date, or print date.

dealer_name:
- Extract seller / dealer / shop / vendor business name.
- Usually present at the top/header of invoice.
- Do not extract Voltas brand name unless it is the actual dealer name.
- Do not extract customer name.

dealer_gst_number:
- Extract dealer GSTIN only.
- GSTIN is exactly 15 characters.
- Pick seller/dealer GSTIN, usually in header.
- Do not pick customer GSTIN if both are present.

dealer_address:
- Extract full dealer/seller address from header area.
- Do not mix with customer address.

customer_name:
- Extract buyer/customer name.
- Look near Bill To, Buyer, Customer Name, Sold To, Party Name, Ship To, Consignee.
- Prefer Bill To / Buyer if both Bill To and Ship To are present.
- Do not extract dealer name.

customer_address:
- Extract full customer/buyer address.
- Look near customer name, Bill To, Buyer, Consignee, or Ship To block.
- Do not extract dealer address.

customer_phone_number:
- Extract customer phone/mobile/contact number only.
- Customer phone number may be multiple.
- Multiple numbers may be separated by "/", ",", "&", "|", "and", or "or".
- Extract all customer phone numbers.
- Digits only.
- Join multiple phone numbers using "^" with no spaces.
- Do not extract dealer phone number.

============================================================
OUTPUT JSON SCHEMA
============================================================
{
  "invoice_number": "string",
  "product_serial_number": "string",
  "date_of_purchase": "string",
  "dealer_name": "string",
  "dealer_gst_number": "string",
  "dealer_address": "string",
  "customer_name": "string",
  "customer_address": "string",
  "customer_phone_number": "string"
}

Return JSON only.
"""

SERIAL_ONLY_PROMPT = """
Extract only the product serial number from this Voltas warranty invoice image.

Rules:
- Product serial number is mostly present with the item name or product description.
- It is often written immediately after the product name or model description.
- It may appear WITHOUT any label like "S.No", "Sr No", "Serial No", etc.
- Even an unlabeled standalone alphanumeric token near the product details
  should be considered if it matches the format rules below.
- Product serial number is alphanumeric only.
- Length must be greater than 14 characters.
- Must contain at least one digit.
- No spaces, slashes, dashes, dots, commas, or special characters inside.
- Extract ALL valid serial numbers.
- If multiple serial numbers are present, join them using "^" with no spaces.
- Do not extract HSN code, GSTIN, invoice number, model number, phone number,
  amount, quantity, rate, or date as a serial number.
- If no valid serial number is visible, return "Not available".

Return JSON only:
{
  "product_serial_number": "string"
}
"""

# =========================================================
# FIELD KEYS
# =========================================================
FIELD_KEYS = [
    "invoice_number",
    "product_serial_number",
    "date_of_purchase",
    "dealer_name",
    "dealer_gst_number",
    "dealer_address",
    "customer_name",
    "customer_address",
    "customer_phone_number"
]

# =========================================================
# IMAGE HELPERS
# =========================================================
def resize_image(image_path, max_size=2048):
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        if max(img.size) <= max_size:
            return image_path

        ratio = max_size / max(img.size)
        new_size = (int(img.size[0] * ratio), int(img.size[1] * ratio))

        temp_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()
        temp_path = os.path.join(temp_dir, os.path.basename(image_path))

        img.resize(new_size, Image.LANCZOS).save(temp_path)
        return temp_path


def encode_image(image_path):
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        img = img.convert("RGB")
        buffer = BytesIO()
        img.save(buffer, format="JPEG")
        return base64.b64encode(buffer.getvalue()).decode()

# =========================================================
# CLEANERS / VALIDATORS
# =========================================================
def clean_text(value):
    if value is None:
        return "Not available"

    value = str(value).strip()

    if value == "" or value.lower() in ["none", "null", "nan", "not available"]:
        return "Not available"

    value = re.sub(r"[\r\n\t]+", " ", value)
    value = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", value).strip()

    return value


def is_valid_product_serial(serial):
    """
    Valid product serial:
    - Alphanumeric only (A-Z, 0-9)
    - Length > 14
    - Must contain at least one digit
    """
    if not serial:
        return False

    serial = str(serial).strip().upper()

    if len(serial) <= 14:
        return False

    if not re.match(r"^[A-Z0-9]+$", serial):
        return False

    if not re.search(r"[0-9]", serial):
        return False

    return True


def clean_product_serial_number(serial_value):
    """
    Extract and keep only valid product serial numbers.
    Multiple valid serial numbers are returned using ^ separator.
    """
    if serial_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    serial_value = str(serial_value).upper().strip()

    if serial_value in ["", "NOT AVAILABLE", "ERROR", "NONE", "NULL", "NAN"]:
        return "Not available"

    valid_serials = []

    # Split by common separators including ^
    chunks = re.split(r"[\^,;/|&\s]+", serial_value)

    for chunk in chunks:
        compact = re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", chunk)

        if is_valid_product_serial(compact):
            if compact not in valid_serials:
                valid_serials.append(compact)

    # Fallback regex scan over raw text
    if not valid_serials:
        candidates = re.findall(r"[A-Z0-9]{15,30}", serial_value)
        for cand in candidates:
            if is_valid_product_serial(cand) and cand not in valid_serials:
                valid_serials.append(cand)

    if valid_serials:
        return "^".join(valid_serials)

    return "Not available"


def clean_customer_phone_number(phone_value):
    if phone_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    phone_value = str(phone_value).strip()

    if phone_value == "" or phone_value.lower() in ["not available", "error", "none", "null", "nan"]:
        return "Not available"

    parts = re.split(r"[\^/,;&|]|\band\b|\bor\b", phone_value, flags=re.IGNORECASE)

    final_numbers = []

    for part in parts:
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)

        if not digits:
            continue

        if len(digits) == 12 and digits.startswith("91"):
            digits = digits[-10:]
        elif len(digits) == 11 and digits.startswith("0"):
            digits = digits[-10:]

        if len(digits) == 10 and digits[0] in ["6", "7", "8", "9"]:
            if digits not in final_numbers:
                final_numbers.append(digits)

    if final_numbers:
        return "^".join(final_numbers)

    return "Not available"


def clean_gstin(gstin_value):
    if gstin_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    gstin_value = str(gstin_value).upper().strip()
    gstin_value = re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", gstin_value)

    pattern = r"^[0-9]{2}[A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z][1-9A-Z]Z[0-9A-Z]$"

    if re.match(pattern, gstin_value):
        return gstin_value

    return "Not available"


def normalize_extracted_data(data):
    normalized = {}

    for key in FIELD_KEYS:
        normalized[key] = clean_text(data.get(key, "Not available"))

    normalized["product_serial_number"] = clean_product_serial_number(
        normalized.get("product_serial_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["customer_phone_number"] = clean_customer_phone_number(
        normalized.get("customer_phone_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["dealer_gst_number"] = clean_gstin(
        normalized.get("dealer_gst_number", "Not available")
    )

    return normalized

# =========================================================
# TARGETED SERIAL EXTRACTION
# =========================================================
def extract_serial_only(image_b64):
    try:
        response = client.chat.completions.create(
            model=MODEL_NAME,
            temperature=0,
            max_tokens=500,
            response_format={"type": "json_object"},
            messages=[
                {
                    "role": "user",
                    "content": [
                        {"type": "text", "text": SERIAL_ONLY_PROMPT},
                        {
                            "type": "image_url",
                            "image_url": {
                                "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_b64}"
                            }
                        }
                    ]
                }
            ]
        )

        raw = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)
        serial = raw.get("product_serial_number", "Not available")

        return clean_product_serial_number(serial)

    except Exception:
        return "Not available"

# =========================================================
# PROCESS IMAGE
# =========================================================
def process_image(image_path):
    backoff = INITIAL_BACKOFF

    for attempt in range(1, MAX_RETRIES + 1):
        try:
            processed_img = resize_image(image_path)
            image_b64 = encode_image(processed_img)

            response = client.chat.completions.create(
                model=MODEL_NAME,
                temperature=0,
                max_tokens=3000,
                response_format={"type": "json_object"},
                messages=[
                    {
                        "role": "user",
                        "content": [
                            {"type": "text", "text": INVOICE_PROMPT},
                            {
                                "type": "image_url",
                                "image_url": {
                                    "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_b64}"
                                }
                            }
                        ]
                    }
                ]
            )

            raw_data = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)

            # =====================================================
            # MULTI-INVOICE SAFE HANDLING
            # =====================================================
            if "invoices" in raw_data and isinstance(raw_data["invoices"], list):

                invoices = raw_data["invoices"]
                merged_data = {k: [] for k in FIELD_KEYS}

                for inv in invoices:
                    inv = normalize_extracted_data(inv)

                    for key in FIELD_KEYS:
                        value = inv.get(key, "Not available")
                        if value and value != "Not available":
                            merged_data[key].append(str(value))

                data = {}

                for key in FIELD_KEYS:
                    if merged_data[key]:
                        if key == "product_serial_number":
                            data[key] = clean_product_serial_number(
                                "^".join(merged_data[key])
                            )
                        elif key == "customer_phone_number":
                            data[key] = clean_customer_phone_number(
                                "^".join(merged_data[key])
                            )
                        else:
                            data[key] = ", ".join(merged_data[key])
                    else:
                        data[key] = "Not available"

            else:
                data = normalize_extracted_data(raw_data)

            # =====================================================
            # SECOND PASS ONLY IF SERIAL NOT FOUND
            # =====================================================
            if data.get("product_serial_number", "Not available") == "Not available":
                serial_second_pass = extract_serial_only(image_b64)
                data["product_serial_number"] = serial_second_pass

            data["file_name"] = os.path.basename(image_path)

            print(f"Processed: {data['file_name']}")
            return data

        except Exception as e:
            if attempt == MAX_RETRIES:
                print(f"Failed after retries: {os.path.basename(image_path)} | Error: {e}")
                break

            print(f"Retry {attempt}/{MAX_RETRIES} for {os.path.basename(image_path)}")
            time.sleep(backoff)
            backoff *= 2

    err_row = {k: "Error" for k in FIELD_KEYS}
    err_row["file_name"] = os.path.basename(image_path)
    return err_row

# =========================================================
# MAIN EXECUTION - IMAGE EXTRACTION
# =========================================================
all_images = [
    os.path.join(IMAGE_FOLDER, f)
    for f in os.listdir(IMAGE_FOLDER)
    if f.lower().endswith((".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png"))
]

print(f"Total images: {len(all_images)}")

results = []

with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=MAX_WORKERS) as executor:
    futures = [executor.submit(process_image, img) for img in all_images]

    for future in as_completed(futures):
        results.append(future.result())

df = pd.DataFrame(results)

# =========================================================
# SAVE PICKLE

os.makedirs(OUTPUT_PKL_FOLDER, exist_ok=True)

timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")

full_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_PKL_FOLDER, pkl_file_name)

df.to_pickle(full_path)

print(f"Pickle File saved at: {full_path}")
print("Exact Columns:", df.columns.tolist())
print("IMAGE EXTRACTION COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")
