# =========================================================
# EXTRACT IDs FROM FILE NAME
# =========================================================
def extract_ids(file_name):
    try:
        file_name = str(file_name)

        # Split on ^
        main_part, rest = file_name.split("^")

        # Extract header_crm_id and sr_id
        header_crm_id, sr_id = main_part.split("_")

        # Extract attch_id (before next _)
        attch_id = rest.split("_")[0]

        return header_crm_id, sr_id, attch_id

    except Exception:
        return None, None, None


# Apply to dataframe
df["header_crm_id"], df["sr_id"], df["attch_id"] = zip(
    *df["file_name"].apply(extract_ids)
)
# =========================================================
# MERGE WITH BASE TABLE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    df,
    base_data,
    on=["header_crm_id", "sr_id"],
    how="left"
)

merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print("Merge completed")



# =========================================================
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS
# =========================================================
TABLE_NAME = "p_unst_str_customer_invoice"
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"   # insert | upsert

create_table_query = f"""
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {TABLE_NAME} (

    id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,

    header_crm_id VARCHAR(50),
    sr_id VARCHAR(50),
    attch_id VARCHAR(50),

    sr_open_date DATETIME,
    sr_closed_date DATETIME,

    file_name TEXT,
    invoice_number VARCHAR(255),
    product_serial_number VARCHAR(255),
    date_of_purchase VARCHAR(255),

    dealer_name TEXT,
    dealer_gst_number VARCHAR(255),
    dealer_address TEXT,

    customer_name TEXT,
    customer_address TEXT,
    customer_phone_number VARCHAR(255),

    UNIQUE KEY uniq_invoice (
        header_crm_id,
        sr_id,
        attch_id
    )
)
"""

cursor.execute(create_table_query)
conn.commit()

# =========================================================
# PREPARE DATA
# =========================================================
insert_cols = [
    "header_crm_id",
    "sr_id",
    "attch_id",
    "sr_open_date",
    "sr_closed_date",
    "file_name",
    "invoice_number",
    "product_serial_number",
    "date_of_purchase",
    "dealer_name",
    "dealer_gst_number",
    "dealer_address",
    "customer_name",
    "customer_address",
    "customer_phone_number"
]

for col in insert_cols:
    if col not in merged_df.columns:
        merged_df[col] = None

records = merged_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

# =========================================================
# GENERATE INSERT / UPSERT SQL
# =========================================================
placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

if WRITE_MODE.lower() == "upsert":

    update_cols = [
        c for c in insert_cols
        if c not in ["header_crm_id", "sr_id", "attch_id"]
    ]

    update_sql = ", ".join(
        [f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols]
    )

    insert_sql = f"""
    INSERT INTO {TABLE_NAME} ({col_list})
    VALUES ({placeholders})
    ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE
    {update_sql}
    """

else:

    insert_sql = f"""
    INSERT IGNORE INTO {TABLE_NAME} ({col_list})
    VALUES ({placeholders})
    """

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT / UPSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH_SIZE = 500
DB_MAX_RETRIES = 5

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH_SIZE):

    batch = records[i:i + BATCH_SIZE]

    for attempt in range(DB_MAX_RETRIES):

        try:

            cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
            conn.commit()

            print(
                f"{WRITE_MODE.upper()} : "
                f"{i} to {min(i + len(batch), len(records))}"
            )

            break

        except Exception as e:

            error_text = str(e)

            if "1205" in error_text:

                print(
                    f"Lock detected. Retry "
                    f"{attempt + 1}/{DB_MAX_RETRIES}"
                )

                time.sleep(2)

            else:

                conn.rollback()

                print(
                    f"Database error in batch "
                    f"starting at row {i}: {e}"
                )

                break

# =========================================================
# CLOSE CONNECTION
# =========================================================
cursor.close()
conn.close()

print(f"{WRITE_MODE.upper()} COMPLETED")
print("FULL PIPELINE COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")

INVOICE_PROMPT = """
You are a highly accurate invoice data extraction system specialized in
CUSTOMER INVOICES submitted to VOLTAS for WARRANTY CLAIMS.

Extract only the required fields from the invoice image and return STRICT JSON ONLY.

============================================================
GLOBAL RULES
============================================================
1. Output ENGLISH ONLY.
2. Do NOT hallucinate.
3. Do NOT guess or infer values.
4. Extract only values clearly visible in the invoice image.
5. If any value is not clearly visible, return "Not available".
6. Return JSON only. No markdown. No explanation. No comments.
7. Dates must be returned in YYYY-MM-DD format.
8. If only partial date is visible, return "Not available".
9. Phone numbers must contain digits only.
10. Addresses must be single-line comma-separated text.
11. Remove extra spaces, line breaks, and unnecessary punctuation.
12. If multiple invoices are present in one image, return:
    {
      "invoices": [
        { same schema },
        { same schema }
      ]
    }

============================================================
MOST IMPORTANT FIELD: product_serial_number
============================================================
Product serial number is VERY CRITICAL.

Definition of a valid product serial number:
- Alphanumeric only (uppercase letters A-Z and digits 0-9).
- Length must be greater than 14 characters.
- Must contain at least one digit.
- Must NOT contain spaces, slashes, dashes, dots, commas, colons, or any special characters inside.
- Usually starts with digits and ends with digits.
- May contain uppercase letters in between.

Where to look (very important):
- Product serial number is mostly present with the item name or product description.
- It is often written immediately after the product name, item name, or model description.
- It may also appear in the line-item table, in the description column,
  or as a standalone alphanumeric token near the product details.
- LABEL IS NOT MANDATORY:
    The serial number may appear WITHOUT any label like "S.No", "Sr No",
    "Serial No", "S/N", etc. It can simply be printed next to or below the
    item name as a standalone alphanumeric value.
- If a label is present, common labels include:
  Serial No, Sr No, Sr.No, S.No, S No, SR NO, S/N, SN,
  Product Serial No, Product Sr No, Machine No, Unit Serial No,
  Barcode, IDU SR NO, ODU SR NO, Indoor Serial No, Outdoor Serial No.
- Even if no label is present, treat any standalone alphanumeric token
  matching the format rules (length > 14, alphanumeric, contains digits)
  near the item/product description as the product serial number.

Multiple serial numbers:
- A customer may buy multiple products in the same invoice.
- Therefore, multiple product serial numbers may be present.
- Extract ALL valid product serial numbers.
- Join multiple valid product serial numbers using "^" with no spaces.

Strict exclusions — do NOT extract these as product_serial_number:
- Model number / model code (e.g., short codes printed in the model column)
- Item code / SKU
- HSN code / SAC code
- GSTIN (15-char taxpayer ID)
- Invoice number / Bill number / Receipt number
- Customer or dealer mobile/phone number
- Quantity / Rate / Amount / Discount values
- Date values
- PIN code

If no valid product serial number is visible, return "Not available".

============================================================
FIELD RULES
============================================================

invoice_number:
- Extract invoice number / bill number / tax invoice number.
- Look for labels such as Invoice No, Bill No, Tax Invoice No, Inv No, Receipt No.
- Keep slashes and dashes if printed.
- Do not confuse with GSTIN, product serial number, model number, HSN, or phone number.

product_serial_number:
- Extract as per the rules above.
- Multiple serials must be separated using "^".

date_of_purchase:
- Extract date ONLY from the actual invoice / bill / tax invoice section.
- Valid sources: Invoice Date, Bill Date, Tax Invoice Date, Purchase Date,
  or the date printed near Invoice No / Bill No / Tax Invoice No,
  or the date in the invoice header / invoice details block.
- STRICTLY IGNORE any date printed at the bottom / footer of the page
  that appears along with latitude, longitude, GPS coordinates,
  geo location, "Printed On", "Generated On", "Downloaded On",
  "Captured On", "Uploaded On", scan date, or system date.
- If the ONLY date visible is near latitude / longitude / GPS / geo stamp
  / footer system print, return "Not available".
- If both invoice date and footer/geo date are visible, return ONLY the invoice date.
- Convert to YYYY-MM-DD.
- Do not use due date, delivery date, warranty date, or print date.

dealer_name:
- Extract seller / dealer / shop / vendor business name.
- Usually present at the top/header of invoice.
- The dealer name MUST NOT contain the word "Voltas".
- Do NOT return "Voltas", "Voltas Limited", "Voltas Ltd", or any name
  that contains the word "Voltas" in it. In such case return "Not available".
- Do not extract customer name.

dealer_gst_number:
- Extract dealer GSTIN only.
- GSTIN is exactly 15 characters.
- Pick seller/dealer GSTIN, usually in header.
- Do not pick customer GSTIN if both are present.

dealer_address:
- Extract full dealer/seller address from header area.
- Do not mix with customer address.

customer_name:
- Extract buyer/customer name.
- Look near Bill To, Buyer, Customer Name, Sold To, Party Name, Ship To, Consignee.
- Prefer Bill To / Buyer if both Bill To and Ship To are present.
- Do not extract dealer name.

customer_address:
- Extract full customer/buyer address.
- Look near customer name, Bill To, Buyer, Consignee, or Ship To block.
- Do not extract dealer address.

customer_phone_number:
- Extract customer phone/mobile/contact number only.
- Customer phone number may be multiple.
- Multiple numbers may be separated by "/", ",", "&", "|", "and", or "or".
- Extract all customer phone numbers.
- Digits only.
- Join multiple phone numbers using "^" with no spaces.
- Do not extract dealer phone number.

============================================================
OUTPUT JSON SCHEMA
============================================================
{
  "invoice_number": "string",
  "product_serial_number": "string",
  "date_of_purchase": "string",
  "dealer_name": "string",
  "dealer_gst_number": "string",
  "dealer_address": "string",
  "customer_name": "string",
  "customer_address": "string",
  "customer_phone_number": "string"
}

Return JSON only.
"""

SERIAL_ONLY_PROMPT = """
Extract only the product serial number from this Voltas warranty invoice image.

Rules:
- Product serial number is mostly present with the item name or product description.
- It is often written immediately after the product name or model description.
- It may appear WITHOUT any label like "S.No", "Sr No", "Serial No", etc.
- Even an unlabeled standalone alphanumeric token near the product details
  should be considered if it matches the format rules below.
- Product serial number is alphanumeric only.
- Length must be greater than 14 characters.
- Must contain at least one digit.
- No spaces, slashes, dashes, dots, commas, or special characters inside.
- Extract ALL valid serial numbers.
- If multiple serial numbers are present, join them using "^" with no spaces.
- Do not extract HSN code, GSTIN, invoice number, model number, phone number,
  amount, quantity, rate, or date as a serial number.
- If no valid serial number is visible, return "Not available".

Return JSON only:
{
  "product_serial_number": "string"
}
"""

# =========================================================
# FIELD KEYS
# =========================================================
FIELD_KEYS = [
    "invoice_number",
    "product_serial_number",
    "date_of_purchase",
    "dealer_name",
    "dealer_gst_number",
    "dealer_address",
    "customer_name",
    "customer_address",
    "customer_phone_number"
]

# =========================================================
# IMAGE HELPERS
# =========================================================
def resize_image(image_path, max_size=2048):
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        if max(img.size) <= max_size:
            return image_path

        ratio = max_size / max(img.size)
        new_size = (int(img.size[0] * ratio), int(img.size[1] * ratio))

        temp_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()
        temp_path = os.path.join(temp_dir, os.path.basename(image_path))

        img.resize(new_size, Image.LANCZOS).save(temp_path)
        return temp_path


def encode_image(image_path):
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        img = img.convert("RGB")
        buffer = BytesIO()
        img.save(buffer, format="JPEG")
        return base64.b64encode(buffer.getvalue()).decode()

# =========================================================
# CLEANERS / VALIDATORS
# =========================================================
def clean_text(value):
    if value is None:
        return "Not available"

    value = str(value).strip()

    if value == "" or value.lower() in ["none", "null", "nan", "not available"]:
        return "Not available"

    value = re.sub(r"[\r\n\t]+", " ", value)
    value = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", value).strip()

    return value


def is_valid_product_serial(serial):
    """
    Valid product serial:
    - Alphanumeric only (A-Z, 0-9)
    - Length > 14
    - Must contain at least one digit
    """
    if not serial:
        return False

    serial = str(serial).strip().upper()

    if len(serial) <= 14:
        return False

    if not re.match(r"^[A-Z0-9]+$", serial):
        return False

    if not re.search(r"[0-9]", serial):
        return False

    return True


def clean_product_serial_number(serial_value):
    """
    Extract and keep only valid product serial numbers.
    Multiple valid serial numbers are returned using ^ separator.
    """
    if serial_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    serial_value = str(serial_value).upper().strip()

    if serial_value in ["", "NOT AVAILABLE", "ERROR", "NONE", "NULL", "NAN"]:
        return "Not available"

    valid_serials = []

    # Split by common separators including ^
    chunks = re.split(r"[\^,;/|&\s]+", serial_value)

    for chunk in chunks:
        compact = re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", chunk)

        if is_valid_product_serial(compact):
            if compact not in valid_serials:
                valid_serials.append(compact)

    # Fallback regex scan over raw text
    if not valid_serials:
        candidates = re.findall(r"[A-Z0-9]{15,30}", serial_value)
        for cand in candidates:
            if is_valid_product_serial(cand) and cand not in valid_serials:
                valid_serials.append(cand)

    if valid_serials:
        return "^".join(valid_serials)

    return "Not available"


def clean_customer_phone_number(phone_value):
    if phone_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    phone_value = str(phone_value).strip()

    if phone_value == "" or phone_value.lower() in ["not available", "error", "none", "null", "nan"]:
        return "Not available"

    parts = re.split(r"[\^/,;&|]|\band\b|\bor\b", phone_value, flags=re.IGNORECASE)

    final_numbers = []

    for part in parts:
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)

        if not digits:
            continue

        if len(digits) == 12 and digits.startswith("91"):
            digits = digits[-10:]
        elif len(digits) == 11 and digits.startswith("0"):
            digits = digits[-10:]

        if len(digits) == 10 and digits[0] in ["6", "7", "8", "9"]:
            if digits not in final_numbers:
                final_numbers.append(digits)

    if final_numbers:
        return "^".join(final_numbers)

    return "Not available"


def clean_gstin(gstin_value):
    if gstin_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    gstin_value = str(gstin_value).upper().strip()
    gstin_value = re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", gstin_value)

    pattern = r"^[0-9]{2}[A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z][1-9A-Z]Z[0-9A-Z]$"

    if re.match(pattern, gstin_value):
        return gstin_value

    return "Not available"


def clean_dealer_name(dealer_value):
    """
    Dealer name must NOT contain the word 'Voltas'.
    If it contains 'Voltas', treat as invalid and return 'Not available'.
    """
    dealer_value = clean_text(dealer_value)

    if dealer_value == "Not available":
        return "Not available"

    if re.search(r"\bvoltas\b", dealer_value, flags=re.IGNORECASE):
        return "Not available"

    return dealer_value


def normalize_extracted_data(data):
    normalized = {}

    for key in FIELD_KEYS:
        normalized[key] = clean_text(data.get(key, "Not available"))

    normalized["product_serial_number"] = clean_product_serial_number(
        normalized.get("product_serial_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["customer_phone_number"] = clean_customer_phone_number(
        normalized.get("customer_phone_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["dealer_gst_number"] = clean_gstin(
        normalized.get("dealer_gst_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["dealer_name"] = clean_dealer_name(
        normalized.get("dealer_name", "Not available")
    )

    return normalized

# =========================================================
# TARGETED SERIAL EXTRACTION
# =========================================================
def extract_serial_only(image_b64):
    try:
        response = client.chat.completions.create(
            model=MODEL_NAME,
            temperature=0,
            max_tokens=500,
            response_format={"type": "json_object"},
            messages=[
                {
                    "role": "user",
                    "content": [
                        {"type": "text", "text": SERIAL_ONLY_PROMPT},
                        {
                            "type": "image_url",
                            "image_url": {
                                "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_b64}"
                            }
                        }
                    ]
                }
            ]
        )

        raw = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)
        serial = raw.get("product_serial_number", "Not available")

        return clean_product_serial_number(serial)

    except Exception:
        return "Not available"

# =========================================================
# PROCESS IMAGE
# =========================================================
def process_image(image_path):
    backoff = INITIAL_BACKOFF

    for attempt in range(1, MAX_RETRIES + 1):
        try:
            processed_img = resize_image(image_path)
            image_b64 = encode_image(processed_img)

            response = client.chat.completions.create(
                model=MODEL_NAME,
                temperature=0,
                max_tokens=3000,
                response_format={"type": "json_object"},
                messages=[
                    {
                        "role": "user",
                        "content": [
                            {"type": "text", "text": INVOICE_PROMPT},
                            {
                                "type": "image_url",
                                "image_url": {
                                    "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_b64}"
                                }
                            }
                        ]
                    }
                ]
            )

            raw_data = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)

            # =====================================================
            # MULTI-INVOICE SAFE HANDLING
            # =====================================================
            if "invoices" in raw_data and isinstance(raw_data["invoices"], list):

                invoices = raw_data["invoices"]
                merged_data = {k: [] for k in FIELD_KEYS}

                for inv in invoices:
                    inv = normalize_extracted_data(inv)

                    for key in FIELD_KEYS:
                        value = inv.get(key, "Not available")
                        if value and value != "Not available":
                            merged_data[key].append(str(value))

                data = {}

                for key in FIELD_KEYS:
                    if merged_dataif key == "product_serial_number":
                            data[key] = clean_product_serial_number(
                                "^".join(merged_data[key])
                            )
                        elif key == "customer_phone_number":
                            data[key] = clean_customer_phone_number(
                                "^".join(merged_data[key])
                            )
                        else:
                            data[key] = ", ".join(merged_data[key])
                    else:
                        data[key] = "Not available"

                # Re-apply dealer cleaner to merged value as well
                data["dealer_name"] = clean_dealer_name(
                    data.get("dealer_name", "Not available")
                )

            else:
                data = normalize_extracted_data(raw_data)

            # =====================================================
            # SECOND PASS ONLY IF SERIAL NOT FOUND
            # =====================================================
            if data.get("product_serial_number", "Not available") == "Not available":
                serial_second_pass = extract_serial_only(image_b64)
                data["product_serial_number"] = serial_second_pass

            data["file_name"] = os.path.basename(image_path)

            print(f"Processed: {data['file_name']}")
            return data

        except Exception as e:
            if attempt == MAX_RETRIES:
                print(f"Failed after retries: {os.path.basename(image_path)} | Error: {e}")
                break

            print(f"Retry {attempt}/{MAX_RETRIES} for {os.path.basename(image_path)}")
            time.sleep(backoff)
            backoff *= 2

    err_row = {k: "Error" for k in FIELD_KEYS}
    err_row["file_name"] = os.path.basename(image_path)
    return err_row

# =========================================================
# MAIN EXECUTION - IMAGE EXTRACTION
# =========================================================
all_images = [
    os.path.join(IMAGE_FOLDER, f)
    for f in os.listdir(IMAGE_FOLDER)
    if f.lower().endswith((".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png"))
]

print(f"Total images: {len(all_images)}")

results = []

with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=MAX_WORKERS) as executor:
    futures = [executor.submit(process_image, img) for img in all_images]

    for future in as_completed(futures):
        results.append(future.result())

df = pd.DataFrame(results)

# =========================================================
# SAVE PICKLE
# =========================================================
os.makedirs(OUTPUT_PKL_FOLDER, exist_ok=True)

timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
pkl_file_name = f"output_voltas_warranty_{timestamp}.pkl"
full_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_PKL_FOLDER, pkl_file_name)

df.to_pickle(full_path)

print(f"Pickle File saved at: {full_path}")
print("Exact Columns:", df.columns.tolist())
print("IMAGE EXTRACTION COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")

# =========================================================
# EXTRACT IDs FROM FILE NAME
# =========================================================
def extract_ids(file_name):
    try:
        file_name = str(file_name)

        # Split on ^
        main_part, rest = file_name.split("^")

        # Extract header_crm_id and sr_id
        header_crm_id, sr_id = main_part.split("_")

        # Extract attch_id (before next _)
        attch_id = rest.split("_")[0]

        return header_crm_id, sr_id, attch_id

    except Exception:
        return None, None, None


# Apply to dataframe
df["header_crm_id"], df["sr_id"], df["attch_id"] = zip(
    *df["file_name"].apply(extract_ids)
)

# =========================================================
# MERGE WITH BASE TABLE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    df,
    base_data,
    on=["header_crm_id", "sr_id"],
    how="left"
)

merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print("Merge completed")

# =========================================================
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS
# =========================================================
TABLE_NAME = "p_unst_str_customer_invoice"
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"   # insert | upsert

create_table_query = f"""
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {TABLE_NAME} (

    id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,

    header_crm_id VARCHAR(50),
    sr_id VARCHAR(50),
    attch_id VARCHAR(50),

    sr_open_date DATETIME,
    sr_closed_date DATETIME,

    file_name TEXT,
    invoice_number VARCHAR(255),
    product_serial_number VARCHAR(255),
    date_of_purchase VARCHAR(255),

    dealer_name TEXT,
    dealer_gst_number VARCHAR(255),
    dealer_address TEXT,

    customer_name TEXT,
    customer_address TEXT,
    customer_phone_number VARCHAR(255),

    UNIQUE KEY uniq_invoice (
        header_crm_id,
        sr_id,
        attch_id
    )
)
"""

cursor.execute(create_table_query)
conn.commit()

# =========================================================
# PREPARE DATA
# =========================================================
insert_cols = [
    "header_crm_id",
    "sr_id",
    "attch_id",
    "sr_open_date",
    "sr_closed_date",
    "file_name",
    "invoice_number",
    "product_serial_number",
    "date_of_purchase",
    "dealer_name",
    "dealer_gst_number",
    "dealer_address",
    "customer_name",
    "customer_address",
    "customer_phone_number"
]

for col in insert_cols:
    if col not in merged_df.columns:
        merged_df[col] = None

records = merged_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

# =========================================================
# GENERATE INSERT / UPSERT SQL
# =========================================================
placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

if WRITE_MODE.lower() == "upsert":

    update_cols = [
        c for c in insert_cols
        if c not in ["header_crm_id", "sr_id", "attch_id"]
    ]

    update_sql = ", ".join(
        [f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols]
    )

    insert_sql = f"""
    INSERT INTO {TABLE_NAME} ({col_list})
    VALUES ({placeholders})
    ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE
    {update_sql}
    """

else:

    insert_sql = f"""
    INSERT IGNORE INTO {TABLE_NAME} ({col_list})
    VALUES ({placeholders})
    """

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT / UPSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH_SIZE = 500
DB_MAX_RETRIES = 5

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH_SIZE):

    batch = records[i:i + BATCH_SIZE]

    for attempt in range(DB_MAX_RETRIES):

        try:

            cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
            conn.commit()

            print(
                f"{WRITE_MODE.upper()} : "
                f"{i} to {min(i + len(batch), len(records))}"
            )

            break

        except Exception as e:

            error_text = str(e)

            if "1205" in error_text:

                print(
                    f"Lock detected. Retry "
                    f"{attempt + 1}/{DB_MAX_RETRIES}"
                )

                time.sleep(2)

            else:

                conn.rollback()

                print(
                    f"Database error in batch "
                    f"starting at row {i}: {e}"
                )

                break

# =========================================================
# CLOSE CONNECTION
# =========================================================
cursor.close()
conn.close()

print(f"{WRITE_MODE.upper()} COMPLETED")
print("FULL PIPELINE COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")

INVOICE_PROMPT = """
You are a highly accurate invoice data extraction system specialized in
CUSTOMER INVOICES submitted to VOLTAS for WARRANTY CLAIMS.

Extract only the required fields from the invoice image and return STRICT JSON ONLY.

============================================================
GLOBAL RULES
============================================================
1. Output ENGLISH ONLY.
2. Do NOT hallucinate.
3. Do NOT guess or infer values.
4. Extract only values clearly visible in the invoice image.
5. If any value is not clearly visible, return "Not available".
6. Return JSON only. No markdown. No explanation. No comments.
7. Dates must be returned in YYYY-MM-DD format.
8. If only partial date is visible, return "Not available".
9. Phone numbers must contain digits only.
10. Addresses must be single-line comma-separated text.
11. Remove extra spaces, line breaks, and unnecessary punctuation.
12. If multiple invoices are present in one image, return:
    {
      "invoices": [
        { same schema },
        { same schema }
      ]
    }

============================================================
MOST IMPORTANT FIELD: product_serial_number
============================================================
Product serial number is VERY CRITICAL.

Definition of a valid product serial number:
- Alphanumeric only (uppercase letters A-Z and digits 0-9).
- Length must be greater than 14 characters.
- Must contain at least one digit.
- Must NOT contain spaces, slashes, dashes, dots, commas, colons, or any special characters inside.
- Usually starts with digits and ends with digits.
- May contain uppercase letters in between.

Where to look (very important):
- Product serial number is mostly present with the item name or product description.
- It is often written immediately after the product name, item name, or model description.
- It may also appear in the line-item table, in the description column,
  or as a standalone alphanumeric token near the product details.
- LABEL IS NOT MANDATORY:
    The serial number may appear WITHOUT any label like "S.No", "Sr No",
    "Serial No", "S/N", etc. It can simply be printed next to or below the
    item name as a standalone alphanumeric value.
- If a label is present, common labels include:
  Serial No, Sr No, Sr.No, S.No, S No, SR NO, S/N, SN,
  Product Serial No, Product Sr No, Machine No, Unit Serial No,
  Barcode, IDU SR NO, ODU SR NO, Indoor Serial No, Outdoor Serial No.
- Even if no label is present, treat any standalone alphanumeric token
  matching the format rules (length > 14, alphanumeric, contains digits)
  near the item/product description as the product serial number.

Multiple serial numbers:
- A customer may buy multiple products in the same invoice.
- Therefore, multiple product serial numbers may be present.
- Extract ALL valid product serial numbers.
- Join multiple valid product serial numbers using "^" with no spaces.

Strict exclusions — do NOT extract these as product_serial_number:
- Model number / model code (e.g., short codes printed in the model column)
- Item code / SKU
- HSN code / SAC code
- GSTIN (15-char taxpayer ID)
- Invoice number / Bill number / Receipt number
- Customer or dealer mobile/phone number
- Quantity / Rate / Amount / Discount values
- Date values
- PIN code

If no valid product serial number is visible, return "Not available".

============================================================
FIELD RULES
============================================================

invoice_number:
- Extract invoice number / bill number / tax invoice number.
- Look for labels such as Invoice No, Bill No, Tax Invoice No, Inv No, Receipt No.
- Keep slashes and dashes if printed.
- Do not confuse with GSTIN, product serial number, model number, HSN, or phone number.

product_serial_number:
- Extract as per the rules above.
- Multiple serials must be separated using "^".

date_of_purchase:
- Extract date ONLY from the actual invoice / bill / tax invoice section.
- Valid sources: Invoice Date, Bill Date, Tax Invoice Date, Purchase Date,
  or the date printed near Invoice No / Bill No / Tax Invoice No,
  or the date in the invoice header / invoice details block.
- STRICTLY IGNORE any date printed at the bottom / footer of the page
  that appears along with latitude, longitude, GPS coordinates,
  geo location, "Printed On", "Generated On", "Downloaded On",
  "Captured On", "Uploaded On", scan date, or system date.
- If the ONLY date visible is near latitude / longitude / GPS / geo stamp
  / footer system print, return "Not available".
- If both invoice date and footer/geo date are visible, return ONLY the invoice date.
- Convert to YYYY-MM-DD.
- Do not use due date, delivery date, warranty date, or print date.

dealer_name:
- Extract seller / dealer / shop / vendor business name.
- Usually present at the top/header of invoice.
- The dealer name MUST NOT contain the word "Voltas".
- Do NOT return "Voltas", "Voltas Limited", "Voltas Ltd", or any name
  that contains the word "Voltas" in it. In such case return "Not available".
- Do not extract customer name.

dealer_gst_number:
- Extract dealer GSTIN only.
- GSTIN is exactly 15 characters.
- Pick seller/dealer GSTIN, usually in header.
- Do not pick customer GSTIN if both are present.

dealer_address:
- Extract full dealer/seller address from header area.
- Do not mix with customer address.

customer_name:
- Extract buyer/customer name.
- Look near Bill To, Buyer, Customer Name, Sold To, Party Name, Ship To, Consignee.
- Prefer Bill To / Buyer if both Bill To and Ship To are present.
- Do not extract dealer name.

customer_address:
- Extract full customer/buyer address.
- Look near customer name, Bill To, Buyer, Consignee, or Ship To block.
- Do not extract dealer address.

customer_phone_number:
- Extract customer phone/mobile/contact number only.
- Customer phone number may be multiple.
- Multiple numbers may be separated by "/", ",", "&", "|", "and", or "or".
- Extract all customer phone numbers.
- Digits only.
- Join multiple phone numbers using "^" with no spaces.
- Do not extract dealer phone number.

============================================================
OUTPUT JSON SCHEMA
============================================================
{
  "invoice_number": "string",
  "product_serial_number": "string",
  "date_of_purchase": "string",
  "dealer_name": "string",
  "dealer_gst_number": "string",
  "dealer_address": "string",
  "customer_name": "string",
  "customer_address": "string",
  "customer_phone_number": "string"
}

Return JSON only.
"""

SERIAL_ONLY_PROMPT = """
Extract only the product serial number from this Voltas warranty invoice image.

Rules:
- Product serial number is mostly present with the item name or product description.
- It is often written immediately after the product name or model description.
- It may appear WITHOUT any label like "S.No", "Sr No", "Serial No", etc.
- Even an unlabeled standalone alphanumeric token near the product details
  should be considered if it matches the format rules below.
- Product serial number is alphanumeric only.
- Length must be greater than 14 characters.
- Must contain at least one digit.
- No spaces, slashes, dashes, dots, commas, or special characters inside.
- Extract ALL valid serial numbers.
- If multiple serial numbers are present, join them using "^" with no spaces.
- Do not extract HSN code, GSTIN, invoice number, model number, phone number,
  amount, quantity, rate, or date as a serial number.
- If no valid serial number is visible, return "Not available".

Return JSON only:
{
  "product_serial_number": "string"
}
"""

FIELD_KEYS = [
    "invoice_number",
    "product_serial_number",
    "date_of_purchase",
    "dealer_name",
    "dealer_gst_number",
    "dealer_address",
    "customer_name",
    "customer_address",
    "customer_phone_number"
]

# =========================================================
# IMAGE HELPERS
# =========================================================
def resize_image(image_path, max_size=2048):
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        if max(img.size) <= max_size:
            return image_path

        ratio = max_size / max(img.size)
        new_size = (int(img.size[0] * ratio), int(img.size[1] * ratio))

        temp_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()
        temp_path = os.path.join(temp_dir, os.path.basename(image_path))

        img.resize(new_size, Image.LANCZOS).save(temp_path)
        return temp_path


def encode_image(image_path):
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        img = img.convert("RGB")
        buffer = BytesIO()
        img.save(buffer, format="JPEG")
        return base64.b64encode(buffer.getvalue()).decode()

# =========================================================
# CLEANERS / VALIDATORS
# =========================================================
def clean_text(value):
    if value is None:
        return "Not available"

    value = str(value).strip()

    if value == "" or value.lower() in ["none", "null", "nan", "not available"]:
        return "Not available"

    value = re.sub(r"[\r\n\t]+", " ", value)
    value = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", value).strip()

    return value


def is_valid_product_serial(serial):
    """
    Valid product serial:
    - Alphanumeric only (A-Z, 0-9)
    - Length > 14
    - Must contain at least one digit
    """
    if not serial:
        return False

    serial = str(serial).strip().upper()

    if len(serial) <= 14:
        return False

    if not re.match(r"^[A-Z0-9]+$", serial):
        return False

    if not re.search(r"[0-9]", serial):
        return False

    return True


def clean_product_serial_number(serial_value):
    """
    Extract and keep only valid product serial numbers.
    Multiple valid serial numbers are returned using ^ separator.
    """
    if serial_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    serial_value = str(serial_value).upper().strip()

    if serial_value in ["", "NOT AVAILABLE", "ERROR", "NONE", "NULL", "NAN"]:
        return "Not available"

    valid_serials = []

    # Split by common separators including ^
    chunks = re.split(r"[\^,;/|&\s]+", serial_value)

    for chunk in chunks:
        compact = re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", chunk)

        if is_valid_product_serial(compact):
            if compact not in valid_serials:
                valid_serials.append(compact)

    # Fallback regex scan over raw text
    if not valid_serials:
        candidates = re.findall(r"[A-Z0-9]{15,30}", serial_value)
        for cand in candidates:
            if is_valid_product_serial(cand) and cand not in valid_serials:
                valid_serials.append(cand)

    if valid_serials:
        return "^".join(valid_serials)

    return "Not available"


def clean_customer_phone_number(phone_value):
    if phone_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    phone_value = str(phone_value).strip()

    if phone_value == "" or phone_value.lower() in ["not available", "error", "none", "null", "nan"]:
        return "Not available"

    parts = re.split(r"[\^/,;&|]|\band\b|\bor\b", phone_value, flags=re.IGNORECASE)

    final_numbers = []

    for part in parts:
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)

        if not digits:
            continue

        if len(digits) == 12 and digits.startswith("91"):
            digits = digits[-10:]
        elif len(digits) == 11 and digits.startswith("0"):
            digits = digits[-10:]

        if len(digits) == 10 and digits[0] in ["6", "7", "8", "9"]:
            if digits not in final_numbers:
                final_numbers.append(digits)

    if final_numbers:
        return "^".join(final_numbers)

    return "Not available"


def clean_gstin(gstin_value):
    if gstin_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    gstin_value = str(gstin_value).upper().strip()
    gstin_value = re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", gstin_value)

    pattern = r"^[0-9]{2}[A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z][1-9A-Z]Z[0-9A-Z]$"

    if re.match(pattern, gstin_value):
        return gstin_value

    return "Not available"


def clean_dealer_name(dealer_value):
    """
    Dealer name must NOT contain the word 'Voltas'.
    If it contains 'Voltas', treat as invalid and return 'Not available'.
    """
    dealer_value = clean_text(dealer_value)

    if dealer_value == "Not available":
        return "Not available"

    if re.search(r"\bvoltas\b", dealer_value, flags=re.IGNORECASE):
        return "Not available"

    return dealer_value


def normalize_extracted_data(data):
    normalized = {}

    for key in FIELD_KEYS:
        normalized[key] = clean_text(data.get(key, "Not available"))

    normalized["product_serial_number"] = clean_product_serial_number(
        normalized.get("product_serial_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["customer_phone_number"] = clean_customer_phone_number(
        normalized.get("customer_phone_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["dealer_gst_number"] = clean_gstin(
        normalized.get("dealer_gst_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["dealer_name"] = clean_dealer_name(
        normalized.get("dealer_name", "Not available")
    )

    return normalized

# =========================================================
# TARGETED SERIAL EXTRACTION
# =========================================================
def extract_serial_only(image_b64):
    try:
        response = client.chat.completions.create(
            model=MODEL_NAME,
            temperature=0,
            max_tokens=500,
            response_format={"type": "json_object"},
            messages=[
                {
                    "role": "user",
                    "content": [
                        {"type": "text", "text": SERIAL_ONLY_PROMPT},
                        {
                            "type": "image_url",
                            "image_url": {
                                "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_b64}"
                            }
                        }
                    ]
                }
            ]
        )

        raw = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)
        serial = raw.get("product_serial_number", "Not available")

        return clean_product_serial_number(serial)

    except Exception:
        return "Not available"

# =========================================================
# PROCESS IMAGE
# =========================================================
def process_image(image_path):
    backoff = INITIAL_BACKOFF

    for attempt in range(1, MAX_RETRIES + 1):
        try:
            processed_img = resize_image(image_path)
            image_b64 = encode_image(processed_img)

            response = client.chat.completions.create(
                model=MODEL_NAME,
                temperature=0,
                max_tokens=3000,
                response_format={"type": "json_object"},
                messages=[
                    {
                        "role": "user",
                        "content": [
                            {"type": "text", "text": INVOICE_PROMPT},
                            {
                                "type": "image_url",
                                "image_url": {
                                    "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_b64}"
                                }
                            }
                        ]
                    }
                ]
            )

            raw_data = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)

            # =====================================================
            # MULTI-INVOICE SAFE HANDLING
            # =====================================================
            if "invoices" in raw_data and isinstance(raw_data["invoices"], list):

                invoices = raw_data["invoices"]
                merged_data = {k: [] for k in FIELD_KEYS}

                for inv in invoices:
                    inv = normalize_extracted_data(inv)

                    for key in FIELD_KEYS:
                        value = inv.get(key, "Not available")
                        if value and value != "Not available":
                            merged_data[key].append(str(value))

                data = {}

                for key in FIELD_KEYS:
                    if merged_dataif key == "product_serial_number":
                            data[key] = clean_product_serial_number(
                                "^".join(merged_data[key])
                            )
                        elif key == "customer_phone_number":
                            data[key] = clean_customer_phone_number(
                                "^".join(merged_data[key])
                            )
                        else:
                            data[key] = ", ".join(merged_data[key])
                    else:
                        data[key] = "Not available"

                # Re-apply dealer cleaner to merged value as well
                data["dealer_name"] = clean_dealer_name(
                    data.get("dealer_name", "Not available")
                )

            else:
                data = normalize_extracted_data(raw_data)

            # =====================================================
            # SECOND PASS ONLY IF SERIAL NOT FOUND
            # =====================================================
            if data.get("product_serial_number", "Not available") == "Not available":
                serial_second_pass = extract_serial_only(image_b64)
                data["product_serial_number"] = serial_second_pass

            data["file_name"] = os.path.basename(image_path)

            print(f"Processed: {data['file_name']}")
            return data

        except Exception as e:
            if attempt == MAX_RETRIES:
                print(f"Failed after retries: {os.path.basename(image_path)} | Error: {e}")
                break

            print(f"Retry {attempt}/{MAX_RETRIES} for {os.path.basename(image_path)}")
            time.sleep(backoff)
            backoff *= 2

    err_row = {k: "Error" for k in FIELD_KEYS}
    err_row["file_name"] = os.path.basename(image_path)
    return err_row

# =========================================================
# MAIN EXECUTION - IMAGE EXTRACTION
# =========================================================
all_images = [
    os.path.join(IMAGE_FOLDER, f)
    for f in os.listdir(IMAGE_FOLDER)
    if f.lower().endswith((".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png"))
]

print(f"Total images: {len(all_images)}")

results = []

with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=MAX_WORKERS) as executor:
    futures = [executor.submit(process_image, img) for img in all_images]

    for future in as_completed(futures):
        results.append(future.result())

df = pd.DataFrame(results)

timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")

df.to_pickle(full_path)

print(f"Pickle File saved at: {full_path}")
print("Exact Columns:", df.columns.tolist())
print("IMAGE EXTRACTION COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")

create_table_query = """
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS p_unst_str_customer_invoice (
    header_crm_id VARCHAR(50),
    sr_id VARCHAR(50),
    attch_id VARCHAR(50),
    sr_open_date DATETIME,
    sr_closed_date DATETIME,
    file_name VARCHAR(255),
    invoice_number TEXT,
    product_serial_number TEXT,
    date_of_purchase TEXT,
    dealer_name TEXT,
    dealer_gst_number VARCHAR(20),
    dealer_address TEXT,
    customer_name TEXT,
    customer_address TEXT,
    customer_phone_number TEXT
)
"""

cursor.execute(create_table_query)
conn.commit()

print("Output table ready")

# =========================================================
# EXTRACT IDs FROM FILE NAME
# =========================================================
def extract_ids(file_name):
    try:
        file_name = str(file_name)

        # Split on ^
        main_part, rest = file_name.split("^")

        # Extract header_crm_id and sr_id
        header_crm_id, sr_id = main_part.split("_")

        # Extract attch_id (before next _)
        attch_id = rest.split("_")[0]

        return header_crm_id, sr_id, attch_id

    except Exception:
        return None, None, None


# Apply to dataframe
df["header_crm_id"], df["sr_id"], df["attch_id"] = zip(
    *df["file_name"].apply(extract_ids)
)

# =========================================================
# MERGE WITH BASE TABLE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    df,
    base_data,
    on=["header_crm_id", "sr_id"],
    how="left"
)

merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print("Merge completed")

# =========================================================
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS
# =========================================================
TABLE_NAME = "p_unst_str_customer_invoice"
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"   # insert | upsert

create_table_query = f"""
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {TABLE_NAME} (

    id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,

    header_crm_id VARCHAR(50),
    sr_id VARCHAR(50),
    attch_id VARCHAR(50),

    sr_open_date DATETIME,
    sr_closed_date DATETIME,

    file_name TEXT,
    invoice_number VARCHAR(255),
    product_serial_number VARCHAR(255),
    date_of_purchase VARCHAR(255),

    dealer_name TEXT,
    dealer_gst_number VARCHAR(255),
    dealer_address TEXT,

    customer_name TEXT,
    customer_address TEXT,
    customer_phone_number VARCHAR(255),

    UNIQUE KEY uniq_invoice (
        header_crm_id,
        sr_id,
        attch_id
    )
)
"""

cursor.execute(create_table_query)
conn.commit()

# =========================================================
# PREPARE DATA
# =========================================================
insert_cols = [
    "header_crm_id",
    "sr_id",
    "attch_id",
    "sr_open_date",
    "sr_closed_date",
    "file_name",
    "invoice_number",
    "product_serial_number",
    "date_of_purchase",
    "dealer_name",
    "dealer_gst_number",
    "dealer_address",
    "customer_name",
    "customer_address",
    "customer_phone_number"
]

for col in insert_cols:
    if col not in merged_df.columns:
        merged_df[col] = None

records = merged_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

# =========================================================
# GENERATE INSERT / UPSERT SQL
# =========================================================
placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

if WRITE_MODE.lower() == "upsert":

    update_cols = [
        c for c in insert_cols
        if c not in ["header_crm_id", "sr_id", "attch_id"]
    ]

    update_sql = ", ".join(
        [f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols]
    )

    insert_sql = f"""
    INSERT INTO {TABLE_NAME} ({col_list})
    VALUES ({placeholders})
    ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE
    {update_sql}
    """

else:

    insert_sql = f"""
    INSERT IGNORE INTO {TABLE_NAME} ({col_list})
    VALUES ({placeholders})
    """

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT / UPSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH_SIZE = 500
DB_MAX_RETRIES = 5

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH_SIZE):

    batch = records[i:i + BATCH_SIZE]

    for attempt in range(DB_MAX_RETRIES):

        try:

            cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
            conn.commit()

            print(
                f"{WRITE_MODE.upper()} : "
                f"{i} to {min(i + len(batch), len(records))}"
            )

            break

        except Exception as e:

            error_text = str(e)

            if "1205" in error_text:

                print(
                    f"Lock detected. Retry "
                    f"{attempt + 1}/{DB_MAX_RETRIES}"
                )

                time.sleep(2)

            else:

                conn.rollback()

                print(
                    f"Database error in batch "
                    f"starting at row {i}: {e}"
                )

                break

# =========================================================
# CLOSE CONNECTION
# =========================================================
cursor.close()
conn.close()

print(f"{WRITE_MODE.upper()} COMPLETED")
print("FULL PIPELINE COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")

INVOICE_PROMPT = """
You are a highly accurate invoice data extraction system specialized in
CUSTOMER INVOICES submitted to VOLTAS for WARRANTY CLAIMS.

Extract only the required fields from the invoice image and return STRICT JSON ONLY.

============================================================
GLOBAL RULES
============================================================
1. Output ENGLISH ONLY.
2. Do NOT hallucinate.
3. Do NOT guess or infer values.
4. Extract only values clearly visible in the invoice image.
5. If any value is not clearly visible, return "Not available".
6. Return JSON only. No markdown. No explanation. No comments.
7. Dates must be returned in YYYY-MM-DD format.
8. If only partial date is visible, return "Not available".
9. Phone numbers must contain digits only.
10. Addresses must be single-line comma-separated text.
11. Remove extra spaces, line breaks, and unnecessary punctuation.
12. If multiple invoices are present in one image, return:
    {
      "invoices": [
        { same schema },
        { same schema }
      ]
    }

============================================================
MOST IMPORTANT FIELD: product_serial_number
============================================================
Product serial number is VERY CRITICAL.

Definition of a valid product serial number:
- Alphanumeric only (uppercase letters A-Z and digits 0-9).
- Length must be greater than 14 characters.
- Must contain at least one digit.
- Must NOT contain spaces, slashes, dashes, dots, commas, colons, or any special characters inside.
- Usually starts with digits and ends with digits.
- May contain uppercase letters in between.

Where to look (very important):
- Product serial number is mostly present with the item name or product description.
- It is often written immediately after the product name, item name, or model description.
- It may also appear in the line-item table, in the description column,
  or as a standalone alphanumeric token near the product details.
- LABEL IS NOT MANDATORY:
    The serial number may appear WITHOUT any label like "S.No", "Sr No",
    "Serial No", "S/N", etc. It can simply be printed next to or below the
    item name as a standalone alphanumeric value.
- If a label is present, common labels include:
  Serial No, Sr No, Sr.No, S.No, S No, SR NO, S/N, SN,
  Product Serial No, Product Sr No, Machine No, Unit Serial No,
  Barcode, IDU SR NO, ODU SR NO, Indoor Serial No, Outdoor Serial No.
- Even if no label is present, treat any standalone alphanumeric token
  matching the format rules (length > 14, alphanumeric, contains digits)
  near the item/product description as the product serial number.

Multiple serial numbers:
- A customer may buy multiple products in the same invoice.
- Therefore, multiple product serial numbers may be present.
- Extract ALL valid product serial numbers.
- Join multiple valid product serial numbers using "^" with no spaces.

Strict exclusions — do NOT extract these as product_serial_number:
- Model number / model code (e.g., short codes printed in the model column)
- Item code / SKU
- HSN code / SAC code
- GSTIN (15-char taxpayer ID)
- Invoice number / Bill number / Receipt number
- Customer or dealer mobile/phone number
- Quantity / Rate / Amount / Discount values
- Date values
- PIN code

If no valid product serial number is visible, return "Not available".

============================================================
FIELD RULES
============================================================

invoice_number:
- Extract invoice number / bill number / tax invoice number.
- Look for labels such as Invoice No, Bill No, Tax Invoice No, Inv No, Receipt No.
- Keep slashes and dashes if printed.
- Do not confuse with GSTIN, product serial number, model number, HSN, or phone number.

product_serial_number:
- Extract as per the rules above.
- Multiple serials must be separated using "^".

date_of_purchase:
- Extract date ONLY from the actual invoice / bill / tax invoice section.
- Valid sources: Invoice Date, Bill Date, Tax Invoice Date, Purchase Date,
  or the date printed near Invoice No / Bill No / Tax Invoice No,
  or the date in the invoice header / invoice details block.
- STRICTLY IGNORE any date printed at the bottom / footer of the page
  that appears along with latitude, longitude, GPS coordinates,
  geo location, "Printed On", "Generated On", "Downloaded On",
  "Captured On", "Uploaded On", scan date, or system date.
- If the ONLY date visible is near latitude / longitude / GPS / geo stamp
  / footer system print, return "Not available".
- If both invoice date and footer/geo date are visible, return ONLY the invoice date.
- Convert to YYYY-MM-DD.
- Do not use due date, delivery date, warranty date, or print date.

dealer_name:
- Extract seller / dealer / shop / vendor business name.
- Usually present at the top/header of invoice.
- The dealer name MUST NOT contain the word "Voltas".
- Do NOT return "Voltas", "Voltas Limited", "Voltas Ltd", or any name
  that contains the word "Voltas" in it. In such case return "Not available".
- Do not extract customer name.

dealer_gst_number:
- Extract dealer GSTIN only.
- GSTIN is exactly 15 characters.
- Pick seller/dealer GSTIN, usually in header.
- Do not pick customer GSTIN if both are present.

dealer_address:
- Extract full dealer/seller address from header area.
- Do not mix with customer address.

customer_name:
- Extract buyer/customer name.
- Look near Bill To, Buyer, Customer Name, Sold To, Party Name, Ship To, Consignee.
- Prefer Bill To / Buyer if both Bill To and Ship To are present.
- Do not extract dealer name.

customer_address:
- Extract full customer/buyer address.
- Look near customer name, Bill To, Buyer, Consignee, or Ship To block.
- Do not extract dealer address.

customer_phone_number:
- Extract customer phone/mobile/contact number only.
- Customer phone number may be multiple.
- Multiple numbers may be separated by "/", ",", "&", "|", "and", or "or".
- Extract all customer phone numbers.
- Digits only.
- Join multiple phone numbers using "^" with no spaces.
- Do not extract dealer phone number.

============================================================
OUTPUT JSON SCHEMA
============================================================
{
  "invoice_number": "string",
  "product_serial_number": "string",
  "date_of_purchase": "string",
  "dealer_name": "string",
  "dealer_gst_number": "string",
  "dealer_address": "string",
  "customer_name": "string",
  "customer_address": "string",
  "customer_phone_number": "string"
}

Return JSON only.
"""

SERIAL_ONLY_PROMPT = """
Extract only the product serial number from this Voltas warranty invoice image.

Rules:
- Product serial number is mostly present with the item name or product description.
- It is often written immediately after the product name or model description.
- It may appear WITHOUT any label like "S.No", "Sr No", "Serial No", etc.
- Even an unlabeled standalone alphanumeric token near the product details
  should be considered if it matches the format rules below.
- Product serial number is alphanumeric only.
- Length must be greater than 14 characters.
- Must contain at least one digit.
- No spaces, slashes, dashes, dots, commas, or special characters inside.
- Extract ALL valid serial numbers.
- If multiple serial numbers are present, join them using "^" with no spaces.
- Do not extract HSN code, GSTIN, invoice number, model number, phone number,
  amount, quantity, rate, or date as a serial number.
- If no valid serial number is visible, return "Not available".

Return JSON only:
{
  "product_serial_number": "string"
}
"""

# =========================================================
# FIELD KEYS
# =========================================================
FIELD_KEYS = [
    "invoice_number",
    "product_serial_number",
    "date_of_purchase",
    "dealer_name",
    "dealer_gst_number",
    "dealer_address",
    "customer_name",
    "customer_address",
    "customer_phone_number"
]

# =========================================================
# IMAGE HELPERS
# =========================================================
def resize_image(image_path, max_size=2048):
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        if max(img.size) <= max_size:
            return image_path

        ratio = max_size / max(img.size)
        new_size = (int(img.size[0] * ratio), int(img.size[1] * ratio))

        temp_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()
        temp_path = os.path.join(temp_dir, os.path.basename(image_path))

        img.resize(new_size, Image.LANCZOS).save(temp_path)
        return temp_path


def encode_image(image_path):
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        img = img.convert("RGB")
        buffer = BytesIO()
        img.save(buffer, format="JPEG")
        return base64.b64encode(buffer.getvalue()).decode()

# =========================================================
# CLEANERS / VALIDATORS
# =========================================================
def clean_text(value):
    if value is None:
        return "Not available"

    value = str(value).strip()

    if value == "" or value.lower() in ["none", "null", "nan", "not available"]:
        return "Not available"

    value = re.sub(r"[\r\n\t]+", " ", value)
    value = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", value).strip()

    return value


def is_valid_product_serial(serial):
    """
    Valid product serial:
    - Alphanumeric only (A-Z, 0-9)
    - Length > 14
    - Must contain at least one digit
    """
    if not serial:
        return False

    serial = str(serial).strip().upper()

    if len(serial) <= 14:
        return False

    if not re.match(r"^[A-Z0-9]+$", serial):
        return False

    if not re.search(r"[0-9]", serial):
        return False

    return True


def clean_product_serial_number(serial_value):
    """
    Extract and keep only valid product serial numbers.
    Multiple valid serial numbers are returned using ^ separator.
    """
    if serial_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    serial_value = str(serial_value).upper().strip()

    if serial_value in ["", "NOT AVAILABLE", "ERROR", "NONE", "NULL", "NAN"]:
        return "Not available"

    valid_serials = []

    # Split by common separators including ^
    chunks = re.split(r"[\^,;/|&\s]+", serial_value)

    for chunk in chunks:
        compact = re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", chunk)

        if is_valid_product_serial(compact):
            if compact not in valid_serials:
                valid_serials.append(compact)

    # Fallback regex scan over raw text
    if not valid_serials:
        candidates = re.findall(r"[A-Z0-9]{15,30}", serial_value)
        for cand in candidates:
            if is_valid_product_serial(cand) and cand not in valid_serials:
                valid_serials.append(cand)

    if valid_serials:
        return "^".join(valid_serials)

    return "Not available"


def clean_customer_phone_number(phone_value):
    if phone_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    phone_value = str(phone_value).strip()

    if phone_value == "" or phone_value.lower() in ["not available", "error", "none", "null", "nan"]:
        return "Not available"

    parts = re.split(r"[\^/,;&|]|\band\b|\bor\b", phone_value, flags=re.IGNORECASE)

    final_numbers = []

    for part in parts:
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)

        if not digits:
            continue

        if len(digits) == 12 and digits.startswith("91"):
            digits = digits[-10:]
        elif len(digits) == 11 and digits.startswith("0"):
            digits = digits[-10:]

        if len(digits) == 10 and digits[0] in ["6", "7", "8", "9"]:
            if digits not in final_numbers:
                final_numbers.append(digits)

    if final_numbers:
        return "^".join(final_numbers)

    return "Not available"


def clean_gstin(gstin_value):
    if gstin_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    gstin_value = str(gstin_value).upper().strip()
    gstin_value = re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", gstin_value)

    pattern = r"^[0-9]{2}[A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z][1-9A-Z]Z[0-9A-Z]$"

    if re.match(pattern, gstin_value):
        return gstin_value

    return "Not available"


def clean_dealer_name(dealer_value):
    """
    Dealer name must NOT contain the word 'Voltas'.
    If it contains 'Voltas', treat as invalid and return 'Not available'.
    """
    dealer_value = clean_text(dealer_value)

    if dealer_value == "Not available":
        return "Not available"

    if re.search(r"\bvoltas\b", dealer_value, flags=re.IGNORECASE):
        return "Not available"

    return dealer_value


def normalize_extracted_data(data):
    normalized = {}

    for key in FIELD_KEYS:
        normalized[key] = clean_text(data.get(key, "Not available"))

    normalized["product_serial_number"] = clean_product_serial_number(
        normalized.get("product_serial_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["customer_phone_number"] = clean_customer_phone_number(
        normalized.get("customer_phone_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["dealer_gst_number"] = clean_gstin(
        normalized.get("dealer_gst_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["dealer_name"] = clean_dealer_name(
        normalized.get("dealer_name", "Not available")
    )

    return normalized

# =========================================================
# TARGETED SERIAL EXTRACTION
# =========================================================
def extract_serial_only(image_b64):
    try:
        response = client.chat.completions.create(
            model=MODEL_NAME,
            temperature=0,
            max_tokens=500,
            response_format={"type": "json_object"},
            messages=[
                {
                    "role": "user",
                    "content": [
                        {"type": "text", "text": SERIAL_ONLY_PROMPT},
                        {
                            "type": "image_url",
                            "image_url": {
                                "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_b64}"
                            }
                        }
                    ]
                }
            ]
        )

        raw = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)
        serial = raw.get("product_serial_number", "Not available")

        return clean_product_serial_number(serial)

    except Exception:
        return "Not available"

# =========================================================
# PROCESS IMAGE
# =========================================================
def process_image(image_path):
    backoff = INITIAL_BACKOFF

    for attempt in range(1, MAX_RETRIES + 1):
        try:
            processed_img = resize_image(image_path)
            image_b64 = encode_image(processed_img)

            response = client.chat.completions.create(
                model=MODEL_NAME,
                temperature=0,
                max_tokens=3000,
                response_format={"type": "json_object"},
                messages=[
                    {
                        "role": "user",
                        "content": [
                            {"type": "text", "text": INVOICE_PROMPT},
                            {
                                "type": "image_url",
                                "image_url": {
                                    "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_b64}"
                                }
                            }
                        ]
                    }
                ]
            )

            raw_data = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)

            # =====================================================
            # MULTI-INVOICE SAFE HANDLING
            # =====================================================
            if "invoices" in raw_data and isinstance(raw_data["invoices"], list):

                invoices = raw_data["invoices"]
                merged_data = {k: [] for k in FIELD_KEYS}

                for inv in invoices:
                    inv = normalize_extracted_data(inv)

                    for key in FIELD_KEYS:
                        value = inv.get(key, "Not available")
                        if value and value != "Not available":
                            merged_data[key].append(str(value))

                data = {}

                for key in FIELD_KEYS:
                    if merged_dataif key == "product_serial_number":
                            data[key] = clean_product_serial_number(
                                "^".join(merged_data[key])
                            )
                        elif key == "customer_phone_number":
                            data[key] = clean_customer_phone_number(
                                "^".join(merged_data[key])
                            )
                        else:
                            data[key] = ", ".join(merged_data[key])
                    else:
                        data[key] = "Not available"

                # Re-apply dealer cleaner to merged value as well
                data["dealer_name"] = clean_dealer_name(
                    data.get("dealer_name", "Not available")
                )

            else:
                data = normalize_extracted_data(raw_data)

            # =====================================================
            # SECOND PASS ONLY IF SERIAL NOT FOUND
            # =====================================================
            if data.get("product_serial_number", "Not available") == "Not available":
                serial_second_pass = extract_serial_only(image_b64)
                data["product_serial_number"] = serial_second_pass

            data["file_name"] = os.path.basename(image_path)

            print(f"Processed: {data['file_name']}")
            return data

        except Exception as e:
            if attempt == MAX_RETRIES:
                print(f"Failed after retries: {os.path.basename(image_path)} | Error: {e}")
                break

            print(f"Retry {attempt}/{MAX_RETRIES} for {os.path.basename(image_path)}")
            time.sleep(backoff)
            backoff *= 2

    err_row = {k: "Error" for k in FIELD_KEYS}
    err_row["file_name"] = os.path.basename(image_path)
    return err_row

# =========================================================
# MAIN EXECUTION - IMAGE EXTRACTION
# =========================================================
all_images = [
    os.path.join(IMAGE_FOLDER, f)
    for f in os.listdir(IMAGE_FOLDER)
    if f.lower().endswith((".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png"))
]

print(f"Total images: {len(all_images)}")

results = []

with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=MAX_WORKERS) as executor:
    futures = [executor.submit(process_image, img) for img in all_images]

    for future in as_completed(futures):
        results.append(future.result())

df = pd.DataFrame(results)

# =========================================================
# SAVE PICKLE
# =========================================================
os.makedirs(OUTPUT_PKL_FOLDER, exist_ok=True)

timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
pkl_file_name = f"output_voltas_warranty_{timestamp}.pkl"
full_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_PKL_FOLDER, pkl_file_name)

df.to_pickle(full_path)

print(f"Pickle File saved at: {full_path}")
print("Exact Columns:", df.columns.tolist())
print("IMAGE EXTRACTION COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")

# =========================================================
# DATABASE CONNECTION
# =========================================================

HOST = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'

cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# LOAD CLAIM HEADER TABLE
# =========================================================
claim_header_table = "s_crm_claim_hdr_flat"

base_query = f"""
SELECT header_crm_id, sr_id, sr_open_date, sr_closed_date
FROM {claim_header_table}
"""

base_data = pd.read_sql(base_query, conn)

print("Base table loaded")

# =========================================================
# CREATE OUTPUT TABLE
# =========================================================
create_table_query = """
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS p_unst_str_customer_invoice (
    header_crm_id VARCHAR(50),
    sr_id VARCHAR(50),
    attch_id VARCHAR(50),

    customer_address TEXT,
    customer_phone_number TEXT
)
"""

cursor.execute(create_table_query)
conn.commit()

print("Output table ready")

# =========================================================
# EXTRACT IDs FROM FILE NAME
# =========================================================
def extract_ids(file_name):
    try:
        file_name = str(file_name)

        # Split on ^
        main_part, rest = file_name.split("^")

        # Extract header_crm_id and sr_id
        header_crm_id, sr_id = main_part.split("_")

        # Extract attch_id (before next _)
        attch_id = rest.split("_")[0]

        return header_crm_id, sr_id, attch_id

    except Exception:
        return None, None, None


# Apply to dataframe
df["header_crm_id"], df["sr_id"], df["attch_id"] = zip(
    *df["file_name"].apply(extract_ids)
)
# =========================================================
# MERGE WITH BASE TABLE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    df,
    base_data,
    on=["header_crm_id", "sr_id"],
    how="left"
)

merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print("Merge completed")


# =========================================================
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS
# =========================================================
TABLE_NAME = "p_unst_str_customer_invoice"
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"   # insert | upsert

create_table_query = f"""
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {TABLE_NAME} (

    id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,

    header_crm_id VARCHAR(50),
    sr_id VARCHAR(50),
    attch_id VARCHAR(50),

    sr_open_date DATETIME,
    sr_closed_date DATETIME,

    file_name TEXT,
    invoice_number VARCHAR(255),
    product_serial_number VARCHAR(255),
    date_of_purchase VARCHAR(255),

    dealer_name TEXT,
    dealer_gst_number VARCHAR(255),
    dealer_address TEXT,

    customer_name TEXT,
    customer_address TEXT,
    customer_phone_number VARCHAR(255),

    UNIQUE KEY uniq_invoice (
        header_crm_id,
        sr_id,
        attch_id
    )
)
"""

cursor.execute(create_table_query)
conn.commit()

# =========================================================
# PREPARE DATA
# =========================================================
insert_cols = [
    "header_crm_id",
    "sr_id",
    "attch_id",
    "sr_open_date",
    "sr_closed_date",
    "file_name",
    "invoice_number",
    "product_serial_number",
    "date_of_purchase",
    "dealer_name",
    "dealer_gst_number",
    "dealer_address",
    "customer_name",
    "customer_address",
    "customer_phone_number"
]

for col in insert_cols:
    if col not in merged_df.columns:
        merged_df[col] = None

records = merged_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

# =========================================================
# GENERATE INSERT / UPSERT SQL
# =========================================================
placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

if WRITE_MODE.lower() == "upsert":

    update_cols = [
        c for c in insert_cols
        if c not in ["header_crm_id", "sr_id", "attch_id"]
    ]

    update_sql = ", ".join(
        [f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols]
    )

    insert_sql = f"""
    INSERT INTO {TABLE_NAME} ({col_list})
    VALUES ({placeholders})
    ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE
    {update_sql}
    """

else:

    insert_sql = f"""
    INSERT IGNORE INTO {TABLE_NAME} ({col_list})
    VALUES ({placeholders})
    """

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT / UPSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH_SIZE = 500
DB_MAX_RETRIES = 5

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH_SIZE):

    batch = records[i:i + BATCH_SIZE]

    for attempt in range(DB_MAX_RETRIES):

        try:

            cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
            conn.commit()

            print(
                f"{WRITE_MODE.upper()} : "
                f"{i} to {min(i + len(batch), len(records))}"
            )

            break

        except Exception as e:

            error_text = str(e)

            if "1205" in error_text:

                print(
                    f"Lock detected. Retry "
                    f"{attempt + 1}/{DB_MAX_RETRIES}"
                )

                time.sleep(2)

            else:

                conn.rollback()

                print(
                    f"Database error in batch "
                    f"starting at row {i}: {e}"
                )

                break

# =========================================================
# CLOSE CONNECTION
# =========================================================
cursor.close()
conn.close()

print(f"{WRITE_MODE.upper()} COMPLETED")
print("FULL PIPELINE COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")
