INVOICE_PROMPT = """
You are a highly accurate invoice data extraction system specialized in
CUSTOMER INVOICES submitted to VOLTAS for WARRANTY CLAIMS.

Extract only the required fields from the invoice image and return STRICT JSON ONLY.

============================================================
GLOBAL RULES
============================================================
1. Output ENGLISH ONLY.
2. Do NOT hallucinate.
3. Do NOT guess or infer values.
4. Extract only values clearly visible in the invoice image.
5. If any value is not clearly visible, return "Not available".
6. Return JSON only. No markdown. No explanation. No comments.
7. Dates must be returned in YYYY-MM-DD format.
8. If only partial date is visible, return "Not available".
9. Phone numbers must contain digits only.
10. Addresses must be single-line comma-separated text.
11. Remove extra spaces, line breaks, and unnecessary punctuation.
12. If multiple invoices are present in one image, return:
    {
      "invoices": [
        { same schema },
        { same schema }
      ]
    }

============================================================
MOST IMPORTANT FIELD: product_serial_number
============================================================
Product serial number is VERY CRITICAL.

Definition of a valid product serial number:
- Alphanumeric only (uppercase letters A-Z and digits 0-9).
- Length must be greater than 14 characters.
- Must contain at least one digit.
- Must NOT contain spaces, slashes, dashes, dots, commas, colons, or any special characters inside.
- Usually starts with digits and ends with digits.
- May contain uppercase letters in between.

Where to look (very important):
- Product serial number is mostly present with the item name or product description.
- It is often written immediately after the product name, item name, or model description.
- It may also appear in the line-item table, in the description column,
  or as a standalone alphanumeric token near the product details.
- LABEL IS NOT MANDATORY:
    The serial number may appear WITHOUT any label like "S.No", "Sr No",
    "Serial No", "S/N", etc. It can simply be printed next to or below the
    item name as a standalone alphanumeric value.
- If a label is present, common labels include:
  Serial No, Sr No, Sr.No, S.No, S No, SR NO, S/N, SN,
  Product Serial No, Product Sr No, Machine No, Unit Serial No,
  Barcode, IDU SR NO, ODU SR NO, Indoor Serial No, Outdoor Serial No.
- Even if no label is present, treat any standalone alphanumeric token
  matching the format rules (length > 14, alphanumeric, contains digits)
  near the item/product description as the product serial number.

Multiple serial numbers:
- A customer may buy multiple products in the same invoice.
- Therefore, multiple product serial numbers may be present.
- Extract ALL valid product serial numbers.
- Join multiple valid product serial numbers using "^" with no spaces.

Strict exclusions — do NOT extract these as product_serial_number:
- Model number / model code (e.g., short codes printed in the model column)
- Item code / SKU
- HSN code / SAC code
- GSTIN (15-char taxpayer ID)
- Invoice number / Bill number / Receipt number
- Customer or dealer mobile/phone number
- Quantity / Rate / Amount / Discount values
- Date values
- PIN code

If no valid product serial number is visible, return "Not available".

============================================================
FIELD RULES
============================================================

invoice_number:
- Extract invoice number / bill number / tax invoice number.
- Look for labels such as Invoice No, Bill No, Tax Invoice No, Inv No, Receipt No.
- Keep slashes and dashes if printed.
- Do not confuse with GSTIN, product serial number, model number, HSN, or phone number.

product_serial_number:
- Extract as per the rules above.
- Multiple serials must be separated using "^".

date_of_purchase:
- Extract invoice date / bill date / purchase date.
- Convert to YYYY-MM-DD.
- Do not use due date, delivery date, warranty date, or print date.

dealer_name:
- Extract seller / dealer / shop / vendor business name.
- Usually present at the top/header of invoice.
- Do not extract Voltas brand name unless it is the actual dealer name.
- Do not extract customer name.

dealer_gst_number:
- Extract dealer GSTIN only.
- GSTIN is exactly 15 characters.
- Pick seller/dealer GSTIN, usually in header.
- Do not pick customer GSTIN if both are present.

dealer_address:
- Extract full dealer/seller address from header area.
- Do not mix with customer address.

customer_name:
- Extract buyer/customer name.
- Look near Bill To, Buyer, Customer Name, Sold To, Party Name, Ship To, Consignee.
- Prefer Bill To / Buyer if both Bill To and Ship To are present.
- Do not extract dealer name.

customer_address:
- Extract full customer/buyer address.
- Look near customer name, Bill To, Buyer, Consignee, or Ship To block.
- Do not extract dealer address.

customer_phone_number:
- Extract customer phone/mobile/contact number only.
- Customer phone number may be multiple.
- Multiple numbers may be separated by "/", ",", "&", "|", "and", or "or".
- Extract all customer phone numbers.
- Digits only.
- Join multiple phone numbers using "^" with no spaces.
- Do not extract dealer phone number.

============================================================
OUTPUT JSON SCHEMA
============================================================
{
  "invoice_number": "string",
  "product_serial_number": "string",
  "date_of_purchase": "string",
  "dealer_name": "string",
  "dealer_gst_number": "string",
  "dealer_address": "string",
  "customer_name": "string",
  "customer_address": "string",
  "customer_phone_number": "string"
}

Return JSON only.
"""

SERIAL_ONLY_PROMPT = """
Extract only the product serial number from this Voltas warranty invoice image.

Rules:
- Product serial number is mostly present with the item name or product description.
- It is often written immediately after the product name or model description.
- It may appear WITHOUT any label like "S.No", "Sr No", "Serial No", etc.
- Even an unlabeled standalone alphanumeric token near the product details
  should be considered if it matches the format rules below.
- Product serial number is alphanumeric only.
- Length must be greater than 14 characters.
- Must contain at least one digit.
- No spaces, slashes, dashes, dots, commas, or special characters inside.
- Extract ALL valid serial numbers.
- If multiple serial numbers are present, join them using "^" with no spaces.
- Do not extract HSN code, GSTIN, invoice number, model number, phone number,
  amount, quantity, rate, or date as a serial number.
- If no valid serial number is visible, return "Not available".

Return JSON only:
{
  "product_serial_number": "string"
}
"""

# =========================================================
# FIELD KEYS
# =========================================================
FIELD_KEYS = [
    "invoice_number",
    "product_serial_number",
    "date_of_purchase",
    "dealer_name",
    "dealer_gst_number",
    "dealer_address",
    "customer_name",
    "customer_address",
    "customer_phone_number"
]

# =========================================================
# IMAGE HELPERS
# =========================================================
def resize_image(image_path, max_size=2048):
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        if max(img.size) <= max_size:
            return image_path

        ratio = max_size / max(img.size)
        new_size = (int(img.size[0] * ratio), int(img.size[1] * ratio))

        temp_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()
        temp_path = os.path.join(temp_dir, os.path.basename(image_path))

        img.resize(new_size, Image.LANCZOS).save(temp_path)
        return temp_path


def encode_image(image_path):
    with Image.open(image_path) as img:
        img = img.convert("RGB")
        buffer = BytesIO()
        img.save(buffer, format="JPEG")
        return base64.b64encode(buffer.getvalue()).decode()

# =========================================================
# CLEANERS / VALIDATORS
# =========================================================
def clean_text(value):
    if value is None:
        return "Not available"

    value = str(value).strip()

    if value == "" or value.lower() in ["none", "null", "nan", "not available"]:
        return "Not available"

    value = re.sub(r"[\r\n\t]+", " ", value)
    value = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", value).strip()

    return value


def is_valid_product_serial(serial):
    """
    Valid product serial:
    - Alphanumeric only (A-Z, 0-9)
    - Length > 14
    - Must contain at least one digit
    """
    if not serial:
        return False

    serial = str(serial).strip().upper()

    if len(serial) <= 14:
        return False

    if not re.match(r"^[A-Z0-9]+$", serial):
        return False

    if not re.search(r"[0-9]", serial):
        return False

    return True


def clean_product_serial_number(serial_value):
    """
    Extract and keep only valid product serial numbers.
    Multiple valid serial numbers are returned using ^ separator.
    """
    if serial_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    serial_value = str(serial_value).upper().strip()

    if serial_value in ["", "NOT AVAILABLE", "ERROR", "NONE", "NULL", "NAN"]:
        return "Not available"

    valid_serials = []

    # Split by common separators including ^
    chunks = re.split(r"[\^,;/|&\s]+", serial_value)

    for chunk in chunks:
        compact = re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", chunk)

        if is_valid_product_serial(compact):
            if compact not in valid_serials:
                valid_serials.append(compact)

    # Fallback regex scan over raw text
    if not valid_serials:
        candidates = re.findall(r"[A-Z0-9]{15,30}", serial_value)
        for cand in candidates:
            if is_valid_product_serial(cand) and cand not in valid_serials:
                valid_serials.append(cand)

    if valid_serials:
        return "^".join(valid_serials)

    return "Not available"


def clean_customer_phone_number(phone_value):
    if phone_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    phone_value = str(phone_value).strip()

    if phone_value == "" or phone_value.lower() in ["not available", "error", "none", "null", "nan"]:
        return "Not available"

    parts = re.split(r"[\^/,;&|]|\band\b|\bor\b", phone_value, flags=re.IGNORECASE)

    final_numbers = []

    for part in parts:
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)

        if not digits:
            continue

        if len(digits) == 12 and digits.startswith("91"):
            digits = digits[-10:]
        elif len(digits) == 11 and digits.startswith("0"):
            digits = digits[-10:]

        if len(digits) == 10 and digits[0] in ["6", "7", "8", "9"]:
            if digits not in final_numbers:
                final_numbers.append(digits)

    if final_numbers:
        return "^".join(final_numbers)

    return "Not available"


def clean_gstin(gstin_value):
    if gstin_value is None:
        return "Not available"

    gstin_value = str(gstin_value).upper().strip()
    gstin_value = re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", gstin_value)

    pattern = r"^[0-9]{2}[A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z][1-9A-Z]Z[0-9A-Z]$"

    if re.match(pattern, gstin_value):
        return gstin_value

    return "Not available"


def normalize_extracted_data(data):
    normalized = {}

    for key in FIELD_KEYS:
        normalized[key] = clean_text(data.get(key, "Not available"))

    normalized["product_serial_number"] = clean_product_serial_number(
        normalized.get("product_serial_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["customer_phone_number"] = clean_customer_phone_number(
        normalized.get("customer_phone_number", "Not available")
    )

    normalized["dealer_gst_number"] = clean_gstin(
        normalized.get("dealer_gst_number", "Not available")
    )

    return normalized

# =========================================================
# TARGETED SERIAL EXTRACTION
# =========================================================
def extract_serial_only(image_b64):
    try:
        response = client.chat.completions.create(
            model=MODEL_NAME,
            temperature=0,
            max_tokens=500,
            response_format={"type": "json_object"},
            messages=[
                {
                    "role": "user",
                    "content": [
                        {"type": "text", "text": SERIAL_ONLY_PROMPT},
                        {
                            "type": "image_url",
                            "image_url": {
                                "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_b64}"
                            }
                        }
                    ]
                }
            ]
        )

        raw = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)
        serial = raw.get("product_serial_number", "Not available")

        return clean_product_serial_number(serial)

    except Exception:
        return "Not available"

# =========================================================
# PROCESS IMAGE
# =========================================================
def process_image(image_path):
    backoff = INITIAL_BACKOFF

    for attempt in range(1, MAX_RETRIES + 1):
        try:
            processed_img = resize_image(image_path)
            image_b64 = encode_image(processed_img)

            response = client.chat.completions.create(
                model=MODEL_NAME,
                temperature=0,
                max_tokens=3000,
                response_format={"type": "json_object"},
                messages=[
                    {
                        "role": "user",
                        "content": [
                            {"type": "text", "text": INVOICE_PROMPT},
                            {
                                "type": "image_url",
                                "image_url": {
                                    "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{image_b64}"
                                }
                            }
                        ]
                    }
                ]
            )

            raw_data = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)

            # =====================================================
            # MULTI-INVOICE SAFE HANDLING
            # =====================================================
            if "invoices" in raw_data and isinstance(raw_data["invoices"], list):

                invoices = raw_data["invoices"]
                merged_data = {k: [] for k in FIELD_KEYS}

                for inv in invoices:
                    inv = normalize_extracted_data(inv)

                    for key in FIELD_KEYS:
                        value = inv.get(key, "Not available")
                        if value and value != "Not available":
                            merged_data[key].append(str(value))

                data = {}

                for key in FIELD_KEYS:
                    if merged_data[key]:
                        if key == "product_serial_number":
                            data[key] = clean_product_serial_number(
                                "^".join(merged_data[key])
                            )
                        elif key == "customer_phone_number":
                            data[key] = clean_customer_phone_number(
                                "^".join(merged_data[key])
                            )
                        else:
                            data[key] = ", ".join(merged_data[key])
                    else:
                        data[key] = "Not available"

            else:
                data = normalize_extracted_data(raw_data)

            # =====================================================
            # SECOND PASS ONLY IF SERIAL NOT FOUND
            # =====================================================
            if data.get("product_serial_number", "Not available") == "Not available":
                serial_second_pass = extract_serial_only(image_b64)
                data["product_serial_number"] = serial_second_pass

            data["file_name"] = os.path.basename(image_path)

            print(f"Processed: {data['file_name']}")
            return data

        except Exception as e:
            if attempt == MAX_RETRIES:
                print(f"Failed after retries: {os.path.basename(image_path)} | Error: {e}")
                break

            print(f"Retry {attempt}/{MAX_RETRIES} for {os.path.basename(image_path)}")
            time.sleep(backoff)
            backoff *= 2

    err_row = {k: "Error" for k in FIELD_KEYS}
    err_row["file_name"] = os.path.basename(image_path)
    return err_row

# =========================================================
# MAIN EXECUTION - IMAGE EXTRACTION
# =========================================================
all_images = [
    os.path.join(IMAGE_FOLDER, f)
    for f in os.listdir(IMAGE_FOLDER)
    if f.lower().endswith((".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png"))
]

print(f"Total images: {len(all_images)}")

results = []

with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=MAX_WORKERS) as executor:
    futures = [executor.submit(process_image, img) for img in all_images]

    for future in as_completed(futures):
        results.append(future.result())

df = pd.DataFrame(results)

# =========================================================
# SAVE PICKLE
# =========================================================
os.makedirs(OUTPUT_PKL_FOLDER, exist_ok=True)

timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
pkl_file_name = f"output_voltas_warranty_{timestamp}.pkl"
full_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_PKL_FOLDER, pkl_file_name)

df.to_pickle(full_path)

print(f"Pickle File saved at: {full_path}")
print("Exact Columns:", df.columns.tolist())
print("IMAGE EXTRACTION COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")

HOST='vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'

# =========================================================

# =========================================================
# CREATE OUTPUT TABLE

create_table_query = """
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS p_unst_str_customer_invoice (
    header_crm_id VARCHAR(50),
    sr_id VARCHAR(50),
    attch_id VARCHAR(50),
    sr_open_date DATETIME,
    sr_closed_date DATETIME,
    file_name VARCHAR(255),
    invoice_number TEXT,
    product_serial_number TEXT,
    date_of_purchase TEXT,
    dealer_name TEXT,
    dealer_gst_number VARCHAR(20),
    dealer_address TEXT,
    customer_name TEXT,
    customer_address TEXT,
    customer_phone_number TEXT
)
"""

cursor.execute(create_table_query)
conn.commit()

print("Output table ready")

# =========================================================
# EXTRACT IDs FROM FILE NAME
# =========================================================
def extract_ids(file_name):
    try:
        file_name = str(file_name)

        # Split on ^
        main_part, rest = file_name.split("^")

        # Extract header_crm_id and sr_id
        header_crm_id, sr_id = main_part.split("_")

        # Extract attch_id (before next _)
        attch_id = rest.split("_")[0]

        return header_crm_id, sr_id, attch_id

    except Exception:
        return None, None, None


# Apply to dataframe
df["header_crm_id"], df["sr_id"], df["attch_id"] = zip(
    *df["file_name"].apply(extract_ids)
)
# =========================================================
# MERGE WITH BASE TABLE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    df,
    base_data,
    on=["header_crm_id", "sr_id"],
    how="left"
)

merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print("Merge completed")



# =========================================================
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS
# =========================================================
TABLE_NAME = "p_unst_str_customer_invoice"
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"   # insert | upsert

create_table_query = f"""
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {TABLE_NAME} (

    id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,

    header_crm_id VARCHAR(50),
    sr_id VARCHAR(50),
    attch_id VARCHAR(50),

    sr_open_date DATETIME,
    sr_closed_date DATETIME,

    file_name TEXT,
    invoice_number VARCHAR(255),
    product_serial_number VARCHAR(255),
    date_of_purchase VARCHAR(255),

    dealer_name TEXT,
    dealer_gst_number VARCHAR(255),
    dealer_address TEXT,

    customer_name TEXT,
    customer_address TEXT,
    customer_phone_number VARCHAR(255),

    UNIQUE KEY uniq_invoice (
        header_crm_id,
        sr_id,
        attch_id
    )
)
"""

cursor.execute(create_table_query)
conn.commit()

# =========================================================
# PREPARE DATA
# =========================================================
insert_cols = [
    "header_crm_id",
    "sr_id",
    "attch_id",
    "sr_open_date",
    "sr_closed_date",
    "file_name",
    "invoice_number",
    "product_serial_number",
    "date_of_purchase",
    "dealer_name",
    "dealer_gst_number",
    "dealer_address",
    "customer_name",
    "customer_address",
    "customer_phone_number"
]

for col in insert_cols:
    if col not in merged_df.columns:
        merged_df[col] = None

records = merged_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

# =========================================================
# GENERATE INSERT / UPSERT SQL
# =========================================================
placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

if WRITE_MODE.lower() == "upsert":

    update_cols = [
        c for c in insert_cols
        if c not in ["header_crm_id", "sr_id", "attch_id"]
    ]

    update_sql = ", ".join(
        [f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols]
    )

    insert_sql = f"""
    INSERT INTO {TABLE_NAME} ({col_list})
    VALUES ({placeholders})
    ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE
    {update_sql}
    """

else:

    insert_sql = f"""
    INSERT IGNORE INTO {TABLE_NAME} ({col_list})
    VALUES ({placeholders})
    """

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT / UPSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH_SIZE = 500
DB_MAX_RETRIES = 5

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH_SIZE):

    batch = records[i:i + BATCH_SIZE]

    for attempt in range(DB_MAX_RETRIES):

        try:

            cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
            conn.commit()

            print(
                f"{WRITE_MODE.upper()} : "
                f"{i} to {min(i + len(batch), len(records))}"
            )

            break

        except Exception as e:

            error_text = str(e)

            if "1205" in error_text:

                print(
                    f"Lock detected. Retry "
                    f"{attempt + 1}/{DB_MAX_RETRIES}"
                )

                time.sleep(2)

            else:

                conn.rollback()

                print(
                    f"Database error in batch "
                    f"starting at row {i}: {e}"
                )

                break

# =========================================================
# CLOSE CONNECTION
# =========================================================
cursor.close()
conn.close()

print(f"{WRITE_MODE.upper()} COMPLETED")
print("FULL PIPELINE COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")

import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from collections import defaultdict
from rapidfuzz import fuzz

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1017
CHECK_NAME  = "Change in ownership"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1017"

# Similarity threshold for NAME comparison
# If name similarity < 70% AND no phone overlap -> exception (ownership change)
NAME_THRESHOLD = 70

# Customer phone columns to combine
CUSTOMER_PHONE_COLS = [
    "calling_from_number",
    "customer_contact",
    "customer_registered_phone",
    "customer_alternate_phone",
]

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA
# =========================================================
# sr_df = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_base_data ",conn)


sr_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM s_crm_claim_hdr_flat "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19'",
    conn
)
print(f"SR rows to process: {len(sr_df)}")

# For grouping by sr_serial_number, pull FULL p_base_data
all_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT header_crm_id, sr_id, sr_number, sr_serial_number, "
    "customer_name, "
    "calling_from_number, customer_contact, "
    "customer_registered_phone, customer_alternate_phone "
    "FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_serial_number IS NOT NULL AND sr_serial_number != ''",
    conn
)
print(f"All p_base_data rows for grouping: {len(all_df)}")

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "error", "na", "n/a"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS


def split_multi(v, sep=r"[\^,;/|]"):
    if is_missing(v):
        return []
    return [x.strip() for x in re.split(sep, str(v)) if x.strip()]


def clean_phone_set(v):
    """Return set of cleaned last-10-digit phone numbers."""
    nums = set()
    for part in split_multi(v):
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)
        if len(digits) >= 10:
            nums.add(digits[-10:])
    return nums


def collect_all_phones(row):
    """Union of all phones across the 4 customer phone columns."""
    phones = set()
    for col in CUSTOMER_PHONE_COLS:
        phones |= clean_phone_set(row.get(col))
    return phones


def clean_serial(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())


def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s


def build_name_string(row):
    """Normalized customer name."""
    return norm_text(row.get("customer_name"))

# =========================================================
# BUILD SERIAL -> [RECORDS] LOOKUP
# =========================================================
serial_records = defaultdict(list)

for _, row in all_df.iterrows():
    serial = clean_serial(row.get("sr_serial_number"))
    if not serial:
        continue
    name    = build_name_string(row)
    phones  = collect_all_phones(row)

    # Skip totally empty profiles
    if not name and not phones:
        continue

    serial_records[serial].append({
        "name":          name,
        "raw_name":      row.get("customer_name"),
        "phones":        phones,
        "sr_number":     row.get("sr_number"),
        "header_crm_id": row.get("header_crm_id"),
    })

print(f"Distinct serial numbers in lookup: {len(serial_records)}")

# =========================================================
# CHECK FUNCTION
# =========================================================
def check_ownership_change(current_serial, current_sr, current_header,
                           current_name, current_phones):
    """
    Compare current name + phones against OTHER records of the SAME serial
    that have DIFFERENT sr_number AND DIFFERENT header_crm_id.

    Flag = 1 (ownership change) if for ANY such other record:
       - Name similarity < NAME_THRESHOLD (70%), AND
       - There is NO overlap between current phones and other's phones.

    (Phone overlap = same household/customer -> don't flag even if name differs.)
    """
    if not current_serial:
        return 0, 100, "no_phone_match", "", "", "", 0

    records = serial_records.get(current_serial, [])

    # Keep only records with DIFFERENT sr_number AND DIFFERENT header_crm_id
    others = [
        r for r in records
        if (r["sr_number"]     != current_sr)
        and (r["header_crm_id"] != current_header)
    ]

    if not others:
        return 0, 100, "no_others", "", "", "", 0

    # Track conflicting (most-different) match where phones didn't overlap
    conflicting_score   = 100
    observed_values     = ""
    conflicting_sr      = ""
    conflicting_header  = ""
    conflicting_phone_status = "no_phone_match"
    any_flagged   = False

    for r in others:
        name_score    = fuzz.token_set_ratio(current_name, r["name"]) if current_name and r["name"] else 0
        phone_overlap = bool(current_phones & r["phones"]) if current_phones and r["phones"] else False

        # Flag if name is significantly different AND phones don't overlap
        is_flagged = (name_score < NAME_THRESHOLD) and (not phone_overlap)

        if is_flagged and name_score < conflicting_score:
            conflicting_score   = name_score
            observed_values     = r["raw_name"] if r["raw_name"] else r["name"]
            conflicting_sr      = r["sr_number"]
            conflicting_header  = r["header_crm_id"]
            conflicting_phone_status = "phone_overlap" if phone_overlap else "no_phone_match"
            any_flagged   = True

    flag = 1 if any_flagged else 0
    return (flag, conflicting_score, conflicting_phone_status,
            observed_values, conflicting_sr, conflicting_header, len(others))

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK
# =========================================================
def row_check(r):
    serial     = clean_serial(r.get("sr_serial_number"))
    name       = build_name_string(r)
    phones     = collect_all_phones(r)
    cur_sr     = r.get("sr_number")
    cur_header = r.get("header_crm_id")

    (flag, lowest_score, phone_status,
     observed_values, conflicting_sr, conflicting_header, total_others) = \
        check_ownership_change(serial, cur_sr, cur_header, name, phones)

    return pd.Series({
        "current_name":                 r.get("customer_name") or "",
        "current_phones":               ", ".join(sorted(phones)) if phones else "",
        "lowest_similarity":            lowest_score,
        "phone_overlap_status":         phone_status,
        "observed_values":              observed_values,
        "conflicting_sr_number":        conflicting_sr,
        "conflicting_header_crm_id":    conflicting_header,
        "total_other_records":          total_others,
        "ownership_change":             flag,
    })

check_results = sr_df.apply(row_check, axis=1)
sr_df["current_name"]              = check_results["current_name"]
sr_df["current_phones"]            = check_results["current_phones"]
sr_df["lowest_similarity"]         = check_results["lowest_similarity"].astype(int)
sr_df["phone_overlap_status"]      = check_results["phone_overlap_status"]
sr_df["observed_values"]           = check_results["observed_values"]
sr_df["conflicting_sr_number"]     = check_results["conflicting_sr_number"]
sr_df["conflicting_header_crm_id"] = check_results["conflicting_header_crm_id"]
sr_df["total_other_records"]       = check_results["total_other_records"].astype(int)
sr_df["ownership_change"]          = check_results["ownership_change"].astype(int)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(flag):
    return "yes" if flag == 1 else "no"


# def build_expected_value():
#     return (f"For the same sr_serial_number across different sr_number and "
#             f"header_crm_id, customer name should remain consistent "
#             f"(similarity >= {NAME_THRESHOLD}%) OR at least one phone "
#             f"number should overlap")

def build_expected_value():
    return ("N/A")


def build_observed_value(total_others, flag, lowest_score, conflicting_sr, conflicting_header):
    if total_others == 0:
        return "No other SR/header found with the same serial number — single owner record"
    if flag == 0:
        return (f"Same serial found in {total_others} other record(s) — "
                f"either customer name is consistent or phone numbers overlap "
                f"(no ownership change detected)")
    return (f"Same serial found in {total_others} other record(s) — lowest "
            f"customer name similarity = {lowest_score}% (against "
            f"conflicting_sr_number={conflicting_sr}, "
            f"conflicting_header_crm_id={conflicting_header}) AND no phone "
            f"number overlap")


def build_additional_remarks(flag, lowest_score, observed_values,
                             conflicting_sr, conflicting_header):
    if flag == 0:
        return ("No ownership change detected — customer name consistent or "
                "phone numbers overlap across records of the same serial")
    return (f"Ownership change detected — same sr_serial_number appears in "
            f"conflicting_sr_number={conflicting_sr}, "
            f"conflicting_header_crm_id={conflicting_header} with a different "
            f"customer name ({lowest_score}% similarity) AND no overlapping "
            f"phone numbers. Observed name: {observed_values}")


output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                    CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                  CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                  now_ts,
    "updated_at":                  now_ts,
    "is_active":                   sr_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":               sr_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                   sr_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                    sr_df.get("attch_id"),
    "category":                    sr_df.get("category"),
    "sr_serial_number":            sr_df.get("sr_serial_number"),
    "customer_name":               sr_df.get("customer_name"),
    "calling_from_number":         sr_df.get("calling_from_number"),
    "customer_contact":            sr_df.get("customer_contact"),
    "customer_registered_phone":   sr_df.get("customer_registered_phone"),
    "customer_alternate_phone":    sr_df.get("customer_alternate_phone"),
    "current_name":                sr_df["current_name"],
    "current_phones":              sr_df["current_phones"],
    "total_other_records":         sr_df["total_other_records"],
    "lowest_similarity":           sr_df["lowest_similarity"],
    "phone_overlap_status":        sr_df["phone_overlap_status"],
    "observed_values":             sr_df["observed_values"],
    "conflicting_sr_number":       sr_df["conflicting_sr_number"],
    "conflicting_header_crm_id":   sr_df["conflicting_header_crm_id"],
    "exception_flag":              sr_df["ownership_change"].apply(build_exception_flag),
    "expected_value":              build_expected_value(),
    "reason": sr_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_observed_value(
            r["total_other_records"],
            r["ownership_change"],
            r["lowest_similarity"],
            r["conflicting_sr_number"],
            r["conflicting_header_crm_id"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
    "additional_remarks": sr_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_additional_remarks(
            r["ownership_change"],
            r["lowest_similarity"],
            r["observed_values"],
            r["conflicting_sr_number"],
            r["conflicting_header_crm_id"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
})

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)


test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'no']

# what should be in observed_value

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Exception=yes (ownership change): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no  (consistent):       {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id VARCHAR(255),
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_serial_number VARCHAR(255),
#   customer_name TEXT,
#   calling_from_number TEXT,
#   customer_contact TEXT,
#   customer_registered_phone TEXT,
#   customer_alternate_phone TEXT,
#   current_name TEXT,
#   current_phones TEXT,
#   total_other_records INT,
#   lowest_similarity INT,
#   phone_overlap_status VARCHAR(50),
#   observed_values TEXT,
#   conflicting_sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   conflicting_header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   expected_value TEXT,
#   observed_value TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id)
# )
# """

# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

# "total_other_records",
# "lowest_similarity","phone_overlap_status",
# "observed_values","conflicting_sr_number","conflicting_header_crm_id",


insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "sr_serial_number",
    "customer_name",
    "calling_from_number","customer_contact",
    "customer_registered_phone","customer_alternate_phone",
    "current_name","current_phones",
    "observed_values",
    "exception_flag","expected_value","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1017")

import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime

from rapidfuzz import fuzz

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1017
CHECK_NAME  = "Change in ownership"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1017"

# Similarity threshold for ADDRESS comparison
# If address similarity < 70% AND no phone overlap -> exception (ownership change)
ADDRESS_THRESHOLD = 70

# Customer phone columns to combine
CUSTOMER_PHONE_COLS = [
    "calling_from_number",
    "customer_contact",
    "customer_registered_phone",
    "customer_alternate_phone",
]

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA
# =========================================================
# sr_df = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_base_data ",conn)


sr_df = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM s_crm_claim_hdr_flat WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19'",
    conn
)
print(f"SR rows to process: {len(sr_df)}")

# For grouping by sr_serial_number, pull FULL p_base_data
all_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT header_crm_id, sr_id, sr_number, sr_serial_number, "
    "customer_city, customer_district, customer_state, customer_pincode, "
    "calling_from_number, customer_contact, "
    "customer_registered_phone, customer_alternate_phone "
    "FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_serial_number IS NOT NULL AND sr_serial_number != ''",
    conn
)
print(f"All p_base_data rows for grouping: {len(all_df)}")

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "error", "na", "n/a"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS


def split_multi(v, sep=r"[\^,;/|]"):
    if is_missing(v):
        return []
    return [x.strip() for x in re.split(sep, str(v)) if x.strip()]


def clean_phone_set(v):
    """Return set of cleaned last-10-digit phone numbers."""
    nums = set()
    for part in split_multi(v):
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)
        if len(digits) >= 10:
            nums.add(digits[-10:])
    return nums


def collect_all_phones(row):
    """Union of all phones across the 4 customer phone columns."""
    phones = set()
    for col in CUSTOMER_PHONE_COLS:
        phones |= clean_phone_set(row.get(col))
    return phones


def clean_serial(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())


def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s


def build_address_string(row):
    """City + District + State + Pincode (normalized)."""
    city     = norm_text(row.get("customer_city"))
    district = norm_text(row.get("customer_district"))
    state    = norm_text(row.get("customer_state"))
    pincode  = norm_text(row.get("customer_pincode"))
    return f"{city} | {district} | {state} | {pincode}".strip()

# =========================================================
# BUILD SERIAL -> [RECORDS] LOOKUP
# =========================================================
serial_records = defaultdict(list)

for _, row in all_df.iterrows():
    serial = clean_serial(row.get("sr_serial_number"))
    if not serial:
        continue
    address = build_address_string(row)
    phones  = collect_all_phones(row)

    # Skip totally empty profiles
    if (not address or address.strip(" |") == "") and not phones:
        continue

    serial_records[serial].append({
        "address":       address,
        "phones":        phones,
        "sr_number":     row.get("sr_number"),
        "header_crm_id": row.get("header_crm_id"),
    })

print(f"Distinct serial numbers in lookup: {len(serial_records)}")

# =========================================================
# CHECK FUNCTION
# =========================================================
def check_ownership_change(current_serial, current_sr, current_header,
                           current_address, current_phones):
    """
    Compare current address + phones against OTHER records of the SAME serial
    that have DIFFERENT sr_number AND DIFFERENT header_crm_id.

    Flag = 1 (ownership change) if for ANY such other record:
       - Address similarity < ADDRESS_THRESHOLD (70%), AND
       - There is NO overlap between current phones and other's phones.

    (Phone overlap = same household -> don't flag even if address differs.)
    """
    if not current_serial:
        return 0, 100, "no_phone_match", "", "", "", 0

    records = serial_records.get(current_serial, [])

    # Keep only records with DIFFERENT sr_number AND DIFFERENT header_crm_id
    others = [
        r for r in records
        if (r["sr_number"]     != current_sr)
        and (r["header_crm_id"] != current_header)
    ]

    if not others:
        return 0, 100, "no_others", "", "", "", 0

    # Track conflicting (most-different) match where phones didn't overlap
    conflicting_score   = 100
    conflicting_addr    = ""
    conflicting_sr      = ""
    conflicting_header  = ""
    conflicting_phone_status = "no_phone_match"
    any_flagged   = False

    for r in others:
        addr_score    = fuzz.token_set_ratio(current_address, r["address"]) if current_address and r["address"] else 0
        phone_overlap = bool(current_phones & r["phones"]) if current_phones and r["phones"] else False

        # Flag if address is significantly different AND phones don't overlap
        is_flagged = (addr_score < ADDRESS_THRESHOLD) and (not phone_overlap)

        if is_flagged and addr_score < conflicting_score:
            conflicting_score   = addr_score
            conflicting_addr    = r["address"]
            conflicting_sr      = r["sr_number"]
            conflicting_header  = r["header_crm_id"]
            conflicting_phone_status = "phone_overlap" if phone_overlap else "no_phone_match"
            any_flagged   = True

    flag = 1 if any_flagged else 0
    return (flag, conflicting_score, conflicting_phone_status,
            conflicting_addr, conflicting_sr, conflicting_header, len(others))

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK
# =========================================================
def row_check(r):
    serial     = clean_serial(r.get("sr_serial_number"))
    address    = build_address_string(r)
    phones     = collect_all_phones(r)
    cur_sr     = r.get("sr_number")
    cur_header = r.get("header_crm_id")

    (flag, lowest_score, phone_status,
     conflicting_addr, conflicting_sr, conflicting_header, total_others) = \
        check_ownership_change(serial, cur_sr, cur_header, address, phones)

    return pd.Series({
        "current_address":              address,
        "current_phones":               ", ".join(sorted(phones)) if phones else "",
        "lowest_similarity":            lowest_score,
        "phone_overlap_status":         phone_status,
        "conflicting_address":          conflicting_addr,
        "conflicting_sr_number":        conflicting_sr,
        "conflicting_header_crm_id":    conflicting_header,
        "total_other_records":          total_others,
        "ownership_change":             flag,
    })

check_results = sr_df.apply(row_check, axis=1)
sr_df["current_address"]           = check_results["current_address"]
sr_df["current_phones"]            = check_results["current_phones"]
sr_df["lowest_similarity"]         = check_results["lowest_similarity"].astype(int)
sr_df["phone_overlap_status"]      = check_results["phone_overlap_status"]
sr_df["conflicting_address"]       = check_results["conflicting_address"]
sr_df["conflicting_sr_number"]     = check_results["conflicting_sr_number"]
sr_df["conflicting_header_crm_id"] = check_results["conflicting_header_crm_id"]
sr_df["total_other_records"]       = check_results["total_other_records"].astype(int)
sr_df["ownership_change"]          = check_results["ownership_change"].astype(int)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(flag):
    return "yes" if flag == 1 else "no"

#             f"OR at least one phone number should overlap")

def build_expected_value():
    return ("N/A")


def build_observed_value(total_others, flag, lowest_score, conflicting_sr, conflicting_header):
    if total_others == 0:
        return "No other SR/header found with the same serial number — single owner record"
    if flag == 0:
        return (f"Same serial found in {total_others} other record(s) — "
                f"either address is consistent or phone numbers overlap "
                f"(no ownership change detected)")
    return (f"Same serial found in {total_others} other record(s) — lowest "
            f"address similarity = {lowest_score}% (against "
            f"conflicting_sr_number={conflicting_sr}, "
            f"conflicting_header_crm_id={conflicting_header}) AND no phone "
            f"number overlap")


def build_additional_remarks(flag, lowest_score, conflicting_addr,
                             conflicting_sr, conflicting_header):
    if flag == 0:
        return ("No ownership change detected — address consistent or "
                "phone numbers overlap across records of the same serial")
    return (f"Ownership change detected — same sr_serial_number appears in "
            f"conflicting_sr_number={conflicting_sr}, "
            f"conflicting_header_crm_id={conflicting_header} with a different "
            f"address ({lowest_score}% similarity) AND no overlapping phone "
            f"numbers. Conflicting address: {conflicting_addr}")


output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                    CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                  CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                  now_ts,
    "updated_at":                  now_ts,
    "is_active":                   sr_df.get("is_active"),

    "customer_contact":            sr_df.get("customer_contact"),
    "customer_registered_phone":   sr_df.get("customer_registered_phone"),
    "customer_alternate_phone":    sr_df.get("customer_alternate_phone"),
    "current_address":             sr_df["current_address"],
    "current_phones":              sr_df["current_phones"],

    "lowest_similarity":           sr_df["lowest_similarity"],

        ),

})

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

        conn.rollback()

                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)

# =========================================================
# META

CHECK_ID    = 1003
CHECK_NAME  = "Contact details match with Customer Invoice"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "phone": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 2},
}

# Base columns to compare against unst phone
PHONE_BASE_COLS = [
    "customer_contact",
    "customer_registered_phone",
    "customer_alternate_phone",
    "customer_sr_raise_phone",
]

    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows: {len(unst_df)}")

    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}

merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_df.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "error", "na", "n/a"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS


def split_multi(v, sep=r"[\^,;/|]"):
    if is_missing(v):
        return []
    return [x.strip() for x in re.split(sep, str(v)) if x.strip()]


def last10_set(v):
    """Return set of last-10-digit phone numbers."""
    nums = set()
    for part in split_multi(v):
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)
        if len(digits) >= 10:
            nums.add(digits[-10:])
    return nums


def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()


def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)


def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False


INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found",
    "blank", "unknown", "missing",
    "not applicable",
    "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."
}

# Substrings that should trigger invalid detection anywhere in the string
INVALID_SUBSTRINGS = (
    "not available",
    "not found",
    "not applicable",
    "n/a",
)

def is_invalid(v):
    """
    Returns True if the value is None, NaN, empty, or contains any known
    NA-like token (case-insensitive, whitespace-tolerant).
    """
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    s = str(v).strip().lower()
    if s == "" or s in INVALID_VALUES:
        return True
    # Substring safety net (handles "Not Available", "  not available  ", etc.)
    for token in INVALID_SUBSTRINGS:
        if token in s:
            return True
    return False


def find_matching_phone(unst_set, base_set, t):
    """
    Return the actual matched phone number (from base_set) if any pair matches.
    Prefers exact match first, then fuzzy match.
    """
    if not unst_set or not base_set:
        return None
    # Exact match first
    common = unst_set & base_set
    if common:
        return next(iter(common))
    # Fuzzy match
    for x in unst_set:
        for y in base_set:
            if fuzzy_match(x, y, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
                return y
    return None


def check_phone_against_many(unst_val, base_vals, t=THRESHOLDS["phone"]):
    """
    Returns:
        match_flag_str, matched_phone, matched_column

    match_flag_str:
        "yes" = Matched with at least one base column
                OR observed value is 'Not available' / invalid (skip check -> yes)
        "no"  = Not matched
    """
    # If OBSERVED (invoice) value is invalid / not available -> treat as MATCH
    if is_invalid(unst_val):
        return "yes", "", ""

    unst_set = last10_set(unst_val)
    if not unst_set:
        return "yes", "", ""

    found_valid_base = False

    for col_name, val in base_vals.items():
        if is_invalid(val):
            continue

        base_set = last10_set(val)
        if not base_set:
            continue

        found_valid_base = True

        matched_phone = find_matching_phone(unst_set, base_set, t)
        if matched_phone:
            return "yes", matched_phone, col_name

    # If no valid base numbers to compare against, treat as match (skip)
    if not found_valid_base:
        return "yes", "", ""

    # Valid numbers were compared but no match found
    return "no", "", ""

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK
# =========================================================
def row_check(r):
    base_vals = {c: r.get(c) for c in PHONE_BASE_COLS}

    match_flag, matched_phone, matched_col = check_phone_against_many(
        r.get("customer_phone_number_unst_str"),
        base_vals
    )

    return pd.Series({
        "customer_contact_match": match_flag,           # "yes" or "no"
        "matched_phone":          matched_phone,         # actual matched number
        "matched_with_column":    matched_col            # base column name
    })


check_results = merged_df.apply(row_check, axis=1)
merged_df["customer_contact_match"] = check_results["customer_contact_match"]
merged_df["matched_phone"]          = check_results["matched_phone"]
merged_df["matched_with_column"]    = check_results["matched_with_column"]

# =========================================================
# SAFETY NET — force yes/no correctly when observed is invalid
# =========================================================
# This guarantees that regardless of anything above, any row where
# customer_phone_number_unst_str is invalid/NA becomes match="yes".
observed_is_invalid_mask = merged_df["customer_phone_number_unst_str"].apply(is_invalid)
merged_df.loc[observed_is_invalid_mask, "customer_contact_match"] = "yes"
merged_df.loc[observed_is_invalid_mask, "matched_phone"]          = ""
merged_df.loc[observed_is_invalid_mask, "matched_with_column"]    = ""

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(match_flag):
    # match=yes -> exception=no ;  match=no -> exception=yes
    return "no" if match_flag == "yes" else "yes"


def build_reason(match_flag, matched_phone, matched_col):
    if match_flag == "yes":
        if matched_phone:
            return (f"Customer phone number {matched_phone} matched with "
                    f"'{matched_col}'")
        return "Customer phone number is matching"
    return "Customer contact number is not matching with any of the phone numbers"


def build_additional_remarks(match_flag, matched_phone, matched_col):
    if match_flag == "yes":
        if matched_phone:
            return (f"Customer phone number from invoice ({matched_phone}) "
                    f"matched with '{matched_col}' in p_base_data")
        return "Customer phone number is matching"
    return ("Customer phone number from invoice did not match with any of: "
            "customer_contact, customer_registered_phone, "
            "customer_alternate_phone, customer_sr_raise_phone")


output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                                  CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                                CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                                now_ts,
    "updated_at":                                now_ts,
    "is_active":                                 merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                             merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                                 merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                                  merged_df["attch_id"],
    "category":                                  merged_df.get("category"),
    "customer_phone_number_observed_value":      merged_df.get("customer_phone_number_unst_str"),
    "customer_contact_expected_value":           merged_df.get("customer_contact"),
    "customer_registered_phone_expected_value":  merged_df.get("customer_registered_phone"),
    "customer_alternate_phone_expected_value":   merged_df.get("customer_alternate_phone"),
    "customer_sr_raise_phone_expected_value":    merged_df.get("customer_sr_raise_phone"),
    "customer_contact_match":                    merged_df["customer_contact_match"],
    "matched_with_column": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: (f"{r['matched_phone']} (in {r['matched_with_column']})"
                   if r["matched_phone"] else ""),
        axis=1
    ),
    "exception_flag": merged_df["customer_contact_match"].apply(build_exception_flag),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_reason(
            r["customer_contact_match"], r["matched_phone"], r["matched_with_column"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
    "additional_remarks": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_additional_remarks(
            r["customer_contact_match"], r["matched_phone"], r["matched_with_column"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
})


output_df['additional_remarks'] = 'NA'

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)


test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

# ==== Diagnostic prints (to confirm the fix works) ====
print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Match=yes (matched):    {(output_df['customer_contact_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Match=no  (not matched):{(output_df['customer_contact_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes:          {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no:           {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")

# Verify no "Not available" rows have exception=yes
na_but_flagged = output_df[
    output_df['customer_phone_number_observed_value'].apply(is_invalid) &
    (output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes')
]
print(f"Rows with observed=NA but exception=yes (should be 0): {len(na_but_flagged)}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id VARCHAR(255),
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   customer_phone_number_unst_str TEXT,
#   customer_contact TEXT,
#   customer_registered_phone TEXT,
#   customer_alternate_phone TEXT,
#   customer_sr_raise_phone TEXT,
#   customer_contact_match TINYINT,
#   matched_with_column VARCHAR(100),
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   observed_value TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id)
# )
# """

# # cursor.execute(create_sql)
# # conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "customer_phone_number_observed_value",
    "customer_contact_expected_value",
    "customer_registered_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_alternate_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_sr_raise_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_contact_match","matched_with_column",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols
               if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1003")


































#!/usr/bin/env python
# coding: utf-8

import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1003
CHECK_NAME  = "Contact details match with Customer Invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1003"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "phone": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 2},
}

# Base columns to compare against unst phone
PHONE_BASE_COLS = [
    "customer_contact",
    "customer_registered_phone",
    "customer_alternate_phone",
    "customer_sr_raise_phone",
]

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows: {len(unst_df)}")

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id", "attch_id"]

unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# MERGE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(
    base_df,
    unst_df.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS),
    on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left"
)
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "error", "na", "n/a"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS


def split_multi(v, sep=r"[\^,;/|]"):
    if is_missing(v):
        return []
    return [x.strip() for x in re.split(sep, str(v)) if x.strip()]


def last10_set(v):
    """Return set of last-10-digit phone numbers."""
    nums = set()
    for part in split_multi(v):
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)
        if len(digits) >= 10:
            nums.add(digits[-10:])
    return nums


def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()


def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)


def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False


INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found"
}

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES


def find_matching_phone(unst_set, base_set, t):
    """
    Return the actual matched phone number (from base_set) if any pair matches.
    Prefers exact match first, then fuzzy match.
    """
    if not unst_set or not base_set:
        return None
    # Exact match first
    common = unst_set & base_set
    if common:
        return next(iter(common))
    # Fuzzy match
    for x in unst_set:
        for y in base_set:
            if fuzzy_match(x, y, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
                return y
    return None


def check_phone_against_many(unst_val, base_vals, t=THRESHOLDS["phone"]):
    """
    Returns:
        match_flag_str, matched_phone, matched_column

    match_flag_str:
        "yes" = Matched with at least one base column
        "no"  = Not matched (or comparable data missing -> treated as no match)
    """
    if is_invalid(unst_val):
        return "no", "", ""

    unst_set = last10_set(unst_val)
    if not unst_set:
        return "no", "", ""

    found_valid_base = False

    for col_name, val in base_vals.items():
        if is_invalid(val):
            continue

        base_set = last10_set(val)
        if not base_set:
            continue

        found_valid_base = True

        matched_phone = find_matching_phone(unst_set, base_set, t)
        if matched_phone:
            return "yes", matched_phone, col_name

    # If no valid base numbers to compare against, treat as no match
    if not found_valid_base:
        return "no", "", ""

    # Valid numbers were compared but no match found
    return "no", "", ""

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK
# =========================================================
def row_check(r):
    base_vals = {c: r.get(c) for c in PHONE_BASE_COLS}

    match_flag, matched_phone, matched_col = check_phone_against_many(
        r.get("customer_phone_number_unst_str"),
        base_vals
    )

    return pd.Series({
        "customer_contact_match": match_flag,           # "yes" or "no"
        "matched_phone":          matched_phone,         # actual matched number
        "matched_with_column":    matched_col            # base column name
    })


check_results = merged_df.apply(row_check, axis=1)
merged_df["customer_contact_match"] = check_results["customer_contact_match"]
merged_df["matched_phone"]          = check_results["matched_phone"]
merged_df["matched_with_column"]    = check_results["matched_with_column"]

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(match_flag):
    # match=yes -> exception=no ;  match=no -> exception=yes
    return "no" if match_flag == "yes" else "yes"


def build_reason(match_flag, matched_phone, matched_col):
    if match_flag == "yes":
        return (f"Customer phone number {matched_phone} matched with "
                f"'{matched_col}'")
    return "Customer contact number is not matching with any of the phone numbers"


def build_additional_remarks(match_flag, matched_phone, matched_col):
    if match_flag == "yes":
        return (f"Customer phone number from invoice ({matched_phone}) matched "
                f"with '{matched_col}' in p_base_data")
    return ("Customer phone number from invoice did not match with any of: "
            "customer_contact, customer_registered_phone, "
            "customer_alternate_phone, customer_sr_raise_phone")


output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                                  CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                                CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                                now_ts,
    "updated_at":                                now_ts,
    "is_active":                                 merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                             merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                                 merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                                  merged_df["attch_id"],
    "category":                                  merged_df.get("category"),
    "customer_phone_number_observed_value":      merged_df.get("customer_phone_number_unst_str"),
    "customer_contact_expected_value":           merged_df.get("customer_contact"),
    "customer_registered_phone_expected_value":  merged_df.get("customer_registered_phone"),
    "customer_alternate_phone_expected_value":   merged_df.get("customer_alternate_phone"),
    "customer_sr_raise_phone_expected_value":    merged_df.get("customer_sr_raise_phone"),
    "customer_contact_match":                    merged_df["customer_contact_match"],
    "matched_with_column": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: (f"{r['matched_phone']} (in {r['matched_with_column']})"
                   if r["matched_phone"] else ""),
        axis=1
    ),
    "exception_flag": merged_df["customer_contact_match"].apply(build_exception_flag),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_reason(
            r["customer_contact_match"], r["matched_phone"], r["matched_with_column"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
    "additional_remarks": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_additional_remarks(
            r["customer_contact_match"], r["matched_phone"], r["matched_with_column"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
})


output_df['additional_remarks']='NA'

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)


test=output_df[output_df['exception_flag']=='yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Match=yes (matched):    {(output_df['customer_contact_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Match=no  (not matched):{(output_df['customer_contact_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes:          {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no:           {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id VARCHAR(255),
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   customer_phone_number_unst_str TEXT,
#   customer_contact TEXT,
#   customer_registered_phone TEXT,
#   customer_alternate_phone TEXT,
#   customer_sr_raise_phone TEXT,
#   customer_contact_match TINYINT,
#   matched_with_column VARCHAR(100),
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   observed_value TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id)
# )
# """

# # cursor.execute(create_sql)
# # conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "customer_phone_number_observed_value",
    "customer_contact_expected_value",
    "customer_registered_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_alternate_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_sr_raise_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_contact_match","matched_with_column",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols
               if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1003")
