    return ("Customer phone number from invoice did not match with any of: "
            "customer_contact, customer_registered_phone, "
            "customer_alternate_phone, customer_sr_raise_phone")


output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                                  CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                                CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                                now_ts,
    "updated_at":                                now_ts,
    "is_active":                                 merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                             merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                                 merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                                  merged_df["attch_id"],
    "category":                                  merged_df.get("category"),
    "customer_phone_number_observed_value":      merged_df.get("customer_phone_number_unst_str"),
    "customer_contact_expected_value":           merged_df.get("customer_contact"),
    "customer_registered_phone_expected_value":  merged_df.get("customer_registered_phone"),
    "customer_alternate_phone_expected_value":   merged_df.get("customer_alternate_phone"),
    "customer_sr_raise_phone_expected_value":    merged_df.get("customer_sr_raise_phone"),
    "customer_contact_match":                    merged_df["customer_contact_match"],
    "matched_with_column": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: (f"{r['matched_phone']} (in {r['matched_with_column']})"
                   if r["matched_phone"] else ""),
        axis=1
    ),
    "exception_flag": merged_df["customer_contact_match"].apply(build_exception_flag),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_reason(
            r["customer_contact_match"], r["matched_phone"], r["matched_with_column"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
    "additional_remarks": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_additional_remarks(
            r["customer_contact_match"], r["matched_phone"], r["matched_with_column"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
})


output_df['additional_remarks']='NA'

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)


test=output_df[output_df['exception_flag']=='yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Match=yes (matched):    {(output_df['customer_contact_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Match=no  (not matched):{(output_df['customer_contact_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes:          {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no:           {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id VARCHAR(255),
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   customer_phone_number_unst_str TEXT,
#   customer_contact TEXT,
#   customer_registered_phone TEXT,
#   customer_alternate_phone TEXT,
#   customer_sr_raise_phone TEXT,
#   customer_contact_match TINYINT,
#   matched_with_column VARCHAR(100),
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   observed_value TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id)
# )
# """

# # cursor.execute(create_sql)
# # conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "customer_phone_number_observed_value",
    "customer_contact_expected_value",
    "customer_registered_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_alternate_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_sr_raise_phone_expected_value",
    "customer_contact_match","matched_with_column",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols
               if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1003")

#!/usr/bin/env python
# coding: utf-8

import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1002
CHECK_NAME  = "Dealer name and GST match with customer invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1002"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "dealer_name": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 3},
    "gstin":       {"ratio": 0.85, "max_edits": 2},
}

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows: {len(unst_df)}")

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id", "attch_id"]

unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# MERGE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(base_df, unst_df.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS), on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left")
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "error", "na", "n/a"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS


def norm_alnum_upper(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())


def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s


BUSINESS_SUFFIXES = {
    "pvt", "private", "ltd", "limited", "llp", "inc", "co", "company",
    "corp", "corporation", "enterprises", "enterprise", "trader", "traders",
    "trading", "agency", "agencies", "sales", "services", "service",
    "and", "the", "of"
}

def norm_dealer_name(v):
    s = norm_text(v)
    if not s:
        return ""
    tokens = [t for t in s.split() if t not in BUSINESS_SUFFIXES]
    return " ".join(tokens)


def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()


def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)


def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False


# def check_dealer_name(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
#     a, b = norm_dealer_name(a), norm_dealer_name(b)
#     if not a or not b:
#         return 0
#     score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a, b)            # 0-100
#     if score >= t["ratio"] * 100:
#         return 1
#     return int(edit_distance(a, b) <= t["max_edits"])


# def check_gstin(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):
#     a, b = norm_alnum_upper(a), norm_alnum_upper(b)
#     if not a or not b:
#         return 0
#     if a == b:
#         return 1
#     if len(a) < 12 or len(b) < 12:
#         return 0
#     return int(fuzzy_match(a, b, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]))

INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "error",
    "na", "n/a", "not found",
    "blank", "unknown", "missing",
    "-", "--", "n.a", "n.a."
}

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES


def check_dealer_name(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
    """
    a = dealer_name (expected / p_base_data)
    b = dealer_name_unst_str (observed / invoice OCR)

    Returns:
        "yes" = matching (or EITHER side is 'not available' / invalid -> treat as match)
        "no"  = not matching
    """

    # If EITHER value is invalid / not available -> treat as MATCH
    if is_invalid(a) or is_invalid(b):
        return "yes"

    a_norm, b_norm = norm_dealer_name(a), norm_dealer_name(b)

    # If either becomes empty after normalization -> treat as match
    if not a_norm or not b_norm:
        return "yes"

    score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a_norm, b_norm)  # 0-100

    if score >= t["ratio"] * 100:
        return "yes"

    if edit_distance(a_norm, b_norm) <= t["max_edits"]:
        return "yes"

    return "no"


def check_gstin(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):
    """
    a = dealer_gst (expected / p_base_data)
    b = dealer_gst_number_unst_str (observed / invoice OCR)

    Returns:
        "yes" = matching (or EITHER side is 'not available' / invalid -> treat as match)
        "no"  = not matching
    """

    # If EITHER value is invalid / not available -> treat as MATCH
    if is_invalid(a) or is_invalid(b):
        return "yes"

    a_norm, b_norm = norm_alnum_upper(a), norm_alnum_upper(b)

    # If either becomes empty after normalization -> treat as match
    if not a_norm or not b_norm:
        return "yes"

    if a_norm == b_norm:
        return "yes"

    if len(a_norm) < 12 or len(b_norm) < 12:
        return "no"

    if fuzzy_match(a_norm, b_norm, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
        return "yes"

    return "no"


# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECKS
# =========================================================
merged_df["dealer_name_match"] = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_dealer_name(r.get("dealer_name"), r.get("dealer_name_unst_str")),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["dealer_gst_match"] = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_gstin(r.get("dealer_gst"), r.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str")),
    axis=1
)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(name_match, gst_match):
    # Exception = "yes" if EITHER name or GST does NOT match
    if name_match == "no" or gst_match == "no":
        return "yes"
    return "no"


def build_observed_value(name_match, gst_match):
    name_txt = (
        "dealer name is matching"
        if name_match == "yes"
        else "dealer name is not matching"
    )

    gst_txt = (
        "GST number is matching"
        if gst_match == "yes"
        else "GST number is not matching"
    )

    return f"{name_txt}; {gst_txt}"


def build_additional_remarks(name_match, gst_match):
    if name_match == "yes" and gst_match == "yes":
        return "Both dealer name and GST number are matching with customer invoice"

    if name_match == "yes" and gst_match == "no":
        return "Dealer name is matching but GST number is not matching with customer invoice"

    if name_match == "no" and gst_match == "yes":
        return "GST number is matching but dealer name is not matching with customer invoice"

    return "Both dealer name and GST number are not matching with customer invoice"


output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                       CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                     CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                     now_ts,
    "updated_at":                     now_ts,
    "is_active":                      merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                  merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                      merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                       merged_df["attch_id"],
    "category":                       merged_df.get("category"),
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value":    merged_df.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
    "dealer_gst_observed_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
    "dealer_name_expected_value":     merged_df.get("dealer_name"),
    "dealer_gst_expected_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst"),
    "dealer_name_match":              merged_df["dealer_name_match"],
    "dealer_gst_match":               merged_df["dealer_gst_match"],
    "exception_flag": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_exception_flag(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_observed_value(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "additional_remarks": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_additional_remarks(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
})

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)


test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Name match=yes:  {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Name match=no:   {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=yes:   {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=no:    {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no (both match):            {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes (one or both mismatch): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id VARCHAR(255),
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   dealer_name_unst_str TEXT,
#   dealer_gst_number_unst_str TEXT,
#   dealer_name TEXT,
#   dealer_gst TEXT,
#   dealer_name_match TINYINT,
#   dealer_gst_match TINYINT,
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   observed_value TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id)
# )
# """

# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()


insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value",
    "dealer_gst_observed_value",
    "dealer_name_expected_value",
    "dealer_gst_expected_value",
    "dealer_name_match","dealer_gst_match",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1002")

        return True
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES


def check_dealer_name(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
    """
    a = dealer_name (expected / p_base_data)
    b = dealer_name_unst_str (observed / invoice OCR)

    Returns:
        "yes" = matching (or observed value is 'not available' -> treat as match)
        "no"  = not matching
    """

    # If OBSERVED (invoice) value is invalid / not available -> treat as MATCH
    if is_invalid(b):
        return "yes"

    # If EXPECTED value is invalid -> cannot match
    if is_invalid(a):
        return "no"

    a_norm, b_norm = norm_dealer_name(a), norm_dealer_name(b)

    if not a_norm or not b_norm:
        # If observed became empty after normalization, treat as match
        if not b_norm:
            return "yes"
        return "no"

    score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a_norm, b_norm)  # 0-100

    if score >= t["ratio"] * 100:
        return "yes"

    if edit_distance(a_norm, b_norm) <= t["max_edits"]:
        return "yes"

    return "no"


def check_gstin(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):
    """
    a = dealer_gst (expected / p_base_data)
    b = dealer_gst_number_unst_str (observed / invoice OCR)

    Returns:
        "yes" = matching (or observed value is 'not available' -> treat as match)
        "no"  = not matching
    """

    # If OBSERVED (invoice) value is invalid / not available -> treat as MATCH
    if is_invalid(b):
        return "yes"

    # If EXPECTED value is invalid -> cannot match
    if is_invalid(a):
        return "no"

    a_norm, b_norm = norm_alnum_upper(a), norm_alnum_upper(b)

    if not a_norm or not b_norm:
        if not b_norm:
            return "yes"
        return "no"

    if a_norm == b_norm:
        return "yes"

    if len(a_norm) < 12 or len(b_norm) < 12:
        return "no"

    if fuzzy_match(a_norm, b_norm, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
        return "yes"

    return "no"


# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECKS
# =========================================================
merged_df["dealer_name_match"] = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_dealer_name(r.get("dealer_name"), r.get("dealer_name_unst_str")),
    axis=1
)

merged_df["dealer_gst_match"] = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_gstin(r.get("dealer_gst"), r.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str")),
    axis=1
)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(name_match, gst_match):
    # Exception = "yes" if EITHER name or GST does NOT match
    if name_match == "no" or gst_match == "no":
        return "yes"
    return "no"


def build_observed_value(name_match, gst_match):
    name_txt = (
        "dealer name is matching"
        if name_match == "yes"
        else "dealer name is not matching"
    )

    gst_txt = (
        "GST number is matching"
        if gst_match == "yes"
        else "GST number is not matching"
    )

    return f"{name_txt}; {gst_txt}"


def build_additional_remarks(name_match, gst_match):
    if name_match == "yes" and gst_match == "yes":
        return "Both dealer name and GST number are matching with customer invoice"

    if name_match == "yes" and gst_match == "no":
        return "Dealer name is matching but GST number is not matching with customer invoice"

    if name_match == "no" and gst_match == "yes":
        return "GST number is matching but dealer name is not matching with customer invoice"

    return "Both dealer name and GST number are not matching with customer invoice"


output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                       CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                     CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                     now_ts,
    "updated_at":                     now_ts,
    "is_active":                      merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                  merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                      merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                       merged_df["attch_id"],
    "category":                       merged_df.get("category"),
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value":    merged_df.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
    "dealer_gst_observed_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
    "dealer_name_expected_value":     merged_df.get("dealer_name"),
    "dealer_gst_expected_value":      merged_df.get("dealer_gst"),
    "dealer_name_match":              merged_df["dealer_name_match"],
    "dealer_gst_match":               merged_df["dealer_gst_match"],
    "exception_flag": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_exception_flag(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_observed_value(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "additional_remarks": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_additional_remarks(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
})

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)


test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Name match=yes:  {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Name match=no:   {(output_df['dealer_name_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=yes:   {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"GST match=no:    {(output_df['dealer_gst_match']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no (both match):            {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes (one or both mismatch): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id VARCHAR(255),
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   dealer_name_unst_str TEXT,
#   dealer_gst_number_unst_str TEXT,
#   dealer_name TEXT,
#   dealer_gst TEXT,
#   dealer_name_match TINYINT,
#   dealer_gst_match TINYINT,
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   observed_value TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id)
# )
# """

# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()


insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value",
    "dealer_gst_observed_value",
    "dealer_name_expected_value",
    "dealer_gst_expected_value",
    "dealer_name_match","dealer_gst_match",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1002")

# coding: utf-8

# In[2]:


import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
from difflib import SequenceMatcher
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from rapidfuzz.distance import Levenshtein

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1002
CHECK_NAME  = "Dealer name and GST match with customer invoice"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1002"

# =========================================================
# THRESHOLDS
# =========================================================
THRESHOLDS = {
    "dealer_name": {"ratio": 0.80, "max_edits": 3},
    "gstin":       {"ratio": 0.85, "max_edits": 2},
}

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA
# =========================================================
base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
    "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
    "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
    conn
)
unst_df = pd.read_sql("SELECT * FROM p_unst_str_customer_invoice", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")
print(f"unst_str_customer_invoice rows: {len(unst_df)}")

# =========================================================
# RENAME COLUMNS
# =========================================================
JOIN_KEYS = ["header_crm_id", "sr_id", "attch_id"]

unst_df = unst_df.rename(
    columns={c: f"{c}_unst_str" for c in unst_df.columns if c not in JOIN_KEYS}
)

# =========================================================
# MERGE
# =========================================================
merged_df = pd.merge(base_df, unst_df.drop_duplicates(subset=JOIN_KEYS), on=JOIN_KEYS, how="left")
merged_df = merged_df.where(pd.notnull(merged_df), None)

print(f"Merged rows: {len(merged_df)}")

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "error", "na", "n/a"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS


def norm_alnum_upper(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    return re.sub(r"[^A-Z0-9]", "", str(v).upper())


def norm_text(v):
    if is_missing(v):
        return ""
    s = str(v).lower()
    s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\s]", " ", s)
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip()
    return s


BUSINESS_SUFFIXES = {
    "pvt", "private", "ltd", "limited", "llp", "inc", "co", "company",
    "corp", "corporation", "enterprises", "enterprise", "trader", "traders",
    "trading", "agency", "agencies", "sales", "services", "service",
    "and", "the", "of"
}

def norm_dealer_name(v):
    s = norm_text(v)
    if not s:
        return ""
    tokens = [t for t in s.split() if t not in BUSINESS_SUFFIXES]
    return " ".join(tokens)


def seq_ratio(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return 0.0
    return SequenceMatcher(None, a, b).ratio()


def edit_distance(a, b):
    if not a or not b:
        return max(len(a or ""), len(b or ""))
    return Levenshtein.distance(a, b)


def fuzzy_match(a, b, ratio_threshold, max_edits):
    if not a or not b:
        return False
    if a == b:
        return True
    if seq_ratio(a, b) >= ratio_threshold:
        return True
    if edit_distance(a, b) <= max_edits:
        return True
    return False


# def check_dealer_name(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
#     a, b = norm_dealer_name(a), norm_dealer_name(b)
#     if not a or not b:
#         return 0
#     score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a, b)            # 0-100
#     if score >= t["ratio"] * 100:
#         return 1
#     return int(edit_distance(a, b) <= t["max_edits"])


# def check_gstin(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):
#     a, b = norm_alnum_upper(a), norm_alnum_upper(b)
#     if not a or not b:
#         return 0
#     if a == b:
#         return 1
#     if len(a) < 12 or len(b) < 12:
#         return 0
#     return int(fuzzy_match(a, b, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]))

INVALID_VALUES = {
    "", "null", "none", "nan",
    "not available", "error",
    "na", "n/a","not found"
}

def is_invalid(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    return str(v).strip().lower() in INVALID_VALUES


def check_dealer_name(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["dealer_name"]):
    if is_invalid(a) or is_invalid(b):
        return 0

    a, b = norm_dealer_name(a), norm_dealer_name(b)

    if not a or not b:
        return 0

    score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(a, b)  # 0-100

    # Match -> 0
    if score >= t["ratio"] * 100:
        return 0

    if edit_distance(a, b) <= t["max_edits"]:
        return 0

    # Not Match -> Exception
    return 1


def check_gstin(a, b, t=THRESHOLDS["gstin"]):
    if is_invalid(a) or is_invalid(b):
        return 0

    a, b = norm_alnum_upper(a), norm_alnum_upper(b)

    if not a or not b:
        return 0

    # Match -> 0
    if a == b:
        return 0

    if len(a) < 12 or len(b) < 12:
        return 0

    # Fuzzy Match -> 0
    if fuzzy_match(a, b, t["ratio"], t["max_edits"]):
        return 0

    # Not Match -> Exception
    return 1


# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECKS
# =========================================================
merged_df["dealer_name_match"] = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_dealer_name(r.get("dealer_name"), r.get("dealer_name_unst_str")),
    axis=1
).astype(int)

merged_df["dealer_gst_match"] = merged_df.apply(
    lambda r: check_gstin(r.get("dealer_gst"), r.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str")),
    axis=1
).astype(int)

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(name_match, gst_match):
    # 1 = exception (mismatch)
    if name_match == 1 or gst_match == 1:
        return "Yes"
    return "No"


def build_observed_value(name_match, gst_match):
    name_txt = (
        "dealer name is not matching"
        if name_match == 1
        else "dealer name is matching"
    )

    gst_txt = (
        "GST number is not matching"
        if gst_match == 1
        else "GST number is matching"
    )

    return f"{name_txt}; {gst_txt}"


def build_additional_remarks(name_match, gst_match):
    if name_match == 0 and gst_match == 0:
        return "Both dealer name and GST number are matching with customer invoice"

    if name_match == 0 and gst_match == 1:
        return "Dealer name is matching but GST number is not matching with customer invoice"

    if name_match == 1 and gst_match == 0:
        return "GST number is matching but dealer name is not matching with customer invoice"

    return "Both dealer name and GST number are not matching with customer invoice"

output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                       CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                     CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                     now_ts,
    "updated_at":                     now_ts,
    "is_active":                      merged_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":                  merged_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                      merged_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                       merged_df["attch_id"],
    "category":                       merged_df.get("category"),
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value":           merged_df.get("dealer_name_unst_str"),
    "dealer_gst_observed_value":     merged_df.get("dealer_gst_number_unst_str"),
    "dealer_name_expected_value":                    merged_df.get("dealer_name"),
    "dealer_gst_expected_value":                     merged_df.get("dealer_gst"),
    "dealer_name_match":              merged_df["dealer_name_match"],
    "dealer_gst_match":               merged_df["dealer_gst_match"],
    "exception_flag": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_exception_flag(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "reason": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_observed_value(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
    "additional_remarks": merged_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_additional_remarks(r["dealer_name_match"], r["dealer_gst_match"]),
        axis=1
    ),
})

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)





test=output_df[output_df['exception_flag']=='es']

print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Exception=no (both match): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=yes (one or both mismatch): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id VARCHAR(255),
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   dealer_name_unst_str TEXT,
#   dealer_gst_number_unst_str TEXT,
#   dealer_name TEXT,
#   dealer_gst TEXT,
#   dealer_name_match TINYINT,
#   dealer_gst_match TINYINT,
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   observed_value TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id)
# )
# """

# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()
  


insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at", "is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "dealer_name_obeserved_value",
    "dealer_gst_observed_value",
    "dealer_name_expected_value",
    "dealer_gst_expected_value",
    "dealer_name_match","dealer_gst_match",
    "exception_flag","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id", "created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()

import os
import re
import time
import pymysql
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime

# =========================================================
# DB CONFIG
# =========================================================
HOST     = 'vl-fida-crm-mysql-flexible-preprod.mysql.database.azure.com'
USER     = 'fidaCRMAdminUser'
PASSWORD = 'IoC2OuNePtR&]94A'
DATABASE = 'vl-fida-crm-db-preprod'

for var_name, var_val in [("DB_HOST", HOST), ("DB_USER", USER),
                          ("DB_PASSWORD", PASSWORD), ("DB_DATABASE", DATABASE)]:
    if not var_val:
        raise ValueError(f"{var_name} environment variable is missing.")

ssl_config = {"ssl_verify_identity": True}

conn = pymysql.connect(
    host=HOST, user=USER, password=PASSWORD, database=DATABASE,
    port=3306, ssl=ssl_config
)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# =========================================================
# META
# =========================================================
CHECK_ID    = 1015
CHECK_NAME  = "Contact number validation from technician record"
NEW_TABLE   = "p_table_1015"

# Customer contact fields to validate
CUSTOMER_PHONE_COLS = [
    "calling_from_number",
    "customer_contact",
    "customer_registered_phone",
    "customer_alternate_phone",
]

# Path to technician master Excel file
TECH_MASTER_EXCEL = r"technician_master.xlsx"   # <-- update this path if needed

# =========================================================
# LOAD DATA
# =========================================================
# base_df = pd.read_sql(
#     "SELECT * FROM p_base_data "
#     "WHERE sr_open_date >= '2025-01-16' "
#     "AND sr_open_date < '2025-01-19' "
#     "AND LOWER(category) IN ('invoice', 'bill', 'customer payment')",
#     conn
# )

base_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT * FROM p_base_data ", conn)

print(f"p_base_data rows: {len(base_df)}")

# ---- Build technician phone master set from p_base_data ----
tech_phones_df = pd.read_sql(
    "SELECT DISTINCT tech_id, tech_name, tech_phone "
    "FROM p_base_data "
    "WHERE tech_phone IS NOT NULL AND tech_phone != ''",
    conn
)
print(f"Distinct technician phone records from p_base_data: {len(tech_phones_df)}")

# ---- Also load technician master Excel (specific columns only) ----
try:
    tech_master_df = pd.read_excel(
        TECH_MASTER_EXCEL,
        usecols=["Tech Id", "First Name", "Last Name", "Cell Phone #"]
    )

    # Combine first + last name into one name field
    tech_master_df["tech_name"] = (
        tech_master_df["First Name"].fillna("").astype(str).str.strip() + " " +
        tech_master_df["Last Name"].fillna("").astype(str).str.strip()
    ).str.strip()

    # Rename to match p_base_data schema
    tech_master_df = tech_master_df.rename(columns={
        "Tech Id":      "tech_id",
        "Cell Phone #": "tech_phone",
    })

    tech_master_df = tech_master_df[["tech_id", "tech_name", "tech_phone"]]
    print(f"Technician master (Excel) rows: {len(tech_master_df)}")
except Exception as e:
    print(f"[WARN] Could not read technician master Excel: {e}")
    tech_master_df = pd.DataFrame(columns=["tech_id", "tech_name", "tech_phone"])

# ---- Combine both sources ----
combined_tech_df = pd.concat([tech_phones_df, tech_master_df], ignore_index=True)
combined_tech_df = combined_tech_df.dropna(subset=["tech_phone"])
combined_tech_df = combined_tech_df[combined_tech_df["tech_phone"].astype(str).str.strip() != ""]
combined_tech_df = combined_tech_df.drop_duplicates(subset=["tech_id", "tech_phone"])
print(f"Total combined technician records: {len(combined_tech_df)}")

# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================
NA_TOKENS = {"", "none", "null", "nan", "not available", "error", "na", "n/a"}

def is_missing(v):
    if v is None:
        return True
    try:
        if pd.isna(v):
            return True
    except Exception:
        pass
    return str(v).strip().lower() in NA_TOKENS


def split_multi(v, sep=r"[\^,;/|]"):
    """Split a value on common multi-value separators."""
    if is_missing(v):
        return []
    return [x.strip() for x in re.split(sep, str(v)) if x.strip()]


def clean_phone_set(v):
    """
    Normal cleaning of phone numbers:
      - split on ^ , ; / |
      - remove ALL non-digit characters (spaces, +, -, (), etc.)
      - keep only last 10 digits
      - drop entries that don't have at least 10 digits
    Returns a set of cleaned 10-digit phone numbers.
    """
    nums = set()
    for part in split_multi(v):
        digits = re.sub(r"\D", "", part)   # keep digits only
        if len(digits) >= 10:
            nums.add(digits[-10:])
    return nums

# =========================================================
# BUILD TECHNICIAN PHONE LOOKUP (exact only)
# =========================================================
# Map: cleaned 10-digit phone -> list of (tech_id, tech_name)
tech_phone_lookup = {}
for _, row in combined_tech_df.iterrows():
    for p in clean_phone_set(row.get("tech_phone")):
        tech_phone_lookup.setdefault(p, []).append(
            (row.get("tech_id"), row.get("tech_name"))
        )

tech_phone_set = set(tech_phone_lookup.keys())
print(f"Total distinct technician phones (cleaned): {len(tech_phone_set)}")

# =========================================================
# CHECK FUNCTION (EXACT MATCH ONLY)
# =========================================================
def check_customer_phones_vs_tech(customer_vals):
    """
    customer_vals: dict {col_name: value}
    Returns:
      flag (0/1)         -> 1 if ANY cleaned customer phone exactly matches ANY cleaned tech phone
      observed_values    -> "9876543210 (from customer_contact)"
      matched_tech_info  -> "Tech ID: T123 | Name: Ramesh | Phone: 9876543210"
      matched_cust_cols  -> "customer_contact"
    """
    hits = []  # (cust_phone, cust_col, tech_id, tech_name)

    for col_name, val in customer_vals.items():
        cust_phones = clean_phone_set(val)
        if not cust_phones:
            continue

        # Exact intersection only
        exact_matches = cust_phones & tech_phone_set
        for p in exact_matches:
            for tid, tname in tech_phone_lookup.get(p, []):
                hits.append((p, col_name, tid, tname))

    if not hits:
        return 0, "", "", ""

    # Deduplicate hits
    seen = set()
    uniq = []
    for h in hits:
        key = (h[0], h[1], h[2])
        if key not in seen:
            seen.add(key)
            uniq.append(h)

    observed_values   = "; ".join([f"{h[0]} (from {h[1]})" for h in uniq])
    matched_tech_info = "; ".join([f"Tech ID: {h[2]} | Name: {h[3]} | Phone: {h[0]}" for h in uniq])
    matched_cust_cols = ", ".join(sorted({h[1] for h in uniq}))

    return 1, observed_values, matched_tech_info, matched_cust_cols

# =========================================================
# APPLY CHECK
# =========================================================
def row_check(r):
    customer_vals = {c: r.get(c) for c in CUSTOMER_PHONE_COLS}
    flag, observed_values, matched_tech_info, matched_cust_cols = \
        check_customer_phones_vs_tech(customer_vals)

    return pd.Series({
        "tech_phone_match":  flag,
        "observed_values":   observed_values,
        "matched_tech_info": matched_tech_info,
        "matched_cust_cols": matched_cust_cols,
    })

check_results = base_df.apply(row_check, axis=1)
base_df["tech_phone_match"]  = check_results["tech_phone_match"].astype(int)
base_df["observed_values"]   = check_results["observed_values"]
base_df["matched_tech_info"] = check_results["matched_tech_info"]
base_df["matched_cust_cols"] = check_results["matched_cust_cols"]

# =========================================================
# OUTPUT BUILD
# =========================================================
now_ts = datetime.now()

def build_exception_flag(flag):
    # Customer phone matching technician phone is SUSPICIOUS -> exception = yes
    return "yes" if flag == 1 else "no"


def build_expected_value():
    return "N/A"


def build_observed_value(flag, observed_values, matched_cust_cols):
    if flag == 1:
        return (f"Customer phone(s) {observed_values} matched with technician "
                f"records (fields involved: {matched_cust_cols})")
    return "No customer contact number matched with any technician record"


def build_additional_remarks(flag, matched_tech_info):
    if flag == 1:
        return (f"Potential conflict - customer contact appears in technician "
                f"database. Matched technician details: {matched_tech_info}")
    return "Clean - no overlap between customer contacts and technician phones"


output_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "check_id":                  CHECK_ID,
    "check_name":                CHECK_NAME,
    "created_at":                now_ts,
    "updated_at":                now_ts,
    "is_active":                 base_df.get("is_active"),
    "header_crm_id":             base_df["header_crm_id"],
    "sr_number":                 base_df.get("sr_number"),
    "attch_id":                  base_df.get("attch_id"),
    "category":                  base_df.get("category"),
    "calling_from_number":       base_df.get("calling_from_number"),
    "customer_contact":          base_df.get("customer_contact"),
    "customer_registered_phone": base_df.get("customer_registered_phone"),
    "customer_alternate_phone":  base_df.get("customer_alternate_phone"),
    "tech_phone_match":          base_df["tech_phone_match"],
    "observed_values":           base_df["observed_values"],
    "matched_tech_info":         base_df["matched_tech_info"],
    "matched_cust_cols":         base_df["matched_cust_cols"],
    "exception_flag":            base_df["tech_phone_match"].apply(build_exception_flag),
    "expected_value":            build_expected_value(),
    "reason": base_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_observed_value(
            r["tech_phone_match"],
            r["observed_values"],
            r["matched_cust_cols"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
    "additional_remarks": base_df.apply(
        lambda r: build_additional_remarks(
            r["tech_phone_match"],
            r["matched_tech_info"]
        ),
        axis=1
    ),
})

output_df = output_df.where(pd.notnull(output_df), None)

test = output_df[output_df['exception_flag'] == 'yes']


print("Flag checks completed.")
print(f"Total rows: {len(output_df)}")
print(f"Exception=yes (tech phone overlap): {(output_df['exception_flag']=='yes').sum()}")
print(f"Exception=no  (clean):              {(output_df['exception_flag']=='no').sum()}")

# =========================================================
# TABLE + INSERT
# =========================================================
WRITE_MODE = "upsert"

# create_sql = f"""
# CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {NEW_TABLE} (
#   id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
#   check_id INT,
#   check_name VARCHAR(255),
#   created_at DATETIME,
#   is_active TINYINT,
#   header_crm_id VARCHAR(255),
#   sr_number VARCHAR(255),
#   attch_id VARCHAR(255),
#   category VARCHAR(255),
#   calling_from_number TEXT,
#   customer_contact TEXT,
#   customer_registered_phone TEXT,
#   customer_alternate_phone TEXT,
#   tech_phone_match TINYINT,
#   matched_phones TEXT,
#   matched_tech_info TEXT,
#   matched_cust_cols VARCHAR(255),
#   exception_flag VARCHAR(10),
#   expected_value TEXT,
#   observed_value TEXT,
#   additional_remarks TEXT,
#   UNIQUE KEY uniq_check_row (check_id, header_crm_id, sr_number, attch_id)
# )
# """

# cursor.execute(create_sql)
# conn.commit()

insert_cols = [
    "check_id","check_name","created_at","updated_at","is_active",
    "header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","category",
    "calling_from_number","customer_contact",
    "customer_registered_phone","customer_alternate_phone",
    "tech_phone_match","observed_values","matched_tech_info","matched_cust_cols",
    "exception_flag","expected_value","reason","additional_remarks"
]

records = output_df[insert_cols].values.tolist()

placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(insert_cols))
col_list = ", ".join(insert_cols)

update_cols = [c for c in insert_cols if c not in ["check_id","header_crm_id","sr_number","attch_id","created_at"]]
update_sql = ", ".join([f"{c}=VALUES({c})" for c in update_cols])

insert_sql = f"""
INSERT INTO {NEW_TABLE} ({col_list})
VALUES ({placeholders})
ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE {update_sql}
"""

# =========================================================
# BATCH INSERT
# =========================================================
BATCH = 500

for i in range(0, len(records), BATCH):
    batch = records[i:i+BATCH]
    try:
        cursor.executemany(insert_sql, batch)
        conn.commit()
        print(f"Inserted {i} to {i+len(batch)}")
    except Exception as e:
        conn.rollback()
        print(f"Error: {e}")

cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("DONE: Data written to table p_table_1015")

        pass

      - remove ALL non-digit characters (spaces, +, -, (), etc.)

            (row.get("tech_id"), row.get("tech_name"))

    """
    customer_vals: dict {col_name: value}
    Returns:
      flag (0/1)         -> 1 if ANY cleaned customer phone exactly matches ANY cleaned tech phone
      matched_phones     -> "9876543210 (from customer_contact)"
      matched_tech_info  -> "Tech ID: T123 | Name: Ramesh | Phone: 9876543210"
      matched_cust_cols  -> "customer_contact"

    for col_name, val in customer_vals.items():
        cust_phones = clean_phone_set(val)
        if not cust_phones:
            continue

        exact_matches = cust_phones & tech_phone_set
        for p in exact_matches:
            for tid, tname in tech_phone_lookup.get(p, []):
                hits.append((p, col_name, tid, tname))

    if not hits:
        return 0, "", "", ""

    seen = set()

    for h in hits:

        if key not in seen:

            uniq.append(h)

    matched_phones    = "; ".join([f"{h[0]} (from {h[1]})" for h in uniq])
    matched_tech_info = "; ".join([f"Tech ID: {h[2]} | Name: {h[3]} | Phone: {h[0]}" for h in uniq])
    matched_cust_cols = ", ".join(sorted({h[1] for h in uniq}))

    return 1, matched_phones, matched_tech_info, matched_cust_cols

    # Customer phone matching technician phone is SUSPICIOUS → exception = yes
    return "yes" if flag == 1 else "no"


def build_expected_value():
    return ("Customer contact numbers (calling_from_number, customer_contact, "
            "customer_registered_phone, customer_alternate_phone) should NOT match "
            "any registered technician phone number")


def build_observed_value(flag, matched_phones, matched_cust_cols):
    if flag == 1:
        return (f"Customer phone(s) {matched_phones} matched with technician "
                f"records (fields involved: {matched_cust_cols})")
    return "No customer contact number matched with any technician record"

    if flag == 1:
        return (f"Potential conflict — customer contact appears in technician "
                f"database. Matched technician details: {matched_tech_info}")
    return "Clean — no overlap between customer contacts and technician phones"
